Cragslane Cavern

**Cragslane Cavern** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and [pit wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Pit_Wolf "Skyrim:Pit Wolf"). It contains only one zone, *[Cragslane Cavern](#Cragslane_Cavern)*.

The Bouncer

The cave is being used for [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") operations and animal blood sports.

## Related Quests

- **[Gambler's Edge](/wiki/Skyrim:Gambler%27s_Edge "Skyrim:Gambler's Edge")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Orcish_Scaled "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Orcish Scaled"): Search for an ill-fated gambler at the pit fights in Cragslane Cavern.
- **[Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand")**: Clear Cragslane Cavern for the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo").

- **[Rescue Mission](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_Mission "Skyrim:Rescue Mission")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to rescue a kidnapped citizen.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The cave is just off the road between [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") and [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). There is a single [Bouncer](/wiki/Skyrim:Bouncer "Skyrim:Bouncer") on guard outside the entrance, with two pit wolves in cages with leveled locks nearby. There is a campfire in front with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") hanging over it, and two small tents containing unowned bedrolls beside the fire separated by a food barrel and a couple sacks. East of the fire is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"). The entrance to the cavern is southwest of the campfire, with a crate and a couple food sacks beside it.

### Cragslane Cavern

The wolf pit and the two gamblers

The entrance leads into a tunnel descending to the south. The bottom is lit by a lantern on a barrel to the left, with a bandit standing guard opposite (see [bugs](#Bugs)). Beyond him, the tunnel narrows; a mead barrel is ahead where the tunnel turns to the west. After a few paces, the tunnel opens into a large cave, entering on a raised wooden structure with a ramp to the north leading down to the ground level. At ground level is a central pit containing two pit wolves, with one pit wolf standing over the corpse of another. There are two gamblers standing near the pit. There are chairs spaced around the pit for the patrons to sit and watch the fights, and a cart on the near side containing a couple [pickaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") and shovels. In the northwest corner is the bar, with a couple stools in front. One bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), one bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), four bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), and two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") are either on or under the counter, while two bottles of [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma"), a bowl of [moon sugar](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Sugar "Skyrim:Moon Sugar"), and a copy of the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Wolf Queen, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v1 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v1")* are under the counter. Behind the bar is an unarmed [gambler](/wiki/Skyrim:Gambler "Skyrim:Gambler") and an armed [barkeep](/wiki/Skyrim:Barkeep "Skyrim:Barkeep"). The Barkeep carries the [Craglane Chest Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Craglane_Chest_Key "Skyrim:Craglane Chest Key"), which opens an apprentice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") behind the bar. There are also a couple mead barrels in the corner, and to the east of the bar is an unowned single bed. To the south are two tunnels, one of which leads to and from the pit, while the other exits in front of it. Under the wooden structure near the chamber's entrance are several crates, barrels, and sacks.

The Butcher

The tunnel to the south leads to another chamber, where the leader of the bandits, the [Butcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Butcher "Skyrim:Butcher"), stands facing away from you. In this cave there is an unowned bedroll against the east wall, while against the rear wall is a small raised area with a wooden ramp going up. There are a couple food barrels and a basket containing [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") here, beside which is a small set of shelves holding four bottles of skooma, a [blue dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Dartwing "Skyrim:Blue Dartwing"), and an expert-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"). To the right of the shelves is a long wooden table holding a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), three more bottles of skooma, two samples of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungus, a bowl of moon sugar, a bottle of Nord mead, and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), with a bunch of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") hanging over the table. To the right of the table are more crates, sacks, and barrels, with a pickaxe and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on top.

In front of the wooden ramp is an apprentice-locked chest with a [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") in front of it. This chest is also opened with the Barkeep's key. Against the west wall are three cages, two of which are apprentice-locked and contain pit wolves, while the third is empty and open. The Butcher carries the [Craglane Dog Cage Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Craglane_Dog_Cage_Key "Skyrim:Craglane Dog Cage Key") that opens these cages. The second tunnel heading north-south leads into the pit, where there is the body of the dead wolf. Between the two tunnels are more barrels and sacks, with a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") on top and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") on the ground beside them.

## Notes

- Reading the [small note](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Note "Skyrim:Small Note"), which can be randomly found on a dead bandit surrounded by wolves, will mark this location on your map.
- Be warned that the Butcher puts up a good fight and usually has an enchanted weapon, as well as a leveled set of unenchanted heavy armor (excluding the helmet). This could be a very long fight, so come prepared.

## Bugs

- The first guard you meet inside Cragslane Cavern has no name, and cannot be pickpocketed or looted after he has been killed. This bug was introduced in [Patch 1.9](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch#Version_1.9 "Skyrim:Patch").
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.1130.0, fixes this bug.
- 4 of the caged and hostile Pit Wolves here can be seen out of their cages before you enter and are not hostile.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, addresses this issue. A copy of the wolf actor being used has been made, and replaces the 4 references with it. The copy has an AI pack to hold the wolves in place until the cage doors are open. The script for the cage doors also has been updated so the wolves will now be hostile once they're free.

## Maps

  Cragslane Cavern

Cragwallow Slope

**Cragwallow Slope** is a medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") home to [conjurers](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer") and [atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach").

Conjurer and atronach

## Related Quests

- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

There is a leveled [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer") guarding the entrance; however, they seem to attack anything on sight, including passive animals. In front of the entrance is a small platform made of wooden planks holding candles and a table, making it an easy location to spot. The magical implements lying about are a sign of the occupants inside. On the table are a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Magicka"), a random [potion of extra magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka"), a random empty [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and a copy of *[The Firmament](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Firmament "Skyrim:The Firmament").*

### Cragwallow Slope

Cragwallow Slope is more or less a narrow earthen cave that goes in a circle. Conjurers are found throughout the loop; due to their close proximity, they will quickly join battle once someone starts casting. The narrow corridors and swarming nature of conjurers and their summons can make for some very tight fights. Running out to break the daisy chain of creatures may be necessary, as trying to fight through [atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach") while casters safely cast on you can quickly become fatal. A high level of [sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") and good ranged attacks can simplify this enormously. The conjurers are leveled, and at very low levels they may only be able to summon [familiars](/wiki/Skyrim:Familiar "Skyrim:Familiar"). They are supported by leveled atronachs.

The entrance leads into a wide tunnel heading east to a T-junction. To the north is a ledge above that can't be reached from here, but will serve as a shortcut to the exit later. To the south the tunnel continues, with three patches of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungus along the tunnel. At the end, it turns east and enters a room containing a leveled conjurer, quite a bit of vegetation, and a square table at the rear with an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") built in, a random empty soul gem on top, and a random potion of magicka and an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") beside it. There is quite a bit of natural light coming in from holes in the ceiling, and two patches of [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") fungus in a darker area. A narrow tunnel climbs to the east in the northeastern corner of the room.

The tunnel is fairly short, and opens into a larger cavern also full of vegetation and holes in the ceiling, with a leveled conjurer just ahead and an atronach patrolling the cavern. Any fighting will alert several more conjurers that are in caves ahead. The cavern curves to the left and exits into a tunnel heading north. The tunnel descends and at the end turns to the east, then continues to descend to a cave that is partially flooded below you with a ledge running around the walls and wicker fencing along the edge to prevent falls. There is a leveled conjurer at the bottom standing in the water, and an atronach patrolling the path nearest you. There is a ramp down to the right leading to the flooded area, and a path all the way around the edge to reach a tunnel heading south. In the flooded area, there is little of interest apart from a random empty soul gem.

Descending path

Turning left and following the path around to the far side, there is a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") on the left and a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") among a pile of firewood. Beyond this is a set of shelves holding a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), two pieces of [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root") in one bowl and two [torchbug thoraxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug_Thorax "Skyrim:Torchbug Thorax") in another, with a basket on the floor beside it containing two fillets of [horker meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat"). At the end, the tunnel heads south, before immediately turning to the west. After a few paces there is a tunnel on the left into a small bedroom containing two unowned single beds, a dresser, an end table, and an unlocked chest. On the dresser is a set of [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), a random potion of magicka, and copies of two common books. On the end table is a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal") and a piece of canis root.

Past this room, the tunnel descends again before opening into a large cavern with part of a fort in front and an atronach standing in a hole in the wall. There is also a high-leveled conjurer behind the atronach, but you may be unable to see them. There are stairs up to the north and south, as well as several parts of the floor of the cavern that can't be seen from the entrance to the cavern.

At the alchemy lab

To the north, up the stairs is a ledge with two unowned single beds, one of which may be occupied by a conjurer. Beyond them is a round wooden table with a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), a sample of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), and three common books on top, and a bookcase to the left holding nine more common books and a bowl containing three [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flowers. Past the bookcase is a barrel containing foodstuffs. Climbing the stairs to the south brings you to the top of a wall with an area behind where a conjurer is normally found working at an alchemy lab, with a table and two chairs to the left. On the table is a random [potion of the warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_the_Warrior "Skyrim:Potion of the Warrior"), a random [potion of true shot](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_True_Shot "Skyrim:Potion of True Shot"), and an apothecary's satchel.

To the right of the lab are two racks hanging from the ceiling over a food barrel, holding three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid, and a bunch of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"). There is a campfire with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") hanging over it against the south wall. To the right of the fire is a bookcase holding nine common books and a quiver of random [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows"). Along the wall to the west are two archery targets on stands, with a round wooden table to the left holding a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow"), a quiver of random arrows, a bowl of [horker stew](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Stew "Skyrim:Horker Stew"), a random potion of healing, and a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina"); a second long bow is on the ground. Along the wall and the edge of the raised area are several wooden benches.

It is important to take out the conjurers on the ledges to make the final battle much more manageable; otherwise, you can be overwhelmed if trying to face all of the enemies at the same time. The central area will contain a higher level conjurer, a summoned creature, and a lesser conjurer. It's imperative to take out the weaker creatures and conjurers while avoiding the boss conjurer at first. The boss will keep summoning an atronach, casting cold spells, and using a very effective heal. Taking him down requires finesse or a lot of potions. If you don't have enough damage output, he can easily out-heal your attacks. Upon killing him, the summoned atronach should disappear, leaving you free to loot the room.

Conjurer

At the southern end of the ground level is an unlocked chest, and against the wall to the east are three empty coffins. There are a few patches of fungus on the ground in the cavern, including two [Namira's Rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"), one white cap, and two [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"). At the northern end of the cavern is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") on the ground. Through the hole in the side of the excavated fort where the atronach and conjurer were standing is a well-lit area with many lit candles on the floor, three empty coffins on your left as you enter, and an unlocked boss chest farther to the south by a second hole in the wall. On your right as you enter this area is a table, a small cage, two bookcases holding twelve common books and a random filled soul gem, and a wardrobe all against the north wall, with food sacks and a barrel between them. In front of these is a long wooden table with three common books, a random potion of healing, a random potion of magicka, a leveled filled soul gem, and a copy of the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Lunar Lorkhan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lunar_Lorkhan "Skyrim:The Lunar Lorkhan")*. A coin purse and an iron sword are located between an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") and a mammoth skull behind a pile of pillars.

The path continues to the north at the rear of the fort area. At the top is a T-junction with a conjurer sitting to the right in a dead end with a couple tables and chairs. At the rear are an adept-locked chest and a bookcase holding an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and eight common books. To the left, the path climbs and leads around to the ledge near the entrance.

## Bugs

- Some of the items are marked as owned by the MarkarthHagsCureFaction, requiring you to steal them unless you help [Bothela](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela "Skyrim:Bothela").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.

## Maps

- 

  Cragwallow Slope

# Skyrim:Creature of Legend

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), checked by [Riliane](/wiki/User:Riliane "User:Riliane") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Track down and tame the last living [Unicorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Unicorn "Skyrim:Unicorn").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Automatically added after purchasing the [Wild Horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Wild Horses") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") |
| Location(s): | [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"), [Lost Prospect Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Prospect_Mine "Skyrim:Lost Prospect Mine") exterior |
| Reward: | [Unicorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Unicorn "Skyrim:Unicorn") mount |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE034\_UnicornQuest |
| Added by: | [Wild Horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Wild Horses") |

The Psijics have restored a single Unicorn to the world

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Go to [the Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum") and read [*Soran's Journal*](/wiki/Skyrim:Soran%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Soran's Journal").
2. Locate and [tame](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Tamable_HorsesCC "Skyrim:Horses") the [Unicorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Unicorn "Skyrim:Unicorn") just west of [Lost Prospect Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Prospect_Mine "Skyrim:Lost Prospect Mine").

### First Named, Last Tamed

Upon installing the [Wild Horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Wild Horses") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"), you will be directed to [the Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum") in the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") to learn more about reports of a recent [Unicorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Unicorn "Skyrim:Unicorn") sighting. Once there, you will find [*Soran's Journal*](/wiki/Skyrim:Soran%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Soran's Journal") sitting on [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub")'s desk. It details the research on Unicorns carried out by a wildlife scholar named Soran Hariksen, who sighted a Unicorn in the forests of [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"). The creature is supposedly from the distant past and was brought forward in time by the [Psijic Order](/wiki/Skyrim:Psijic_Order "Skyrim:Psijic Order") after the [last living Unicorn](/wiki/Oblivion:Unicorn "Oblivion:Unicorn") was sacrificed to [Hircine](/wiki/Lore:Hircine "Lore:Hircine") during his [quest](/wiki/Oblivion:Hircine "Oblivion:Hircine") in [*Oblivion*](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion").

Once you have read the journal, you will be directed to an area just west of the entrance to [Lost Prospect Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Prospect_Mine "Skyrim:Lost Prospect Mine"). The Unicorn can be found right next to the nearby pond. It is a [wild horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horse "Skyrim:Wild Horse") and will run away from you if approached. It must be [tamed](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Tamable_HorsesCC "Skyrim:Horses"), which is a mechanic added by the Creation. You must mount the Unicorn until it stops bucking in order to claim it as your own. You may be thrown off when it bucks, which will necessitate chasing it down again once you get back on your feet.

### Reward

Once tamed, the Unicorn will become your mount. If you decide to switch to a different mount, it will make its way to the College of Winterhold courtyard and wait for you there.

## Notes

- Like other horses, the Unicorn can be [named](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Horse_NamingCC "Skyrim:Horses") and [saddled](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#SaddlesCC "Skyrim:Horses"), which are two other mechanics added by this Creation. To do this, you must visit a [stable](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables") with the Unicorn as your active mount.

## Quest Stages

| Creature of Legend (ccBGSSSE034\_UnicornQuest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 0 |  | A wildlife scholar is rumored to have tracked down a legendary Unicorn. The last of these creatures was supposed to have been slain long ago. I should investigate and see what I can find. *Objective 0:* Find information about the Unicorn |
| 10 |  | I found the journal of wildlife scholar Soran Hariksen at the College of Winterhold, which contained details on the whereabouts of the Unicorn. I should locate it to see if I can tame it, and take care of it as my own. *Objective 10:* Find and tame the Unicorn |
| 20 | ☑ | A wildlife scholar was able to track down and verify the existence of a Unicorn. Using information that I found in his journal, I located the Unicorn, tamed it, and claimed it as my own. If I need to find it again, it will be at the College of Winterhold courtyard. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE034_UnicornQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE034_UnicornQuest`.

# Skyrim:Creatures

## Overview

This page provides a list of all **creature** types in *[Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")*.

:   **[Animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals")** – Animals comprise various mundane creatures that have no magical or weapon-wielding abilities.

    :   :   [Ash Hopper](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Hopper "Skyrim:Ash Hopper")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") • [Bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear") • [Bristleback](/wiki/Skyrim:Bristleback "Skyrim:Bristleback")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") • [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") • [Cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow") • [Deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer "Skyrim:Deer") • [Dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog") • [Fox](/wiki/Skyrim:Fox "Skyrim:Fox") • [Goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") • [Horker](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker "Skyrim:Horker") • [Horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses") • [Mammoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth") • [Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab") • [Nix-Hound](/wiki/Skyrim:Nix-Hound_(creature) "Skyrim:Nix-Hound (creature)")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Nix-Hound "Skyrim:Nix-Hound") • [Rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit "Skyrim:Rabbit") • [Sabre Cat](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Sabre Cat") • [Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") • [Slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Slaughterfish") • [Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf")

:   **[Ash Creatures](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Creatures "Skyrim:Ash Creatures")** – Horrific monsters associated with [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain"). Note that [Ash Zombies](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Zombie "Skyrim:Ash Zombie")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal") are considered [NPCs](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs"), not creatures.

    :   :   [Ash Guardian](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Guardian "Skyrim:Ash Guardian")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") • [Ash Spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")

:   **[Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra")** – Daedra are creatures from the planes of Oblivion. Note that [Golden Saints](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Saint "Skyrim:Golden Saint")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers"), [Dark Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Seducer "Skyrim:Dark Seducer")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers") and [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora "Skyrim:Dremora") are [NPCs](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs"), not creatures, and therefore are not listed here.

    :   :   [Flame Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Flame Atronach") • [Frost Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Frost Atronach") • [Lurker](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") • [Seeker](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") • [Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Storm Atronach")

:   **[Dwarven Automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons")** – Dwarven Automatons are ancient, robot-like machines encountered in [Dwarven Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins").

    :   :   [Dwarven Ballista](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ballista "Skyrim:Dwarven Ballista")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") • [Dwarven Centurion](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion") • [Dwarven Sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere") • [Dwarven Spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider")

:   **[Monsters](/wiki/Skyrim:Monsters "Skyrim:Monsters")** – Monsters are creatures with various magical abilities, ranging from magical attacks to various magical resistances.

    :   :   [Burnt Spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Burnt_Spriggan "Skyrim:Burnt Spriggan")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") • [Chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") • [Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") • [Elytra Nymph](/wiki/Skyrim:Elytra_Nymph "Skyrim:Elytra Nymph")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers") • [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") • [Fire Wyrm](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Wyrm "Skyrim:Fire Wyrm")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") • [Frost Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Giant "Skyrim:Frost Giant")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") • [Frostbite Spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") • [Gargoyle](/wiki/Skyrim:Gargoyle "Skyrim:Gargoyle")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") • [Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") • [Goblin](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblin "Skyrim:Goblin")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblins "Skyrim:Goblins") • [Hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") • [Ice Wraith](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith") • [Magic Anomaly](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Anomaly "Skyrim:Magic Anomaly") • [Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch "Skyrim:Netch")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") • [Riekling](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") • [Spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiders "Skyrim:Spiders")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") • [Spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") • [Troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll") • [Werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf") • [Wisp](/wiki/Skyrim:Wisp "Skyrim:Wisp")

:   **[Passive Creatures](/wiki/Skyrim:Passive_Creatures "Skyrim:Passive Creatures")** – Passive creatures are completely unable to attack or harm you.

    :   :   [Aquatic Creatures](/wiki/Skyrim:Passive_Creatures#Aquatic_Creatures "Skyrim:Passive Creatures") • [Food](/wiki/Skyrim:Passive_Creatures#Food "Skyrim:Passive Creatures") • [Insects](/wiki/Skyrim:Passive_Creatures#Insects "Skyrim:Passive Creatures") • [Other Creatures](/wiki/Skyrim:Passive_Creatures#Other_Creatures "Skyrim:Passive Creatures")

:   **[Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead "Skyrim:Undead")** – Undead creatures consist of spirits, reanimated skeletons, and reanimated corpses. [Vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") are also considered undead, but are undead NPCs instead of creatures.

    :   :   [Ayleid Lich](/wiki/Skyrim:Ayleid_Lich "Skyrim:Ayleid Lich")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause") • [Bone Colossus](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Colossus "Skyrim:Bone Colossus")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromantic_Grimoire "Skyrim:Necromantic Grimoire") • [Bone Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Wolf_(creature) "Skyrim:Bone Wolf (creature)")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Wolf "Skyrim:Bone Wolf") • [Death Hound](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Hound "Skyrim:Death Hound")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") • [Dragon Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") • [Draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") • [Ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost "Skyrim:Ghost") • [Skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") • [Wight](/wiki/Skyrim:Wight "Skyrim:Wight")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause") • [Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Zombie "Skyrim:Zombie")

Crescius Caerellius

**Crescius Caerellius** is an [elderly](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder "Skyrim:Elder") [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [miner](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner_(class) "Skyrim:Miner (class)") living in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"). He is almost eighty years old, and has spent many years on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") looking for a new source of [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony"). A decade ago, he underwent a period of depression at his failure to find anything, and this led to him meeting [Aphia Velothi](/wiki/Skyrim:Aphia_Velothi "Skyrim:Aphia Velothi"), his current wife. He's now convinced that his great-grandfather [Gratian Caerellius](/wiki/Skyrim:Gratian_Caerellius "Skyrim:Gratian Caerellius") was killed by something in the [local mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine") other than a tunnel collapse, as the East Empire Company claims. During the quest [The Final Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent"), you will have to prove old Crescius right, a task that will put Raven Rock back on the map.

If attacked, he will defend himself with a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"). He wears farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000261bd "Skyrim:Boots"). He carries, among [other things](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Caerellius_House_Key "Skyrim:Caerellius House Key") to [his house](/wiki/Skyrim:Caerellius_House "Skyrim:Caerellius House").

Unlike many other citizens, Crescius avoided the spell of [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)") and will never be seen working on the [Earth Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Earth_Stone "Skyrim:Earth Stone"). Instead, he sleeps inside his [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Caerellius_House "Skyrim:Caerellius House") every night between 11pm and 7am. He skips breakfast (see [bugs](#Bugs)) and then spends the entire day in the house, cooking, relaxing, or talking to Aphia. Once you reopen the mine, Crescius will no longer stay at home all day long, but will instead be promoted to foreman of the ebony mine and will spend the majority of the day in the office inside the mine.

## Related Quests

- **[Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_(quest) "Skyrim:Dragonborn (quest)")**: Travel to the island of [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") to find out what's happening there.
- **[An Axe to Find](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Axe_to_Find "Skyrim:An Axe to Find")**: Retrieve an [ancient Nordic pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nordic_Pickaxe "Skyrim:Ancient Nordic Pickaxe") for [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory").
- **[The Final Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent")**: Find out what happened to the [great-grandfather](/wiki/Skyrim:Gratian_Caerellius "Skyrim:Gratian Caerellius") of Crescius Caerellius.
- **[It's All In The Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:It%27s_All_In_The_Taste "Skyrim:It's All In The Taste")**: Distribute [Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri")'s [Sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Sujamma "Skyrim:Sadri's Sujamma") to the citizens of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
- **[Her Word Against Theirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Her_Word_Against_Theirs "Skyrim:Her Word Against Theirs")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Spread the word of the Goddess [Almalexia](/wiki/Lore:Almalexia "Lore:Almalexia").

## Dialogue

His greetings can be:

:   *"If it wasn't for my wife, Aphia, I'd have joined my ancestors long ago."*
:   *"For all I know, I might be the last Imperial left on Solstheim."*
:   *"Maybe I won't live as long as the dark elves, but at least I didn't abandon my home."*

When approached before The Final Descent is finished:

:   *"There was a time when this town meant something. Now it's all gone."*

When spoken to:

:   **Are there any other Imperials in Raven Rock?**
:   *"Those cowards left decades ago. Every single damned one of them. The moment the ebony mine dried up, they pulled up stakes. Ridiculous!"*
:   **Ridiculous? Why?**
:   *"Solsthiem*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *is still rich in ebony ore. I know there's more down there... I can smell it. I come from three generations of miners, and I'm telling you that the East Empire Company was wrong. They just didn't want to spend the coin trying to find it."*

:   **Tell me about your family.**
:   *"Our home has stood in Raven Rock since the colony was founded. Gratian helped build it with his own two hands. After Gratian died, he left behind a wife and a son... my grandfather, Rellicus. Rellicus lived there for quite a long time, working in the other sections of the mine until he was slain by reavers."*
:   **And your parents?**
:   *"I never knew my father... my mother and I always lived alone. I asked her about him many times, but she seemed angry and refused to speak about him, so eventually I let it go. When I was old enough, I began working in the mine hoping to make my fortune and eventually move to the Imperial City."*
:   **Then it dried up.**
:   *"Unfortunately, yes. I only had enough coin saved to send one of us back to the Imperial City, so I sent my mother alone. I wanted her to see her homeland before she died."*
:   **And you've been alone ever since?**
:   *"Until I met my darling Aphia, yes. I suppose you could have called me a bitter old hermit... now I'm just old."*

Once the mine is open again:

:   *"I can't believe you found a way to reopen the mines. I don't know how to thank you."*
:   **How are things now that the mines are open again?**
:   *"I've been made the foreman of the mine thanks to everything you did down there. It's good to get the old nose working again. I missed sniffing out the ebony deposits and getting my hands dirty. Best of all, Aphia isn't so cross when I go down there any more!"*
:   **Can I dig for ebony in Raven Rock Mine?**
:   *"Of course! In fact, Councilor Morvayn has given you the full run of the place. Help yourself to whatever you like. We're all in agreement that you're entitled to as much as you can carry."*

He will also change his response on how his predecessors are ridiculous:

:   *"Well you know it as well as I do. Raven Rock Mine wasn't empty at all... it's still rich in ebony ore. I came from three generations of miners, and I couldn't get anyone to believe me. Well we showed them, didn't we!"*

### The Final Descent

Crescius in Raven Rock Mine

You will initially find him inside [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine"), in the very first chamber, busy discussing with his wife:

**Crescius**: *"Damn it, woman! I said to leave me be!"*
**Aphia**: *"Crescius, last time you explored the mine you almost fell to your death. I'm not spending the rest of my days as a widow!"*
**Crescius**: *"And I'm telling you that I'll do whatever it takes to find my great-grandfather's remains. He's down here, I can feel it."*
**Aphia**: *"That was almost two centuries ago. There may be nothing left to find."*
**Crescius**: *"Just let me go, woman!"*
**Aphia**: *"Crescius, you're an obstinate old fool and you're going to get yourself killed."*

If you speak to Crescius after this conversation:

:   *"Who in the blazes are you?! Can't you see I'm busy?"*
:   **Busy doing what?**
:   *"Why should I tell you? I don't even know who you are."*

If you leave conversation, he will say:

:   *"Sure, ignore the ravings of a 'crazy old man.' I get it."*
:   *"At least hear me out before you walk away."*

You will then have three options:

:   **Perhaps I could help.**
:   *"Hmph, maybe. Been difficult trusting people lately, they think I'm crazy."*

:   **I'm just exploring.**

    :   *"Exploring, huh? Most folks think this place isn't worth the effort."*

:   **It's dangerous here for an old man.**

    :   *"Ask most of the folks around here and they'd agree with you."*

All three options will lead to:

:   *"But mark my words, these mines hold a secret that could put Raven Rock back on the map."*
:   **What sort of secret would be hidden here?**
:   *"A secret the East Empire Company swept under the rug two centuries ago. It killed my great-grandfather, and left Raven Rock with a worthless and tainted mine."*
:   **East Empire Company?**
:   *"You never heard of them? They're the largest trading company in Tamriel, originally chartered by the Emperor of Cyrodiil himself."*
:   **Who was your great-grandfather?**
:   *"Gratian Caerellius. He spent his entire life exploring ancient ruins across Tamriel and he died in these very mines almost 200 years ago."*
:   **How did he die?**
:   *"East Empire Company called it 'a terrible accident,' claiming that he was lost in a rockfall, but I know better."*
:   **What's your proof?**
:   *"My wife and I were cleaning out our home, and we came across some of my great-grandfather's things locked in an old chest. I found an unsent letter he'd written to the East Empire Company, and a key."*
:   **What did the letter say?**
:   *"It describes a discovery that was made in the mine by some of the diggers. They wanted Gratian to take a closer look. The East Empire Company must have felt it was of great value, as they locked that section of the mine off from everyone else."*
:   **The key is to the locked section?**
:   *"It is. Well, I assume it is. I haven't been able to find the entrance."*

:   **This is hardly proof of anything.**

    :   *"Now you're starting to sound like everyone else."*

:   **I admit, this does sound suspicious.**

    :   *"Finally! Someone who believes me."*

:   **I still think you're crazy.**

    :   *"Sigh. I don't care what you, or anyone else thinks about me."*

All three options lead to:

:   *"I'm telling you... there's something big down there, something that the East Empire Company wanted to hide from everyone."*
:   **Why are you telling me all of this?**
:   *"Look, my wife nags that I'm too old to go traipsing around these mines chasing my story. Time's my enemy... it's caught up with me before I could find the answers that I'm looking for."*
:   **So you do need my help.**
:   *"I do. I want to know what happened to Gratian, and what the East Empire Company is keeping from all of us."*
:   **Any idea where to start?**
:   *"Gratian kept a journal of notes about his discoveries. If you can find his... remains, I'm hoping it will help. Here's everything I have. The letter, the key. Please, do this for me so I can finally regain the respect that I've lost."*
:   **Are you sure Gratian's death wasn't an accident?**
:   *"Look, I know I don't have much to go on. I have that unsent letter, and that's really it. But I also have a miner's instinct that's run in my family from before Gratian was even born. I may sound like a crazy old man to you, but I'm telling you, the tunnels here are solid... they would never collapse like that."*
:   **Why were you arguing with Aphia?**
:   *"She thinks that old age has addled my mind... that I'm seeing things when there's nothing to be seen. I realize she cares about me, but she has to understand that I can't rest until I find out what happened to Gratian."*
:   **What if she's right and I don't find anything?**
:   *"Then I'll settle down peacefully and never set foot in this mine again. I've been waiting for this moment for a long time... even before I discovered Gratian's old things. I just hope both of you don't mistake my enthusiasm for insanity."*

Once you leave conversation:

:   *"Be careful down there, the mine can be treacherous."*

Once you return with the [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Gratian%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Gratian's Journal") of his deceased great-grandfather:

:   *"You're back! Please, tell me what you found."*
:   **You were right all along. (Give journal)**
:   *"Let me see that! Ha, I knew it! Gratian's death wasn't because of a rockfall, it was just a story to keep people away from the tombs. Now that I have his journal in hand, I can get some closure from the East Empire Company. Make them pay for lying to everyone."*
:   **Good luck with that.**
:   *"Thank you. Now, I believe I owe you a little more than a debt of gratitude for all that work you did. Here... it's not much, but it's the best an old, retired miner can do."*

He will then hand you a leveled amount of gold and the quest will finish. Soon afterward, [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine") will be reopened, making Raven Rock a prosperous town once again, with numerous citizens now employed.

### Dragonborn

:   **Do you know someone called Miraak?**
:   *"I recognize the name, but... I don't know how I know it. It sounds so familiar."*
:   **Tell me anything you can.**
:   *"It's so strange. I feel like it's from a dream. Something about the Earth Stone, and a shrine... That's it. That's all I can think of."*

### An Axe to Find

Speaking to Crescius after accepting the quest from Glover:

:   **Glover wants his Ancient Nordic Pickaxe back.**
:   *"The damn fool doesn't even deserve to have it! The pickaxe was made for mining, not selling. I'll bet he stole it from the Skaal in the first place."*

Three options are available, two of which will make both Crescius and Glover respond differently:

:   **It doesn't belong to you.**

    :   *"Oh, very well. Here. Tell him I hope he drops the thing on his foot."*

:   **Fine, you keep it.**

    :   *"Now you're finally talking some sense. A mining tool belongs in a mining family. Just tell him I lost it or something."*

:   **Let me think about this.**

    :   *"Good. Now let me get back to what I was doing."*

### It's All In The Taste

During the quest [It's All In The Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:It%27s_All_In_The_Taste "Skyrim:It's All In The Taste"), Crescius will taste some of [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri")'s [sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Sujamma "Skyrim:Sadri's Sujamma"):

:   **Geldis Sadri wants you to try his new drink.**
:   *"Hmph, he's begging for patrons again, eh? Well, I suppose I could have just a bit."*

## Conversations

*"They thought I was a crazy old fool. But I proved them wrong."*

**Crescius**: *"You're too good to me, Aphia. I only wish I could remain with you longer."*
**Aphia**: *"It doesn't matter, my husband. Let's simply cherish the time we have for now."*
**Crescius**: *"And what will you do when I'm gone?"*
**Aphia**: *"Then I'll simply have to fall in love with some other senile, grousing old fool."*

**Crescius**: *"They've laughed at me, Aphia. They thought I was a crazy old fool. But I proved them wrong."*
**Aphia**: *"People laugh at things they don't believe. It helps them accept the unknown."*
**Crescius**: *"You're too kind to people, always giving them the benefit of the doubt. Don't know how you put up with it."*
**Aphia**: *"Well, I put up with you, don't I?"*

## Bugs

- All of the beds in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") are incorrectly owned by Crescius, making sleeping impossible for the residents there.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.5, fixes this bug.
- Crescius was supposed to wake up at 6am for a one-hour breakfast, but his sleeping package lasts until 7am and always takes precedence.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.2, fixes this bug.
- During [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward"), [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory") is supposed to be able to provide a lead for who could be Steward for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth"), but his dialogue was mistakenly assigned to Crescius.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Criminal

## Overview

A version of the criminal

The **Criminal** is a rogue [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") who has [escaped jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Escaped_Criminal "Skyrim:Escaped Criminal"), and can be found in any of the nine [holds](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds"). Your job is to kill them, but they can be difficult to track down as they constantly travel back and forth. Their appearance is random and their equipment and stats are leveled ([any from this list](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit#Light_Armor "Skyrim:Bandit")).

## Related Quests

- **[Escaped Criminal](/wiki/Skyrim:Escaped_Criminal "Skyrim:Escaped Criminal")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to hunt down an escaped criminal. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

# Skyrim:Cronvangr Cave

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Cronvangr Cave ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cronvangr+Cave)) | | |
| # of Zones | 2 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |

Cronvangr Cave

**Cronvangr Cave** is a medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") and [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). It contains two zones: *[Cronvangr Cave](#Cronvangr_Cave)* and *[Cronvangr Broodlair](#Cronvangr_Broodlair)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(B) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (B)")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear out a beast den. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Recruit [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran")'s old allies for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Caught in a Web](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_in_a_Web "Skyrim:Caught in a Web")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Contest "Skyrim:The Contest"): Search for legendary artifacts in a spider den.
- **[Pets of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim_(quest) "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim"): Find trained pets around Skyrim.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The cave entrance is in the northwestern area of the sulfur pools characteristic of central [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"), almost due east of [Mixwater Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixwater_Mill "Skyrim:Mixwater Mill"). The exterior hints at what can be found inside: it is covered in webs, and one [egg sac](/wiki/Skyrim:Egg_Sac "Skyrim:Egg Sac") is in front of the entrance. A dead [mammoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth") is to the left. There are also several plants that can be harvested for ingredients in the surrounding area.

### Cronvangr Cave

The first chamber in the cave

Secret vampire area

The first room contains six frostbite spiders, an egg sac, and an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"). A small button on the northwest wall will open a rock door to a cavern, which contains a wooden building and several vampires on a raised area at the back of the cavern. Beware a [flame spout trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap") in the passage on the way to the vampires. The vampires are generally all found sleeping in the building; however, some of them may be awake, so be careful if you don't see them. On the lower level, there's a circle of candles around a dead body and two long tables with benches, one of which holds a single loose [coin](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). Two ramps up to the raised area and building are against the cave wall.

The inside of the building is a mess, strewn with viscera and gore. There are three single beds (normally all occupied by three sleeping vampires), a central table with a random filled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") and a copy of the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Locked Room](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Locked_Room "Skyrim:The Locked Room")* on top, a second table with an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe") and a [strong box](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") on top, several chairs, barrels, and sacks, and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") with a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison") next to it at the foot of one of the beds. There are several corpses nearby and in the cavern itself, which the vampires may raise to help them fight. Six poisons and a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") are on two sets of shelves, among [ruined books](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book") and other clutter. One more random potion can be found next to the barrels to the left of the shelves, on one of which is an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Apothecary.27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Containers"). A second chest, this one adept-locked, can be found behind the building near an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") and [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters"). A [sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_(item) "Skyrim:Sapphire (item)") can be found on top of a barrel next to the second chest. There is also a long wooden table and bench behind the building with two loose coins on it.

The rest of the zone can be reached from another tunnel in the first room. It consists of a sparsely lit cobwebbed pathway winding down into a cavern with a pool of water at the bottom, with two egg sacs and a [mammoth tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Parts#Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Animal Parts") along the path. There are several small frostbite spiders along the path, and it is possible for one or more of the spiders to fall off the ledges and into the water below. The spiders will often become trapped in the water, as the pathway out is fairly narrow and the spiders don't navigate it properly. This makes killing any spiders that fall much more difficult without the use of archery or long-range spells. An unlocked chest and a floating skeleton can be found in the water. A small pathway to the east leads to the second zone, *Cronvangr Broodlair*.

### Cronvangr Broodlair

Broodlair with a giant frostbite spider

The zone begins on a twisting path with several webs you need to break through and several small frostbite spiders along it. A small chest can be found in front of you where the tunnel turns to the right; it is hidden by two layers of spider webbing behind an unlootable desiccated corpse, and can be easily overlooked. The path continues to the broodlair proper, where a giant frostbite spider will drop from the ceiling to join many other, smaller spiders. A boss-level chest can be found in the back of this room, with a large egg sac to the right and a [moonstone ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein") to the left.

There's a shortcut back to the first zone up the slope to the north, with an egg sac on your left shortly before you re-enter the first zone. The shortcut will place you on a ledge above the passageway just before the first room of *Cronvangr Cave*.

## Notes

- Two ore veins are outside near the cave entrance. A [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") is 60 feet west-southwest of the entrance, straight ahead when exiting the cave [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=117664&y=-5824&zoom=16&legacy=true). A [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") is 150 feet northeast of the entrance, on the ridge near the trees [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=121792&y=-2768&zoom=16&legacy=true).
- A pair of leveled [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") have taken to practicing their craft on a large stone altar due east of the cave entrance. On the altar is a leveled poison, a potion, and a leveled soul gem. Scattered about the pools of hot water surrounding the altar are a few lootable [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") corpses, a pair of [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"), and the partial skeleton of a novice [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer"). A chest can also be found in the hot water east of the cave entrance, in the same general area as the altar.
- Internally, the location is referred to as **Cronvangr Hall**, presumably a name remaining from earlier in the game's development. This name also appears in the location data, causing it to display on the local map. The cave was once intended to house a unique faction of vampires, the Cronvangr Clan, under the leadership of Vlkoslak. You would have awoken here at some point at the start of a set of [unused vampire-related quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests").

# Skyrim:Crowstooth's Camp

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Camp.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Camp.png) | Camp: Crowstooth's Camp ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Crowstooth%27s+Camp)) | | |

| Southwest of [Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower"), and west of the [Ruins of Rkund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Rkund "Skyrim:Ruins of Rkund"). | |

Crowstooth's Camp

**Crowstooth's Camp** is a small [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") encampment southwest of [Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower"), and west of the [Ruins of Rkund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Rkund "Skyrim:Ruins of Rkund").

It is a bare bones affair. Tents have been set up, but the grass has not been cleared; there is no storage, crafting station, resting place, or furniture. It is occupied by [Crowstooth's](/wiki/Skyrim:Crowstooth "Skyrim:Crowstooth") forces, who were separated from her prior to the events of [Bones for a Crow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bones_for_a_Crow "Skyrim:Bones for a Crow").

## Residents

| Resident(s) |
| --- |
| [Linelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Linelle "Skyrim:Linelle") the [Hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") |

## Related Quests

- **[Bones for a Crow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bones_for_a_Crow "Skyrim:Bones for a Crow")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dragon_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dragon Plate"): Hunt down the Forsworn Crowstooth.

## Walkthrough

The camp is most easily reached by traveling by way of [Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower") from the ground. The exit of the tower opens out onto the same continuous mountainside area as both the camp and the [Ruins of Rkund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Rkund "Skyrim:Ruins of Rkund"). From here, there is a path to left leading to Rkund and to the right ending at the camp.

On the southeast side of the camp is a fallen tree. Next to the tree is a copy of the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") skill book *[Proper Lock Design and Construction](/wiki/Skyrim:Proper_Lock_Design "Skyrim:Proper Lock Design")*.

Once these forces are defeated, Crowstooth's second-in-command, [Linelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Linelle "Skyrim:Linelle"), must be looted for [her note](/wiki/Skyrim:Linelle%27s_Note "Skyrim:Linelle's Note"), which has information on where Crowstooth has gone.

## Notes

- The enemies here, including Linelle the Hagraven, will respawn after the quest is completed. Linelle's note does not respawn.
- The lockpicking skill book, *Proper Lock Design and Construction*, is the same one as mentioned at [Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower"). The camp makes it easier to locate, but won't be present until you start the related quest.

Crowstooth

**Crowstooth** is a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") who is encountered during the quest [Bones for a Crow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bones_for_a_Crow "Skyrim:Bones for a Crow").

Crowstooth wears a set of [Forsworn Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Armor "Skyrim:Forsworn Armor"). She has a [Forsworn Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Bow "Skyrim:Forsworn Bow"), a unique [Forsworn Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Sword "Skyrim:Forsworn Sword") and the unique Forsworn axe [Tyrant's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Tyrant%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Tyrant's Bane"), and carries a number of [Forsworn Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Arrow "Skyrim:Forsworn Arrow"), in addition to a random selection of loot. She is accompanied by [Alvasorr the Rat](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvasorr_the_Rat "Skyrim:Alvasorr the Rat"), who will back her up in the final fight of the quest.

She and Alvasorr appear at the northern tower in [Arcwind Point](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcwind_Point "Skyrim:Arcwind Point") after the player has killed her second-in-command [Linelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Linelle "Skyrim:Linelle") and followed the hints from [Linelle's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Linelle%27s_Note "Skyrim:Linelle's Note"). One of the other bounty hunters who went after Crowstooth, [Bjormund Wind-Strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Bjormund_Wind-Strider "Skyrim:Bjormund Wind-Strider"), lies dead at the top of the tower and can be looted for his unique Dragonplate Armor.

Be prepared for a difficult battle before you even get to Crowstooth; high-level [Draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") will be present at Arcwind Point and are difficult to avoid as you take the path north to reach the tower. If [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") is complete and [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") is also installed, a leveled [Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") appears, harassing the Draugr who will be [Shouting](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") at it when you arrive.

## Related Quests

- **[Bones for a Crow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bones_for_a_Crow "Skyrim:Bones for a Crow")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dragon_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dragon Plate"): Hunt down the Forsworn Crowstooth.

# Skyrim:Crustacean Extermination

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Exterminate unruly mudcrabs.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Viriya](/wiki/Skyrim:Viriya "Skyrim:Viriya") |
| Location(s): | West of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") |
| Reward: | [Alik'ri Fishing Rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27ri_Fishing_Rod "Skyrim:Alik'ri Fishing Rod") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE001\_Crab\_MQ2 |
| Added by: | [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [No Contest](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Contest "Skyrim:No Contest") | **Next →** [Tusked Terror](/wiki/Skyrim:Tusked_Terror "Skyrim:Tusked Terror") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [No Contest](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Contest "Skyrim:No Contest") | | → Next | [Tusked Terror](/wiki/Skyrim:Tusked_Terror "Skyrim:Tusked Terror") | | |

Crustacean Extermination

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read the *[Letter on Mudcrab Attacks](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_on_Mudcrab_Attacks "Skyrim:Letter on Mudcrab Attacks")*.
2. Travel to the shack west of Dawnstar.
3. Kill the 12 Frenzied Mudcrabs.
4. Search [Seviur](/wiki/Skyrim:Seviur "Skyrim:Seviur") for his [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Seviur%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Seviur's Journal") and read it.
5. Return to Viriya.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Swarm of frenzied mudcrabs

This quest can be started after [No Contest](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Contest "Skyrim:No Contest") has been completed by talking to Viriya:

:   **Know of anyone in need of fishing work around Skyrim?**
:   *"Maybe you can help me. You're headed to Dawnstar. It's all in this note. This won't be easy, but that's why I'm sending you. Think you can handle it?"*
:   **I'm always up for one of your crab dilemmas.** / **Just point me toward something with claws, and I'll make it dead.**
:   *"Thanks."*

Either option leads to the same outcome. Viriya will hand you a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_on_Mudcrab_Attacks "Skyrim:Letter on Mudcrab Attacks") that mentions multiple accounts of fishermen being attacked near a small shack on the shore west of Dawnstar by a swarm of mudcrabs. Travel to the shack, west of Dawnstar to investigate. Once you arrive at the shack [frenzied mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Frenzied_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Frenzied Mudcrab") will begin to swarm you, kill all twelve of them.

Once you have killed all the mudcrabs, investigate the body of [Seviur](/wiki/Skyrim:Seviur "Skyrim:Seviur") to find his [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Seviur%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Seviur's Journal"). Read the journal and you will discover that Seviur was using pacification magic and necromancy on mudcrabs which started to fail, until eventually the mudcrabs turned on him in a frenzy. You can then return to Viriya to speak to her:

:   **The mudcrabs have been slain. They were driven into a fury by a necromancer.**
:   *"We sure show them, eh? Thanks for your part in all that."*
:   **Seviur drew them to the coast using magic, but he lost control over them.**
:   *"I understand. I've come to rely on you. There's something I want you to have. It was my father's. It would be my honor if you carried it. May the gods keep you."*
:   **This Alik'ri rod is fit for a master fisherman. Thank you, Viriya.**
:   *"Stay sharp out there."*

You will be rewarded with an [Alik'ri Fishing Rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27ri_Fishing_Rod "Skyrim:Alik'ri Fishing Rod") and the ability to craft the rod.

## Quest Stages

Now that the mudcrabs have been defeated, I should return to Viriya. *Objective 50:* Return to Viriya |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 38, 300.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE001_Crab_MQ2 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE001_Crab_MQ2`.

# Skyrim:Crypt of the Heart

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), checked by [Dwarfmp](/wiki/User:Dwarfmp "User:Dwarfmp") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Investigate rumors of a ghost that haunts the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Started by reading *[Crypt of the Heart - Draft](/wiki/Skyrim:Crypt_of_the_Heart_-_Draft "Skyrim:Crypt of the Heart - Draft")* at the Silver-Blood Inn in Markarth |
| Location(s): | [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn"), bridge next to [Reachcliff Secret Entrance](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachcliff_Secret_Entrance "Skyrim:Reachcliff Secret Entrance"), grave west of [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal"), [Karthspire Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire_Camp "Skyrim:Karthspire Camp") |
| Reward: | Full set of [Ebony Spell Knight Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Spell_Knight_Armor "Skyrim:Ebony Spell Knight Armor") ([enchanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Knight_Armor_Items#Ebony_Spell_Knight_Armor "Skyrim:Spell Knight Armor Items"), version dependent on quest completion), [iron Spell Knight armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Spell_Knight_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Spell Knight Armor"), [steel Spell Knight armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Spell_Knight_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Spell Knight Armor"); ability to craft each armor set |
| ID: | ccEDHSSE002\_Quest |
| Added by: | [Spell Knight Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Knight_Armor "Skyrim:Spell Knight Armor") |

A Breton ghost is known to haunt the banks of the Karth

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read *[Crypt of the Heart - Draft](/wiki/Skyrim:Crypt_of_the_Heart_-_Draft "Skyrim:Crypt of the Heart - Draft")* in the [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn").
2. Travel to the bridge next to [Reachcliff Secret Entrance](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachcliff_Secret_Entrance "Skyrim:Reachcliff Secret Entrance") and follow the [Ghost Knight](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_Knight "Skyrim:Ghost Knight") to his grave.
3. Defeat the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") at the grave and read *[Forsworn Shaman's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Shaman%27s_Note "Skyrim:Forsworn Shaman's Note")*.
4. Locate the [Beldama Witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Beldama_Witch "Skyrim:Beldama Witch") at [Karthspire Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire_Camp "Skyrim:Karthspire Camp") and take the [Corrupted Human Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Corrupted_Human_Heart "Skyrim:Corrupted Human Heart").
5. Return to the knight's grave and make a choice:
   - Place the corrupted heart in the grave and defeat the knight's corrupted spirit in combat, then loot his grave for a set of Ebony Spell Knight Armor.
   - Use the [Shrine of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mara "Skyrim:Shrine of Mara") to cleanse the knight's heart, then return it to his grave to be given a set of Ebony Spell Knight Armor by the appeased spirit.

### The Order of the Crypt

A lone flower marks the site of the ghostly apparitions

This quest will automatically begin upon installing the [Spell Knight Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Knight_Armor "Skyrim:Spell Knight Armor") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). You will be directed to visit the [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") to seek out rumors that might have crossed the border from [High Rock](/wiki/Lore:High_Rock "Lore:High Rock"). Once at the inn, your quest marker will direct you to a guest room containing a book named *[Crypt of the Heart - Draft](/wiki/Skyrim:Crypt_of_the_Heart_-_Draft "Skyrim:Crypt of the Heart - Draft")*. Reading it will reveal the story of the Order of the Crypt, a knightly order from [Shornhelm](/wiki/Lore:Shornhelm "Lore:Shornhelm"), and the tragic tale of a knight named [Simon Rodayne](/wiki/Skyrim:Simon_Rodayne "Skyrim:Simon Rodayne") who fell in love with (or was tricked by) a witch of the [Beldama Wyrd](/wiki/Lore:Beldama_Wyrd "Lore:Beldama Wyrd") named [Daenella](/wiki/Skyrim:Daenella "Skyrim:Daenella"). Their relationship brought the order into conflict with the witches, driving the coven further and further east. It is said that Simon's ghost haunts the banks of the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River"), below his hilltop tomb.

You will then be directed to investigate these ghost sightings by travelling to a bridge that crosses the Karth River just next to [Reachcliff Secret Entrance](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachcliff_Secret_Entrance "Skyrim:Reachcliff Secret Entrance"). On this bridge, you will find a lone [red mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"); when approached, a [Ghost Knight](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_Knight "Skyrim:Ghost Knight") will appear behind you and will wander off to the south, towards [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal").

Follow the ghost as it makes its way up the slope. It will guide you to a grave west of Dushnikh Yal, which is surrounded by three hostile [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). Kill the attackers and loot the [Forsworn Shaman](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Shaman "Skyrim:Forsworn Shaman")'s body. She will be carrying a *[Forsworn Shaman's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Shaman%27s_Note "Skyrim:Forsworn Shaman's Note")*, which you must read to progress the quest. It reveals that the Beldama Wyrd has come to [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") in search of Daenella in order to punish her for her betrayal. They have taken Simon's heart from his grave and have brought it to [Karthspire Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire_Camp "Skyrim:Karthspire Camp") to defile it. Surrounding the grave, you will find the bodies of two [Knights of the Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Knight_of_the_Crypt "Skyrim:Knight of the Crypt") who had been sent to the Reach to track down and kill the Beldama witches. If you wish, you can loot their bodies for a full set of [Iron Spell Knight Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Spell_Knight_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Spell Knight Armor") and [Steel Spell Knight Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Spell_Knight_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Spell Knight Armor").

Daenella and her lover's heart

### A Stolen Heart

Journey to [Karthspire Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire_Camp "Skyrim:Karthspire Camp") and prepare for a fight; the campsite is swarming with Forsworn, and with this Creation installed you will have to deal with the added threat of [Beldama Witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Beldama_Witch "Skyrim:Beldama Witch") and a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") called the [Beldama Ward Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Beldama_Ward_Mother "Skyrim:Beldama Ward Mother"). They are located on the eastern side of the camp.

Once you've subdued the many enemies at the campsite, approach the sacrificial altar where the Beldama witches are found. On it, you will find the corpse of Daenella, who had been captured by the witches and killed with the knowledge that the Ward Mother planned to corrupt her beloved's heart and return it to his grave tainted, damning his soul for eternity. Sure enough, you will find a [Corrupted Human Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Corrupted_Human_Heart "Skyrim:Corrupted Human Heart") on a pedestal in front of the altar. Take it and return to the knight's grave.

### A Choice

Lovers reunited

A set of ebony armor is your reward

Once you have the heart, you will be instructed to return it to the knight's grave, with the optional step of first purifying the heart of corruption.

If you choose to place the corrupted heart within the grave, the corrupted spirit of Simon Rodayne will appear and attack you for damning his soul. He wields a [bound sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Sword "Skyrim:Bound Sword") in combat. Once you banish the ghost, you will be directed to loot his grave for a full set of enchanted [Ebony Spell Knight Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Spell_Knight_Armor "Skyrim:Ebony Spell Knight Armor") in order to complete the quest. This set has enchantments focused on offense (see [Spell Knight Armor items](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Knight_Armor_Items#Ebony_Spell_Knight_Armor "Skyrim:Spell Knight Armor Items")).

If you instead wish to purify his heart, you must first activate the [Shrine of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mara "Skyrim:Shrine of Mara") found at his tomb. Once this is done, place [Simon Rodayne's Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Simon_Rodayne%27s_Heart "Skyrim:Simon Rodayne's Heart") within his grave. This will cause a brief apparition of Simon and Daenella, finally reunited in death. The ghostly lovers will then disappear, and in their place a full set of enchanted Ebony Spell Knight Armor will materialize above the grave. This set has enchantments focused on defense. Take the armor to complete the quest.

Regardless of which option you choose, you will now be able to craft Spell Knight armor from [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel"), and [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") at any [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), provided you have the necessary skill perks.

## Notes

- The name of this quest (and the related book) is a reference to the [Crypt of Hearts](/wiki/Lore:Crypt_of_Hearts "Lore:Crypt of Hearts"), which the Order of the Crypt is sworn to protect.
- Once the Crypt of the Heart-Draft is read at Silver-Blood Inn you can head straight to the gravesite of Simon Rodayne circumventing the bridge ghost.
- The Beldama coven can be attacked directly without going through Karthspire Camp by heading southwest from [Soljund's Sinkhole](/wiki/Skyrim:Soljund%27s_Sinkhole "Skyrim:Soljund's Sinkhole") and approaching the altar from above.
- At Karthspire Camp, the dead giant on the altar and the giant's toe will be absent during this quest, replaced by Daenella and the Corrupted Human Heart.

## Bugs

- The Knights of the Crypt may not spawn around Rodayne's grave.
- The quest may mark as completed after picking up three of the armor pieces, making it impossible to pick up the fourth.
