Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccEDHSSE002_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccEDHSSE002_Quest`.

## Overview

Crystaldrift Cave

**Crystaldrift Cave** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). It contains only one zone, *[Crystaldrift Cave](#Crystaldrift_Cave)*.

It serves as the final resting place for an insane [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Gadnor "Skyrim:Gadnor"), with a shrine to [Kynareth](/wiki/Lore:Kynareth "Lore:Kynareth") built to watch over him and bring peace to weary travelers.

## Related Quests

- **[Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(B) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (B)")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear out a beast den. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Recruit [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran")'s old allies for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Nerveshatter](/wiki/Skyrim:Nerveshatter_(quest) "Skyrim:Nerveshatter (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers"): Track down the Daedric artifact Nerveshatter.

### Exterior

The path to the cave is a short way past [Snow-Shod Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow-Shod_Farm "Skyrim:Snow-Shod Farm") coming from Riften. It winds its way around before reaching a fork in the path: taking the right-hand path takes you past the cave entrance. It then loops around the rock outcrop that the cave is formed from, passing a path to [Lost Tongue Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Tongue_Overlook "Skyrim:Lost Tongue Overlook") and a [dragon mound](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mounds "Skyrim:Dragon Mounds") before completing the loop along the left-hand path. As you approach the cave, there are up to two leveled animals standing guard by a dead [deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer "Skyrim:Deer"). Blood is splattered on the ground around the cave entrance. Following the loop past the cave, to the south, you come to a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") on the right after a short distance.

### Crystaldrift Cave

As you enter the cave, there will be a random grouping of animals which may attack each other first. After descending an earthen ramp and entering the cave proper, there is a pile of eight portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks") that have been knocked out of a long open box in front of you. To the right, on a large rock against the northwest wall is a [shrine of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Shrine of Kynareth"), with a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a [plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate") holding five loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), and several lit candles around it. With the [Saints & Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, you can also find the journal *[Gadnor's Last Wishes](/wiki/Skyrim:Gadnor%27s_Last_Wishes "Skyrim:Gadnor's Last Wishes")* on the shrine, which gives instructions on how to obtain the artifact [Nerveshatter](/wiki/Skyrim:Nerveshatter "Skyrim:Nerveshatter"). In the western quarter of the cave is a camp consisting of a campfire, with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") hanging over it and a couple of pots holding three [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and three [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"). There is a hay pile against the west wall, with a rack to the right holding two bunches of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"). To the left of the hay pile, against the southwest wall is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot. There is also a barrel containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") with an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") on top near the fire.

On the other side of the fire next to a rock pillar is a crate with a basket holding two [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and a few more loose vegetables on top. In the center of the cave is a large flat-topped rock. Resting on top of the slab are the remains of a [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") adventurer named [Gadnor](/wiki/Skyrim:Gadnor "Skyrim:Gadnor") with his unique [Staff of Charming](/wiki/Skyrim:Gadnor%27s_Staff_of_Charming "Skyrim:Gadnor's Staff of Charming") lying next to him. He carries a copy of the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Mystery of Talara, v 2](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystery_of_Talara,_v_2 "Skyrim:Mystery of Talara, v 2")*. Around the rock are three [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") plants, with several fungi found throughout the cave, including five [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), five [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), and one [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"). To the northeast, near a shallow pool of water, is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"). At the rear of the cave, a short way up an earthen ramp against the south wall, is a [moonstone ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein").

## Maps

- 

  Crystaldrift Cave

Cuinanthil

**Cuinanthil** is a [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") [destruction mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction_Mage "Skyrim:Destruction Mage") who can be found with his [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") bodyguard [Inimoro](/wiki/Skyrim:Inimoro "Skyrim:Inimoro") in Markarth. He carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a copy of [Beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar_(book) "Skyrim:Beggar (book)"), his [family seal](/wiki/Skyrim:Cuinanthil%27s_Family_Seal "Skyrim:Cuinanthil's Family Seal") and a selection of [random items](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#LootCitizenPocketsRich "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). He wears [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"). He is the brother of [Ernanthil](/wiki/Skyrim:Ernanthil "Skyrim:Ernanthil").

## Related Quests

- **[Fortunate Son](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortunate_Son "Skyrim:Fortunate Son")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup"): Claim a fortune.

## Spells

Cuinanthil knows the following spells:

[Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration")
:   [Stoneflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Stoneflesh "Skyrim:Stoneflesh")

[Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction")
:   [Chain Lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Chain Lightning"), [Lightning Bolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Bolt "Skyrim:Lightning Bolt"), [Thunderbolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Thunderbolt "Skyrim:Thunderbolt"), [Lightning Cloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Cloak "Skyrim:Lightning Cloak")

[Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration")
:   [Close Wounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Close_Wounds "Skyrim:Close Wounds"), [Steadfast Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steadfast_Ward "Skyrim:Steadfast Ward")

## Quest-Related Dialogue

When spoken to:

:   **Never mind, I mistook you for someone else.**
:   *"I understand."*

:   **Spare a coin for a beggar?**
:   *"Walk away. Now."*

:   **Are you new in town? I can help show you around.**
:   *"Walk away. Now."*

You can try and inform Cuinanthil about the planned robbery:

:   **Someone is trying to rob you. I have proof.**
:   *"You expect me to believe that?"*

:   :   **In this note the thief mentions you by name. (Persuade)**
    :   *"It would seem so. Now, get out of my way."* (succeed)
    :   *"That doesn't change anything. Now, get out of my way."* (fail)

:   :   **On second thought, never mind.**
    :   *"And now you'll walk away, if you know what's good for you."*

You will then need to return to him later in the quest in a courier's outfit:

:   **I've been looking for you.**

    :   - He doesn't reply.

Next choices of dialogue will appear.

:   **I'm a courier and I have an important message to deliver to you.**
:   *"You expect me to believe that?"*

:   **Greetings, I'm with the courier service.**
:   *"You expect me to believe that?"*

:   **Got something I'm supposed to deliver - your hands only.**
:   *(He turns to his Dunmer body guard and says), "Do you wish to confess something now?'* (This choice of dialogue will cause the bodyguard to start fighting city guards and civilians in his attempt to escape arrest.)

Culling the Beast

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Fura Bloodmouth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fura_Bloodmouth "Skyrim:Fura Bloodmouth") or [Garan Marethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Garan_Marethi "Skyrim:Garan Marethi").
2. Kill the boss [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") in its lair.

## Detailed Walkthrough

You can talk to [Fura Bloodmouth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fura_Bloodmouth "Skyrim:Fura Bloodmouth") or [Garan Marethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Garan_Marethi "Skyrim:Garan Marethi") to receive this quest. They will explain either:

- *"A bunch of feral vampires are running wild, upsetting the mortals. When the prey is riled, it makes things difficult for us. Go cull the brutish beasts before the problem gets out of hand."*
- *"A cadre of lesser beasts has become a nuisance, taking too bold an approach to their feeding. The herd is becoming distressed, which makes it more difficult for us to slip in and out undetected. It is time to cull the weak."*

They will then mark a random location from a list of possible locations:
[Bloodlet Throne](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodlet_Throne "Skyrim:Bloodlet Throne"), [Broken Fang Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Fang_Cave "Skyrim:Broken Fang Cave"), [Haemar's Shame](/wiki/Skyrim:Haemar%27s_Shame "Skyrim:Haemar's Shame"), [Mara's Eye Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Mara%27s_Eye_Pond "Skyrim:Mara's Eye Pond"), [Moldering Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Moldering_Ruins "Skyrim:Moldering Ruins"), [Movarth's Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Movarth%27s_Lair "Skyrim:Movarth's Lair"), [Pinemoon Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinemoon_Cave "Skyrim:Pinemoon Cave"), [Potema's Catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Potema%27s_Catacombs "Skyrim:Potema's Catacombs"), [Redwater Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den "Skyrim:Redwater Den"), [Shriekwind Bastion](/wiki/Skyrim:Shriekwind_Bastion "Skyrim:Shriekwind Bastion")

You will be directed to kill the leveled vampire boss that is near the end of one of these locations. Upon return, you are rewarded three [Potions of Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Blood "Skyrim:Potion of Blood") with a chance of 25% or a radiant leveled enchanted item otherwise (a circlet, necklace, ring, a piece of heavy armor, a piece of light armor or a weapon). You'll be told one of the following lines:

- *"Good job. At first you may pity the thin-bloods. But after disposing of a few, you realize they aren't worth the worry."*
- *"You have done well. It may seem cruel that we hold our thin-blooded kin in low esteem. But our needs must come before theirs."*

## Notes

- This is a repeatable quest.

## Quest Stages

| Culling the Beast (DLC1RV02) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | <Alias=QuestGiver> has sent me to destroy the <Alias=Boss> at <Alias=Dungeon>. *Objective 10:* Kill the <Alias=Boss> at <Alias=Dungeon> |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Return to <Alias=QuestGiver> |
| 255 | ☑ | <Alias=QuestGiver> sent me to <Alias=Dungeon> where I destroyed the <Alias=Boss>. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1RV02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1RV02`.

# Skyrim:Cultist

## Overview

**Cultists** are mysterious followers of [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)"), the first [Dragonborn](/wiki/Lore:Dragonborn "Lore:Dragonborn"), who live in his [temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak") on the island of [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") and carry out his wishes. Once you have been recognized as Dragonborn during the quest [The Way of the Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Way_of_the_Voice "Skyrim:The Way of the Voice"), a pair of cultists will be sent to [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") to hunt you and kill you for being a "false" Dragonborn. All cultists are powerful mages, relying on summoning and elemental magic spells in combat. The type of cultist you encounter depends on your level, and you will continue to meet low-level cultists even at high levels.

### Cultists

A Cultist firing a shock spell

Cultists are members of the [Conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer_(class) "Skyrim:Conjurer (class)") NPC class and use [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") spells in battle. All cultists of Miraak wear a uniform of [robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Cultist_Robes "Skyrim:Cultist Robes"), [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Cultist_Boots "Skyrim:Cultist Boots"), [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Cultist_Gloves "Skyrim:Cultist Gloves"), and an eerie bone [mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Cultist_Mask "Skyrim:Cultist Mask"). Arch Cultists wear a standard [warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") outfit instead, consisting of a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Boots") along with [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), [hooded black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Black Mage Robes"), robes of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Alteration "Skyrim:Fortify Alteration"), robes of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Destruction "Skyrim:Fortify Destruction"), robes of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration"), or robes of [Fortify Magicka Rate](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka_Rate "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka Rate").

Cultists also carry a leveled dagger ([iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger"), [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Dagger "Skyrim:Glass Dagger"), or an enchanted dagger of any quality from iron to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric")). They also have a 10% chance to carry a leveled [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") or Destruction staff.

In addition to the gear listed above, cultists have a small chance to carry [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), Novice or Apprentice level [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") (common, uncommon, or rare), [recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes"), and a small amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). If the quest [Conjuration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Conjuration Ritual Spell") or [Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions") was completed, they are also carrying up to two [atronach forge recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge_Recipe "Skyrim:Atronach Forge Recipe") in their inventories - one at 2% chance for each completed quest.

On death, cultists have a 10% chance to drop potions and poisons, and a 5% chance to drop one of the following scrolls:

- **Alteration:** [Scroll of Mass Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Scroll of Mass Paralysis")
- **Conjuration:** [Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach"), [Scroll of Dread Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Dread_Zombie "Skyrim:Scroll of Dread Zombie")
- **Destruction:**[Scroll of Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Blizzard "Skyrim:Scroll of Blizzard"), [Scroll of Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Scroll of Fire Storm")
- **Illusion:** [Scroll of Call to Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Call_to_Arms "Skyrim:Scroll of Call to Arms"), [Scroll of Harmony](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Harmony "Skyrim:Scroll of Harmony"), [Scroll of Hysteria](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Hysteria "Skyrim:Scroll of Hysteria"), [Scroll of Mayhem](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mayhem "Skyrim:Scroll of Mayhem")
- **Restoration:** [Scroll of Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Bane of the Undead"), [Scroll of Guardian Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Guardian_Circle "Skyrim:Scroll of Guardian Circle")

Master Cultists and Arch Cultists have the same miscellaneous items and daggers as other cultists, and have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Chain Lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Staff of Chain Lightning"), [Staff of Fireballs](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Fireballs "Skyrim:Staff of Fireballs"), or a [Staff of Ice Storms](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ice_Storms "Skyrim:Staff of Ice Storms") and do not have the leveled lists for atronach forge recipes.

### Summoner Cultists

A Cultist with a flame atronach ally

These cultists have the ability to use Destruction magic as well, but prefer to summon [flame atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Flame Atronach") and [seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker") to fight alongside them. They wear the same cultist's outfit as the cultists listed above, except Master Cultists and Arch Cultists, who wear the warlock outfit instead. Otherwise, their weapons, staves, and miscellaneous inventory items are the same as non-summoner cultists.

## Related Quests

- **[Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_(quest) "Skyrim:Dragonborn (quest)")**: Travel to the island of [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") to find out what's happening there.
- **[The Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:The Temple of Miraak")**: Uncover the source of [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)")'s power in the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak").

### World Interactions

- **[Cultist Attack](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Cultists_vs_Player "Skyrim:World Interactions")** [DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")

## Dialogue

Cultists encountered in Solitude

### Dragonborn

Once the main quest [The Way of the Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Way_of_the_Voice "Skyrim:The Way of the Voice") is finished, you will be approached by a pair of hostile cultists at the first city or town you enter. These cultists will question you with *"You there! You're the one they call Dragonborn?"* You have several dialogue options with which to respond:

| Player Response | Cultists' Response |
| --- | --- |
| **"Yes, I am Dragonborn."** | *"Your lies fall on deaf ears, Deceiver. The True Dragonborn comes... You are but his shadow."* |
| **"The Greybeards seem to think so."** | *"Then it is too late. The lie has already taken root in the hearts of men. So we shall expose them to the falseness in their hearts by tearing out yours, Deceiver!"* |
| **"I don't know what you're talking about."** | *"Your lies fall on deaf ears, Deceiver! We know you are the False Dragonborn! You shall not stand in the way of the true Dragonborn's return. He comes soon, and we shall offer him your heart!"* |

Each response will eventually lead to them saying: *"When Lord Miraak appears all shall bear witness. None shall stand to oppose him!"* They will turn hostile and engage you in combat immediately thereafter.

You can also exit conversation with them, though they will still turn hostile immediately:
*"You cannot escape the truth. You cannot escape the True Dragonborn! When Lord Miraak appears all shall bear witness. None will stand to oppose him!"*

### Combat

- *The unworthy flee before the Master's power.*
- *Another offering for the Master.*
- *You cannot escape Miraak's sight!*
- *You cannot escape the Dragonborn's justice!*
- *You won't win!*
- *Miraak help me!*
- *I shall not fall!*
- *For Miraak!*
- *The truth will take you!*
- *Master, guide my hand!*
- *The true Dragonborn will judge you!*
- *You will be an offering to the Master!*
- *Your soul belongs to Miraak!*
- *The true Dragonborn returns to this world soon, and all will be judged!*
- *The rightful Dragonborn comes soon!*
- *We shall clear the way for the coming of the true Dragonborn!*
- *Your blood will flow in Miraak's name!*
- *Your false reign ends now!*
- *You would dare call yourself the true Dragonborn?*
- *I will purify the world for Miraak's return!*
- *None shall stand against Miraak!*

When cultists lose sight of you, they say:

- *Find them!*

## Notes

- You must be at least level 25 for random encounters with Cultists to appear in Skyrim. Ones on Solstheim will happen regardless of your level.

## Bugs

- The bodies of the Cultists that initially attack you during Dragonborn may never disappear, even if they are raised and subsequently become ash piles.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
  - To remove a body, open the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console"), click on the body to be removed, and use the `disable` command.
- Random encounters with Cultists are supposed to terminate after Miraak's death in [At the Summit of Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:At_the_Summit_of_Apocrypha "Skyrim:At the Summit of Apocrypha"), but don't.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.2, fixes this bug.
- The two Cultists outside the Temple of Miraak may never despawn even after the Dragonborn questline is finished. They may also respawn and attack you again.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.8, fixes this bug.

### Books

- ***[Atlas of Dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Atlas_of_Dragons "Skyrim:Atlas of Dragons")*** by [Brother Mathnan](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Brother_Mathnan "Lore:Books by Author") — A glossary of Skyrim's dragons
- ***[Skorm Snow-Strider's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Skorm_Snow-Strider%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Skorm Snow-Strider's Journal")*** by [Skorm Snow-Strider](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Skorm_Snow-Strider "Lore:Books by Author") — The journal of a First Era Nordic commander and his encounter with the Dragon Cult

Curate Melita

**Curate Melita** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") Curate of the Tribunal Temple. She can be rescued during [Careless Curation](/wiki/Skyrim:Careless_Curation "Skyrim:Careless Curation"), and will relocate herself to [Ashfall's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfall%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Ashfall's Tear") as an Apothecary vendor for the [Tribunal Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribunal_Temple "Skyrim:Tribunal Temple"). Alternatively, you can choose to kill her.

## Related Quests

- **[Careless Curation](/wiki/Skyrim:Careless_Curation "Skyrim:Careless Curation")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Find the missing Curate to retrieve the [Mask of Sotha Sil](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Sotha_Sil "Skyrim:Mask of Sotha Sil").

### Careless Curation

:   *"Maybe you can help me."*

:   :   **Actually, I'm going to kill you and take the mask.**
    :   *"Don't hurt me. You win."*

:   :   **Do you have the mask?**
    :   *"Uh... yeah."*

:   :   **I'm here to rescue you on behalf of the Goddess.**
    :   *"Oh. Good job. Here... My way of saying thanks."*

If talked with after choosing the first option:

:   **Let me untie your bonds.**
:   *"Thanks!"*

## Notes

- She's supposed to be a [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") trainer and does have a conversation about that, but you can never receive [training](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") from her, even with a low Restoration skill.

Curwe outside Loreius Farm

**Curwe** is a [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") and the wife of [Vantus Loreius](/wiki/Skyrim:Vantus_Loreius "Skyrim:Vantus Loreius"). She lives with him on [their farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Loreius_Farm "Skyrim:Loreius Farm"). If you alert the guards to Cicero's activities during [Delayed Burial](/wiki/Skyrim:Delayed_Burial "Skyrim:Delayed Burial"), then Cicero will kill Curwe and her husband.

She wakes up every morning at 7am and starts the day with a one-hour breakfast. At 8am she heads outside and starts working the land, at times sweeping the porch. At 7pm she takes a one-hour dinner before she goes to bed early at 8pm.

Curwe wears a set of green farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000261bd "Skyrim:Boots"). She is equipped with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Loreius_Famhouse "Skyrim:Key to Loreius Famhouse") to the farmhouse, as well as a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

After betraying [Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero") during [Delayed Burial](/wiki/Skyrim:Delayed_Burial "Skyrim:Delayed Burial"), the corpse in Loreius Farm uses a different form, the refid is 0007f42c, the baseid is 0007f42a.

## Related Quests

- **[Delayed Burial](/wiki/Skyrim:Delayed_Burial "Skyrim:Delayed Burial")**: Convince an unwilling [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Vantus_Loreius "Skyrim:Vantus Loreius") to help fix a stranded [jester's](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero") broken wagon wheel.

## Dialogue

Attempting to speak to her will result in only one response:

:   *"You need something talk to my husband. Vantus Loreius. Or just Loreius, if it's all the same to you."*

## Conversations

While she doesn't talk much to strangers, she will often debate with her husband:

:   **Curwe**: *"You know, I was thinking of expanding the herb garden. Make room for some new plants I'm planning."*
:   **Vantus**: *"That should be all right. How much space were you planning?"*
:   **Curwe**: *"Oh, half the field should do."*
:   **Vantus**: *"Half the field? What could need half the field?"*
:   **Curwe**: *"I just think pollinating would be easier if I could do a lot of plants at once."*
:   **Vantus**: *"Uh... why don't we talk about this later?"*

:   **Curwe**: *"I had a look at that boneyard the other day, Vantus. The one to the Northwest."*
:   **Vantus**: *"I told you I don't like you going there. I've seen scavengers picking at the mammoths. They could be dangerous."*

# Skyrim:Cynric Endell

## Overview

| Cynric Endell (RefID: 000D4FDA) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionThievesGuild](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionThievesGuild "Skyrim:CrimeFactionThievesGuild"); [FavorExcludedFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction "Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction"); [Riften Thieves Guild Headquarters Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Thieves_Guild_Headquarters_Faction "Skyrim:Riften Thieves Guild Headquarters Faction"); [ThievesGuildFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:ThievesGuildFaction "Skyrim:ThievesGuildFaction") (Agent); [TownRiftenFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownRiftenFaction "Skyrim:TownRiftenFaction") | | |

Cynric Endell practicing archery

**Cynric Endell** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [thief](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatThief "Skyrim:CombatThief") and a member of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). Before joining the Guild, he worked as a jailbreaker but quit after a botched job landed him in a [High Rock](/wiki/Lore:High_Rock "Lore:High Rock") prison for three long years. He now spends most of his time training his archery skills.

After waking up at 8am, Cynric will wander around the Cistern for two hours and then head over to the dining table for a two hour breakfast. Once he's finished, he'll relax for another two hours and then spend the rest of his day training his marksmanship on the Cistern practice target, with a four-hour break between 6pm and 10pm. At 2am he calls it a day and heads back to his bed, which is just to the left when entering the Cistern from the secret entrance.

He wears the standard [Thieves Guild armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Thieves_Guild_Armor "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"), [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Thieves_Guild_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"), [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Thieves_Guild_Boots "Skyrim:Specialty Gear") and [hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Thieves_Guild_Hood_Alt "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"). He is equipped with a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") and a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow") supplemented with 12 [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"). He also carries two [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and up to 18 septims.

## Related Quests

- **[The Pursuit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pursuit "Skyrim:The Pursuit")**: Break into [Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey")'s [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Riftweald_Manor "Skyrim:Riftweald Manor") and search for clues.
- **[Under New Management](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_New_Management "Skyrim:Under New Management")**: Become the Guild Master of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").

### The Pursuit

Before you convince the guild of [Karliah](/wiki/Skyrim:Karliah "Skyrim:Karliah")'s innocence, he'll refuse to speak with you:

:   *"So it's true. You've turned traitor. I can't believe it."*

After though, he'll be stunned:

:   *"I never saw this coming, I thought we were just having a run of bad luck."*

### Under New Management

Before speaking to Brynjolf:

:   *"So, you're finally going to make Guild Master, eh? Well, you better track down Brynjolf to seal the deal."*

If spoken to during the ceremony:

:   *"Hang on. When the ceremony's done, we'll talk."*

## Dialogue

When greeted he'll reply:

:   *"I think you're all right. In fact, I'm kind of impressed how well you're doing around here. Just keep it between us, okay?"*
:   *"I've seen a lot of thieves come and go, but I've never seen anyone as good as me."*
:   *"I could crack the lock on any house blindfolded before you even got your picks out of your pocket."*
:   *"Been in the Guild a long time... joined right after [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf"). Not interested in leadership though, that's more his kind of thing."*
:   *"I don't care if [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") was chosen as a Guild Third over me, she deserved it."*
:   *"I kind of like watching things from where I am. Making money is all I care about."*

When spoken to directly he can be asked about his profession:

:   **How did you become so good at picking locks?**
:   *"Pull up a chair, my friend... this is quite a tale. When I started out in this business, I wasn't really interested in the Guild or being a thief."*
:   **With skills like yours? Why not?**
:   *"I didn't mean to imply I was earning an honest living either. With my lock picking aptitude, I was a natural at jailbreaking... made a great deal of gold doing it too."*
:   **Jailbreaking? What's that?**
:   *"It's where a client pays you to get arrested, and you get thrown into a prison for the express purpose of breaking out. Usually it's to free someone the client cares about... and sometimes to... well, to kill someone on their behalf. Either way, the trick was in the escape, and that's where my strengths came in handy."*
:   **Why did you stop doing it?**
:   *"Well, as a jailbreaker, you work alone. No Guild to back you up. I'd do jobs for the Thieves Guild and the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Lore:Dark_Brotherhood "Lore:Dark Brotherhood"), but if things didn't go as planned, I was on my own."*
:   **I think I see what you're getting at.**
:   *"The last jailbreak I attempted failed. I was imprisoned in High Rock for three years before they let me go. After that I promised myself I'd never do it again."*
:   **Why did you join the Guild and not the Brotherhood?**
:   *"I don't know. I think I realized that out in the world, my skills would bring me more wealth as a thief rather than an assassin. Killing someone in a jail is much easier than what the Dark Brotherhood deals with. I guess I wanted to play it safe. I already knew [Delvin](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory"), I asked if I could join up, and that was that."*

Once you become Guild Master, he'll offer his support:

:   *"As long as you continue to make us all rich, I'm behind you."*

If you've been suspended from the Guild, Cynric will refuse to talk to you, stating:

:   *"Hmph. I don't talk with Guild traitors."*

When exiting conversation he can say:

:   *"Some other time, perhaps."*
:   *"I'm sure we'll speak again."*

## Conversations

Cynric will at times engage in random conversations with fellow guild members, as listed below:

:   **Cynric**: *"So, [Thrynn](/wiki/Skyrim:Thrynn "Skyrim:Thrynn"), you were a bandit, huh?"*
:   **Thrynn**: *"Yeah, what of it?"*
:   **Cynric**: *"So is it true, bandits get... you know, real friendly with the wildlife?"*
:   **Thrynn**: *"You're an idiot."*

:   **[Niruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Niruin "Skyrim:Niruin")**: *"All right. I have everything you asked for all ready to go."*
:   **Cynric**: *"I hope this deal goes through. I'm putting quite a bit of coin on the line... and the last two you set up fell through."*
:   **Niruin**: *"I don't understand it either. They were a sure thing, I swear."*
:   **Cynric**: *"You just better hope this one isn't another waste of my coin."*

:   **[Rune](/wiki/Skyrim:Rune "Skyrim:Rune")**: *"Take a look around. Have you ever laid eyes on such wealth?"*
:   **Cynric**: *"Never. This is the best the Guild's done since I've been a part of it."*

## Notes

- In the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*, the summary for him reads *"Cynric is an older member of the Thieves Guild, joining shortly after Brynjolf and Delvin Mallory. He's quiet, reserved, and generally not as boisterous as the rest of his fellow Guild members, but once in conversation, his extreme cynicism surfaces. His specialty is break-ins, which he executes with his superior lockpicking abilities. He's never been a problem for the Guild but tends to shy away from leadership, explaining why Vex surpassed him as a Guild Third."*

# Skyrim:Daedric Quests

## Overview

**Daedric quests** are quests given by the [Daedric Princes](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes"), usually with a Daedric [Artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Artifacts "Skyrim:Artifacts") as a reward. Daedric quests are not considered [side quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Side_Quests "Skyrim:Side Quests").

Most Daedric quests also have an associated "pointer quest", a miscellaneous quest objective that leads you to the actual Daedric quest. It is not always necessary to obtain the pointer quest before starting the Daedric quest; in some cases, you can start the Daedric quest by simply visiting the related shrine or other location where a Daedric worshipper can be found.

Most Daedric quests can only be removed from your active quest list upon successful completion. However, a few of the quests can be failed, which usually occurs if you kill the quest giver. For example, you can kill [Silus Vesuius](/wiki/Skyrim:Silus_Vesuius "Skyrim:Silus Vesuius") upon entering his home, resulting in the failure of [Pieces of the Past](/wiki/Skyrim:Pieces_of_the_Past "Skyrim:Pieces of the Past").

| Daedric Quest | Prince | Level Req. | Reward | | Pointer Quest and/or Shrine Location |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |

## Achievements

[Achievements](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") related to Daedric quests are:

-  **Daedric Influence** (10 points/Bronze) — Acquire a Daedric [Artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Artifacts "Skyrim:Artifacts")
-  **Oblivion Walker** (30 points/Silver) — Collect 15 Daedric [Artifacts](/wiki/Skyrim:Artifacts "Skyrim:Artifacts")
  - It is possible to miss the Oblivion Walker achievement. To receive it, you must not simply complete 15 Daedric quests, but must also choose the quest endings that give you Daedric Artifacts.
  - Quests which do not simply result in you receiving one artifact are:
    - Those which can be completed without receiving an artifact: [A Daedra's Best Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Daedra%27s_Best_Friend "Skyrim:A Daedra's Best Friend") ([The Rueful Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rueful_Axe "Skyrim:The Rueful Axe") does not count as a Daedric Artifact), [Pieces of the Past](/wiki/Skyrim:Pieces_of_the_Past "Skyrim:Pieces of the Past"), and [Waking Nightmare](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare").
    - Those which can be failed: [Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane"), [Pieces of the Past](/wiki/Skyrim:Pieces_of_the_Past "Skyrim:Pieces of the Past"), [The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors"), and [The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death").
    - Those where an NPC can die before giving you the quest: [A Daedra's Best Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Daedra%27s_Best_Friend "Skyrim:A Daedra's Best Friend") and [The Whispering Door](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Whispering_Door "Skyrim:The Whispering Door").
    - [Blindsighted](/wiki/Skyrim:Blindsighted "Skyrim:Blindsighted"): the [Skeleton Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton_Key "Skyrim:Skeleton Key") does not count as a Daedric Artifact for these achievements.
      - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.2, fixes this bug.
  - [Ill Met By Moonlight](/wiki/Skyrim:Ill_Met_By_Moonlight "Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight"): both the [Savior's Hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Savior%27s_Hide "Skyrim:Savior's Hide") and the [Ring of Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Hircine "Skyrim:Ring of Hircine") count as Daedric Artifacts, and both can be obtained at the same time.
  - You do not need to possess the artifacts to increment the achievement counter; just choose the ending that results in the quest adding to your artifacts total. However, all but one of the quests have the increment scripted to taking possession of an artifact. The exception is [The Cursed Tribe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe"), where the quest ends but the artifact is placed in front of you rather than in your inventory. You do not need to keep the artifacts once you have them, though they can be used to verify which quests have been completed "correctly".
  - The game tracks the number of Daedric Artifacts and the number of completed Daedric quests separately. The only relevant statistic visible in-game is the number of "Daedric Quests Completed" (under "General Stats" in your journal). Since the quest statistic is incremented even if you complete a quest without receiving the artifact, it may not reliably indicate your progress toward the Oblivion Walker achievement.
  - Although [Black Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book "Skyrim:Black Book")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") are artifacts associated with [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Lore:Hermaeus_Mora "Lore:Hermaeus Mora"), they do not count toward these achievements.
  - Daedric Artifacts added through the [Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") do not count toward these achievements. These include the [Bittercup](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup_(item) "Skyrim:Bittercup (item)")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup"), the [Bow of Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow_of_Shadows_(item) "Skyrim:Bow of Shadows (item)")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow_of_Shadows "Skyrim:Bow of Shadows"), the [Gray Cowl of Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:Gray_Cowl_of_Nocturnal "Skyrim:Gray Cowl of Nocturnal")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_Returns! "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl Returns!"), [Goldbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand_(item) "Skyrim:Goldbrand (item)")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand "Skyrim:Goldbrand"), [Nerveshatter](/wiki/Skyrim:Nerveshatter "Skyrim:Nerveshatter")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers"), the [Ring of Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Khajiit "Skyrim:Ring of Khajiit")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"), [Scourge](/wiki/Skyrim:Scourge "Skyrim:Scourge")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause"), [Shadowrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowrend_(item) "Skyrim:Shadowrend (item)")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowrend "Skyrim:Shadowrend"), the [Staff of Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Sheogorath_(item) "Skyrim:Staff of Sheogorath (item)")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Sheogorath "Skyrim:Staff of Sheogorath"), the [Sword of Jyggalag](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword_of_Jyggalag "Skyrim:Sword of Jyggalag")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers"), and [Umbra](/wiki/Skyrim:Umbra_(item) "Skyrim:Umbra (item)")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Umbra "Skyrim:Umbra").
    - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.2, addresses this issue. However, it is only fixed for content within the patch's purview (the three artifacts from free Creation Club content: [Nerveshatter](/wiki/Skyrim:Nerveshatter "Skyrim:Nerveshatter")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers"), the [Ring of Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Khajiit "Skyrim:Ring of Khajiit")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"), and the [Sword of Jyggalag](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword_of_Jyggalag "Skyrim:Sword of Jyggalag")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers")).

# Skyrim:Daedric Shrines

## Overview

Sacellum of Boethiah

 This page lists all the **Daedric shrines** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). [Shrines](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines "Skyrim:Shrines") to the [Nine Divines](/wiki/Lore:Nine_Divines "Lore:Nine Divines") are listed on a separate page. Many of the Daedric shrines are involved in the [Daedric quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Quests "Skyrim:Daedric Quests").

:    **[Shrine of Azura](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Azura "Skyrim:Shrine of Azura")** — The shrine to the Daedric Prince Azura. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shrine+of+Azura)
:    **[Sacellum of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacellum_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Sacellum of Boethiah")** — The shrine to the Daedric Prince Boethiah. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sacellum+of+Boethiah)
:    **[Haemar's Shame](/wiki/Skyrim:Haemar%27s_Shame "Skyrim:Haemar's Shame")** — A medium-sized cave east of Helgen containing vampires. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Haemar%27s+Shame)
:    **[Giant's Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Grove "Skyrim:Giant's Grove")** — A grove accessed through Fallowstone Cave containing a giant whose tribe has defiled a shrine of Malacath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Giant%27s+Grove)
:    **[Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mehrunes_Dagon "Skyrim:Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon")** — The shrine to the Daedric Prince Mehrunes Dagon. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shrine+of+Mehrunes+Dagon)
:    **[Statue to Meridia](/wiki/Skyrim:Statue_to_Meridia "Skyrim:Statue to Meridia")** — The shrine to the Daedric Prince Meridia. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Statue+to+Meridia)
:   **[Abandoned House](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_House "Skyrim:Abandoned House")** — A building in Markarth next to Arnleif and Sons Trading Company with a shrine to the Daedric Prince Molag Bal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Abandoned+House)
:    **[Reachcliff Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachcliff_Cave "Skyrim:Reachcliff Cave")** — A small cave east-southeast of Markarth containing draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reachcliff+Cave)
:   **[Shrine of Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Nocturnal "Skyrim:Shrine of Nocturnal")** — The Thieves Guild's headquarters in Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Ragged+Flagon+-+Cistern)
:    **[Shrine to Peryite](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_to_Peryite "Skyrim:Shrine to Peryite")** — The shrine to the Daedric Prince Peryite. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shrine+to+Peryite)

## Notes

- There are also small obelisks known as "Daedric shrines" that confer a blessing on activation similar to the blessings provided by the shrines to the Nine Divines. These smaller Daedric shrines for [Azura](/wiki/Lore:Azura "Lore:Azura"), [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah"), and [Mephala](/wiki/Lore:Mephala "Lore:Mephala") are found in the [Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple "Skyrim:Temple") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim").

Daenella

Daenella is a dead [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") who was a witch of the [Beldama Wyrd](/wiki/Lore:Beldama_Wyrd "Lore:Beldama Wyrd"). Her body is found at [Karthspire Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire_Camp "Skyrim:Karthspire Camp") during [Crypt of the Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Crypt_of_the_Heart "Skyrim:Crypt of the Heart"), on the rock where normally the dead [Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") lies.

She wears [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes") with matching [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"). A random selection of gold based on your level can be found on her body, and possibly a [gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Leveled_Gems "Skyrim:Leveled Lists") and/or an [ingredient](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). Additionally, she knows the spell [Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing").

Daenella

Daenella appears as a ghost after you've cleansed [Simon Rodayne's Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Simon_Rodayne%27s_Heart "Skyrim:Simon Rodayne's Heart") at his grave, together with the ghost of [Simon Rodayne](/wiki/Skyrim:Simon_Rodayne "Skyrim:Simon Rodayne"), to show their thanks for reuniting them.

Other than her ghostly appearance and the lack of leveled loot on her, she is identical to the version above.

## Related Quests

- **[Crypt of the Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Crypt_of_the_Heart "Skyrim:Crypt of the Heart")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Knight_Armor "Skyrim:Spell Knight Armor"): Investigate rumors of a ghost that haunts the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River").

## Notes

- Her body cannot be [reanimated](/wiki/Skyrim:Reanimate "Skyrim:Reanimate").

## Bugs

- Daenella's body may be found before the start of the related quest. A sacrificed [Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") will be lying on top of her corpse.

Dagny

**Dagny** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") who lives in [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach"). She is the daughter of [Jarl Balgruuf the Greater](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater"), and sister of [Frothar](/wiki/Skyrim:Frothar "Skyrim:Frothar") and [Nelkir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelkir "Skyrim:Nelkir").

She, like the Jarl's other children, spends all her time inside Dragonsreach. She wakes up at 6am, and stays in the kid's room in the Jarl's Quarters talking with the other children before heading out to play in the main hall at 9am. She spends her whole day in the hall, taking an hour long lunch at 12pm and a two hour long dinner at 5pm. After dinner, she heads back to the kid's room and waits there till 10pm, when she goes to bed for eight hours of sleep.

She wears red [child's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Child%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Child's Clothes") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes#000e80a8 "Skyrim:Shoes"). She carries a selection of [food and toys](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Child "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), and a small amount of gold.

## Dialogue

When approached she can say:

:   *"Absurd that you can't get good sweet rolls in this skeeverhole of a city."*
:   *"One of the new servants? Remember that I like my meat rare."*
:   *"Blasted war. I was due a new dress from [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), but it will never get here."*
:   *"I'm so angry, I can hardly stand it! Father promised me a new dress days ago, now where is it?"*

If you've [captured](/wiki/Skyrim:The_World-Eater%27s_Eyrie "Skyrim:The World-Eater's Eyrie") [Odahviing](/wiki/Skyrim:Odahviing "Skyrim:Odahviing") and approach her, she will say:

:   *"Father won't let me go see the dragon."*

## Conversations

Dagny sometimes complains to Frothar as well, though he won't put up with it:

**Dagny**: *"I'm so angry, I can hardly stand it! Father promised me a new dress days ago, now where is it?"*
**Frothar**: *"It takes a while to make a dress, Dagny. You have to be patient."*
**Dagny**: *"But I don't want to be patient! I want my dress right now! Father promised!"*
**Frothar**: *"All you ever do is complain about what you want. You're a spoiled baby."*
**Dagny**: *"I'm going to tell father you said that. He'll tan your hide for sure!"*

## Notes

- One of Dagny's lines (*"Where is papa? I want to ride Karinda now!"*) indicates that Dagny was supposed to have a pet horse named [Karinda](/wiki/Skyrim:Karinda "Skyrim:Karinda"), but it does not appear in game.
- If Whiterun is conquered by the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"), then Dagny's father will move to the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") but she will not. Also, her dialogue will not change.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, addresses this issue. She will move to the Blue Palace.

Dagur

**Dagur** is the [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") innkeeper of [The Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth") in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). [Haran](/wiki/Skyrim:Haran "Skyrim:Haran") is his wife, and together they have a daughter, [Eirid](/wiki/Skyrim:Eirid "Skyrim:Eirid"). While Haran feels less compelled to dig into [Ranmir's](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir") past, Dagur would like to see the drunk get back on his feet, and for someone to find out what happened to Ranmir's former [lover](/wiki/Skyrim:Isabelle_Rolaine "Skyrim:Isabelle Rolaine").

He wears the standard barkeeper's [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0005B6A1 "Skyrim:Clothing") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#00018801 "Skyrim:Clothing"). He wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and carries a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Drowned Sorrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Drowned_Sorrows "Skyrim:Drowned Sorrows")**: Find [Isabelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Isabelle_Rolaine "Skyrim:Isabelle Rolaine"), [Ranmir's](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir") lost love.

## Dialogue

His greetings:

:   *"Let me know if you need anything. We're here to provide."*
:   *"If there's anything you need, just let me know."*
:   *"If you've business with the College, you're welcome to stay here. It's where most of our business comes from, in fact."*
:   *"Unlike some folks here in town, we have nothing against the College or the people that come and go."*
:   *"Don't worry about Nelacar. He has a permanent room here at the Inn, but he keeps to himself and doesn't cause any trouble."*

If the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") take Winterhold he gets new greetings:

:   *"Turns out who runs Winterhold doesn't change much. Can't say I'm surprised."*
:   *"I won't complain about Korir being gone, but I don't expect things to really be any different."*

When spoken to:

:   **What can you tell me about Winterhold?**
:   *"I'm afraid there's not much to be said. Winterhold is hardly what it used to be. You can talk to [Birna](/wiki/Skyrim:Birna "Skyrim:Birna") if you need to buy anything. She doesn't have much, but could certainly use the coin. And then there's our little inn. Most of the business we get is from folks here to visit the College, though even that's dried up some."*

:   **I overheard something about a College.**
:   *"That's right. College of Winterhold, just north of town. Hard to miss."*

### Containment

When the town is [under siege](/wiki/Skyrim:Containment "Skyrim:Containment"), he says:

:   *"What's going on out there? What happened?"*

### The Black Star

When asked about an elven mage who studies stars, during [The Black Star](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star "Skyrim:The Black Star"):

:   **Is there an elven mage here that studies stars?**
:   *"The mages are up in the College. You can ask them, if they'll let you in. Then again, Nelacar might know. He's an old-timer from the College, but he has a room here."*

### Drowned Sorrows

:   **Anything around here that needs doing?**
:   *"Well, not exactly. Listen, we're friends, right? I wondered if I could ask a favor of you."*

:   :   **Sorry, not interested.**
    :   *"Ah. Well, some other time, perhaps."*

:   :   **What can I do for you?**
    :   *"It's about Ranmir. Don't get me wrong, I don't have a problem with him being here all the time. He mostly keeps to himself, and so far he's been able to pay. I just hate to see what's happened to him. He hasn't always been like this, you know. Drunk, I mean."*

Offering to help will lead to:

:   **What did he used to be like?**
:   *"Oh, he was a different person. Happy, outgoing... Like anyone who's in love."*

:   **What's this got to do with me?**
:   *"Well, I'm getting to that. Just let me explain."*

:   **So what happened to him?**
:   *"See, Ranmir was involved with a pretty young woman named Isabelle Rolaine. The two of them were very happy together, I thought. One day, she just disappeared. Ranmir was convinced she'd run off with someone else, leaving him behind. He turned to drinking, and what's left of him is what you see here every day."*
:   **What can be done about it now?**
:   *"I'm not sure. I hoped that maybe if she could be found, if he had some sort of explanation, that maybe he could put himself back together. I'm in no position to go searching for her, but perhaps you could."*

## Conversations

When you first enter The Frozen Hearth, he can be seen having a conversation with [Nelacar](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelacar "Skyrim:Nelacar"):

:   **Nelacar**: *"I'm sorry, could you describe the smell?"*
:   **Dagur**: *"Like some horrible monster was turned inside out, then exploded. What did you do?"*
:   **Nelacar**: *"It was a minor miscalculation. I've already corrected it for future experiments."*
:   **Dagur**: *"This, this is why people have a problem with your college, Nelacar."*

Dagur will often converse with customers and family around the inn:

:   **Dagur**: *"I understand Korir has been complaining about our customers again."*
:   **Haran**: *"What of it? It's our inn, and they cause him no harm."*
:   **Dagur**: *"I believe he was suggesting their presence causes him harm."*
:   **Haran**: *"Well, then he's welcome to eat and drink at home, isn't he?"*

:   **Haran**: *"I understand Eirid's been playing 'Hunt the Elf' again."*
:   **Dagur**: *"It's just children playing, Haran. I wouldn't fret over it."*
:   **Haran**: *"I'm not 'fretting.' I don't want Eirid playing those sorts of games!"*
:   **Dagur**: *"All right, all right. I'll speak to her."*

:   **Dagur**: *"Are we running low on mead?"*
:   **Haran**: *"No. Even Ranmir can only drink so much."* or *"No, without Ranmir around we're running out of stock far less often than we used to."*
:   **Dagur**: *"Let's just keep an eye on the supply. It's such a chore to restock."*
:   **Haran**: *"I suppose that's a benefit to having so few customers."*

:   **Dagur**: *"Is everything well, Nelacar?"*
:   **Nelacar**: *"Oh yes, quite fine. My accommodations here continue to be just what I need."*
:   **Dagur**: *"There hasn't been any... problems?"*
:   **Nelacar**: *"Are you referring to your other customers? No, everything is quite alright. I expect a little animosity now and then."*
:   **Dagur**: *"I see. Well, let me know if things get out of hand"*

:   **Nelacar**: *"I say, you didn't hear any loud noises last night? No, ahh... explosion sounds?"*
:   **Dagur**: *"No, I certainly didn't! Is there any reason you're asking me?"*
:   **Nelacar**: *"No, certainly not. A small experiment may have gone awry, but clearly with no discernible consequences."*
:   **Dagur**: *"I... see. And is this something I need to worry about in the future?"*
:   **Nelacar**: *"Oh, I certainly hope not! That would be quite unfortunate for my research."*

# Skyrim:Daighre's House

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Daighre's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Daighre%27s+House)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| LeftHandMineDaighresHouse | |
| Region | |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | |
| Location | |
| Southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | |

Daighre's House

**Daighre's House** is the home of [Daighre](/wiki/Skyrim:Daighre "Skyrim:Daighre"), next door to [Skaggi's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaggi%27s_House "Skyrim:Skaggi's House"), near the [Left Hand Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Mine "Skyrim:Left Hand Mine").

It is the first house on the left after crossing the bridge leading to the entrance to the Left Hand mine. It contains only one interior zone, *[Daighre's House](#Daighre.27s_House)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Daighre](/wiki/Skyrim:Daighre "Skyrim:Daighre")  [Erith](/wiki/Skyrim:Erith "Skyrim:Erith")  [Torom](/wiki/Skyrim:Torom "Skyrim:Torom") ([dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog")) |

## Walkthrough

Inside Daighre's house

### Exterior

It is a single story Dwemer dwelling in a small settlement, where the miners from the [Left Hand Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Mine "Skyrim:Left Hand Mine") live. The entrance is frequently left unlocked. The [miner's barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Miner%27s_Barracks "Skyrim:Left Hand Miner's Barracks") are directly opposite. There is a [juniper tree](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") growing on the roof.

### Daighre's House

Inside it is a single roomed house with a large fireplace in the middle of the north wall with a pot hanging in front of it containing a [grilled chicken breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Chicken_Breast "Skyrim:Grilled Chicken Breast") and a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"). To the left of the fireplace is an unlocked non-respawning [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing leveled items, with a basket on the floor containing two [gourds](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") and [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel on either side of it. Coming out from the west wall is a long wooden table with a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a grilled chicken breast and a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") in a cast iron pot on top of the table. On a ledge on the west wall is a [deer hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Hide "Skyrim:Deer Hide"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a loaf of bread and a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"). Against the south wall is a dresser with a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") on top and containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"). At the other end of the room there are two single owned beds, [Daighre](/wiki/Skyrim:Daighre "Skyrim:Daighre")'s is along the north wall and [Erith](/wiki/Skyrim:Erith "Skyrim:Erith")'s is along the east wall. There is a ledge along the east wall with a copy of *[Horker Attacks](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Attacks "Skyrim:Horker Attacks")* and a couple of food sacks on top, with a rack hanging from the ceiling above holding a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"). There is a food barrel in the southeastern corner with a crate and sack to the right. On the crate is a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips").

## Notes

- Aside from most barrels and sacks, all containers in the house are [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") and safe to store items in.

Daighre

**Daighre** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [miner](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner_(class) "Skyrim:Miner (class)") living in [Left Hand Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Mine "Skyrim:Left Hand Mine"), just outside [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). She is the mother of [Erith](/wiki/Skyrim:Erith "Skyrim:Erith").

Daighre wears a set of [miner's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_Clothes#00080697 "Skyrim:Miner's Clothes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#00080699 "Skyrim:Boots"). Like most miners, she is equipped with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), and carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Daighre%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Daighre's House") to [her house](/wiki/Skyrim:Daighre%27s_House "Skyrim:Daighre's House"), as well as a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine_(quest) "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine (quest)")**: Clear the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") from [Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine").

### Kolskeggr Mine

When the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") attack her friends she will feel very sorry for them and during the quest will remark:

:   *"Poor [Pavo](/wiki/Skyrim:Pavo_Attius "Skyrim:Pavo Attius") and [Gat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gat_gro-Shargakh "Skyrim:Gat gro-Shargakh"). To have lived through a Forsworn attack."*
:   *"Another day, another settlement gets attacked. No place in the [Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") is safe from the Forsworn."*

## Dialogue

When approached she can say:

:   *"I'm the hardest worker in Left Hand. Better than any man."*
:   *"Most women would rather die than dig, but I have a daughter to raise."*
:   *"My Erith has her father's eyes. She's all I have left of him."*

## Conversations

She may randomly have conversations with her daughter or her boss, [Skaggi Scar-Face](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaggi_Scar-Face "Skyrim:Skaggi Scar-Face"):

*"I'm sorry my daughter gives you so much trouble."*

:   **Daighre**: *"Skaggi tells me that you were bothering him today. Can't you and [Torom](/wiki/Skyrim:Torom "Skyrim:Torom") just play by yourselves?"*
:   **Erith**: *"But mom, it's so boring with just me and Torom. I was just asking Skaggi some questions."*
:   **Daighre**: *"You leave him alone. I don't want to hear Skaggi telling me you've been bothering him again!"*
:   **Erith**: *"Yes, ma'am."*

:   **Erith**: *"Mama, can we talk. You know, about papa?"*
:   **Daighre**: *"Of course, sweetie. What'd you like to know?"*
:   **Erith**: *"I don't know. What'd he look like?"*
:   **Daighre**: *"He had your soft face, and that silly grin you get when you've done something wrong. That's his, too."*

:   **Skaggi**: *"You work hard, Daighre. Glad you have stayed with us."*
:   **Daighre**: *"I'm grateful, Skaggi. I'm sorry my daughter gives you so much trouble."*

:   **Daighre**: *"Do you think the Forsworn will come here? I mean, if they attacked [Kolskeggr](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine")...."*
:   **Skaggi**: *"Let's just hope that doesn't happen."*

# Skyrim:Dainty Sload

## Overview

This article is about the ship. For the quest, see [The Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:The Dainty Sload").

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Shipwreck.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Shipwreck.png) | Ship: Dainty Sload ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dainty+Sload)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |

| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DaintySloadExterior01, DaintySloadExterior02, DaintySload01 | |

| North of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude")  Southwest of [Solitude Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Solitude Lighthouse") | |

The Dainty Sload

The **Dainty Sload** is a [ship](/wiki/Skyrim:Shipwrecks "Skyrim:Shipwrecks") docked north of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").

The ship is currently docked for supplies. It has one interior zone: the *[Dainty Sload](#Dainty_Sload)*.

## Related Quests

- **[The Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:The Dainty Sload")**: Frame a ship's captain to get revenge for a [jilted merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur").
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.

### Exterior

Sload figurehead

The Dainty Sload's topside deck is guarded by two [corsairs](/wiki/Skyrim:Corsair "Skyrim:Corsair"): one sits or stands looking out to sea, while another roams the deck. If you wish to avoid them, wait until the roaming corsair disappears behind the cabin and slip through the unlocked door. There are numerous sacks and barrels on-deck containing a mixture of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). You can also find a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") and to the right of the entrance to the cabin there are two bottles of [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") on top of a crate. Against the port-side railing are two open crates; one contains five [giant lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen") and the other several [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). On shore by the start of the jetty is a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") bush and two patches of [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Grass Pod").

### Dainty Sload

One of the corsairs

If your [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") skill is fairly high, then it is a quite easy to slip past all of the corsairs that wait below-decks. To the right of the entrance is a rare [fur helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Helmet "Skyrim:Fur Helmet") and set of [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor") on a sideboard and crate. Next to this is a cupboard with a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"), a woodcutter's axe and [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace") on the shelves, and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). Turning around at the bottom of the stairs, you will find a kitchen of sorts on the left with quite a few items of food in barrels and open crates. One of the open crates contains a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") and a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), while the other contains [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and cheese. There is a table and chairs where two corsairs sit. Behind them is a cupboard with an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") on the shelf and a sideboard beside the table with a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a common [book](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") on top. Following the linear passage, there is an open door with a random [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") on the floor to the left. Through the door and past another table with bread, cheese, and a [tomato](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato") on top, and behind among a stack of crates is a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute"). You will come to a room on the left with a sleeping corsair inside who will wake shortly after the door is opened. In this room is an unowned single bed, an end table with a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") on top and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") beside it, and a sideboard with three bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a gourd, a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") and a single loose [septim](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on top. Past this room is a set of shelves holding several small mead barrels, two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine").

Following the passage to the waterlogged bowels of the ship brings you to the last corsair on board. Under the stairs just descended is an unlocked chest, and to the right of the room are two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid") and a bunch of [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam"). Opposite these, on top of a barrel is a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"). Through the door at the far end is a set of shelves straight ahead, holding a [draught of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength"), a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), two bunches of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), and a common book. To the left is an adept-locked chest. On top of the end table in the corner to the right is another fur helmet and [fur shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Shoes "Skyrim:Fur Shoes").

The First Mate onboard

Follow the passage all the way to the end to face the [first mate](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Mate "Skyrim:First Mate"), who will be found sitting at a table facing away from you. On the table is an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem"), a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"), a bottle of alto wine, two [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle"), a deathbell flower, three copies of *[The Firmament](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Firmament "Skyrim:The Firmament")*, a plate of [horker loaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Loaf "Skyrim:Horker Loaf") and a [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), a loaf of bread and a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Dance in Fire, v6](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v6 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v6")*. Just before the first mate, there is another unowned bed on the right and end table opposite with a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") on top and a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots") beside the bed. The captain's chest can be unlocked with the [Dainty Sload footlocker key](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload_Footlocker_Key "Skyrim:Dainty Sload Footlocker Key"), which is carried by the first mate. Backtrack to the captain's chest. If you are here during the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:The Dainty Sload") the captain's chest is where you need to place the [Balmora Blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Balmora_Blue "Skyrim:Balmora Blue"). Beside this a cupboard with [fur bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Bracers "Skyrim:Fur Bracers"), a food sack, a deathbell flower, a basket containing a bunch of tundra cotton, five common books, and an empty [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") on the shelves, with another pair of fur shoes on the floor beside it. Continue backtracking to a dining table laid with fine crockery, holding two [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steaks, three [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), two bottles of alto wine, a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), bread and cheese, a bunch of tundra cotton and a potion of regeneration.

## Notes

- On the other side of the rocks by the plants is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein").
- During the quest, you can kill everyone on the ship, including the First Mate, with no repercussions at all.
- If the corsairs and the First Mate have been killed prior to the quest [The Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:The Dainty Sload"), the ship will fully reset, giving you a chance to double your loot.
- The Balmora Blue that you need to plant in the Captain's Chest during the quest The Dainty Sload is never removed from the chest after planting it there. The Balmora Blue also loses its quest item status afterwards, allowing you to take it back out of the Captain's Chest.
- During [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity"), anyone who escapes the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy") with you will eventually end up close to the ship and disappear if not killed in a hostile random encounter. Their deaths can also be avoided by fast-traveling once you are outside Reeking Cave.
- The corsairs may carry [scimitars](/wiki/Skyrim:Scimitar "Skyrim:Scimitar"), which are otherwise quite difficult to find.

# Skyrim:Dalan Merchad

## Overview

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionWinterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionWinterhold "Skyrim:CrimeFactionWinterhold"); [ShipsNorthwindFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:ShipsNorthwindFaction "Skyrim:ShipsNorthwindFaction") | | |

Dalan Merchad

**Dalan Merchad** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") who works at the [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") docks. He serves as a sailor aboard the ship [The North Wind](/wiki/Skyrim:The_North_Wind "Skyrim:The North Wind"), under the ship's captain, [Kjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjar "Skyrim:Kjar").

He despises Windhelm and with the ship permanently docked, Dalan has no choice but to wander around on deck all day and night, without getting any sleep, at times pausing to sit down and eat.

Dalan wears merchant [clothing](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0004223C "Skyrim:Clothing") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0004223d "Skyrim:Boots"). He wields an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") in combat, and carries a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

When approached:

:   *"Never much cared for Windhelm. The place is depressing."*
:   *"I'm a lot happier out here on the deck than I am wandering around in that ruin of a city."*
:   *"I heard those [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") out west live in caves. Can't be any worse than trying to live in Windhelm."*
:   *"Can't wait until we raise anchor. Anytime the boat's not moving, I start to get impatient."*

## Bugs

- Dalan is in the Winterhold crime faction, rather than the Eastmarch one.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.
