# Skyrim:Dampened Spirits

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Put [Maven Black-Briar's](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar") competition out of business.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf") |
| Location(s): | [The Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(place) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (place)"), [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare"), [Honningbrew Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Meadery "Skyrim:Honningbrew Meadery") |
| Reward: | Enchanted leveled one-handed weapon; [Mallus Maccius](/wiki/Skyrim:Mallus_Maccius "Skyrim:Mallus Maccius") becomes available as a [fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Fences "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") |
| ID: | TG03 |
| Suggested Level: | 8 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Loud and Clear](/wiki/Skyrim:Loud_and_Clear "Skyrim:Loud and Clear") | **Next →** [Scoundrel's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Scoundrel%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Scoundrel's Folly") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Loud and Clear](/wiki/Skyrim:Loud_and_Clear "Skyrim:Loud and Clear") | | → Next | [Scoundrel's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Scoundrel%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Scoundrel's Folly") | | |

The vat containing Sabjorn's new mead

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar").
2. Meet [Mallus Maccius](/wiki/Skyrim:Mallus_Maccius "Skyrim:Mallus Maccius") at [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare").
3. Speak to [Sabjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabjorn "Skyrim:Sabjorn") in the [Honningbrew Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Meadery "Skyrim:Honningbrew Meadery").
4. Engage in some industrial sabotage and witness the mead tasting failure.
5. Acquire the promissory note and return to Maven.

### Preparation

As you will be battling [Ataxia](/wiki/Skyrim:Ataxia "Skyrim:Ataxia")-bearing skeevers, [resist disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Disease "Skyrim:Resist Disease") or [cure disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Cure Disease") [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") or [enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchantments "Skyrim:Enchantments") are useful. Furthermore, given the vermin's speed, a fast, light melee weapon is advised. Given [Hamelyn](/wiki/Skyrim:Hamelyn "Skyrim:Hamelyn")'s magical ability, resist [magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Magic "Skyrim:Resist Magic"), [shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Shock "Skyrim:Resist Shock"), [fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Resist Fire"), and [frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Frost "Skyrim:Resist Frost") spells or enchantments are useful.

### Black-Briar Business

Now that you're a full member of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), you've been told that [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar") wants to see you. You are likely to find her on the second floor of [The Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb"). After a condescending greeting, Maven will solicit your cooperation in putting her competitor, the [Honningbrew Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Meadery "Skyrim:Honningbrew Meadery"), out of business. She will also ask you to perform some industrial espionage to understand how Honningbrew could have started up their operation and achieved success so quickly. She will direct you to meet [Mallus Maccius](/wiki/Skyrim:Mallus_Maccius "Skyrim:Mallus Maccius") at [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") for further instructions.

### Meet Mallus Maccius

Mallus will tell you that [Sabjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabjorn "Skyrim:Sabjorn"), Honningbrew's owner, is planning to hold a special tasting for an important personage, and that you must poison the mead for the occasion. He suggests that you approach Sabjorn and offer to help him with a pest infestation, then use the poison he will give you to accomplish the deed. He instructs you to access the mead vats through a tunnel leading there from the meadery's basement. Although he claims you could alternatively pick the lock on the brewery door, you can't, as it requires a key which is only found inside the boilery. His own motives are quite simple: he'll be given control of the meadery from Maven once Sabjorn is out of the way.

### Infestation Elimination

Sabjorn will quickly accept your offer to help and provide you with the required poison as well as the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Meadery_Key "Skyrim:Honningbrew Meadery Key") to the Meadery. If you successfully [persuade](/wiki/Skyrim:Persuade "Skyrim:Persuade") him, he'll even give you half your pay upfront (500 gold) - although the way things turn out, this is all you'll get from him.

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| That's the only way I operate. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: Oh, very well. Here's half. You get the rest when the job's done. **Failed**: Well that's not how I operate, so forget it. | | | | **Passed**: Get 500 gold **Failed**: Nothing |
| You'd better, or I yell "skeever." **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: Okay, okay. No need to make rash decisions. Here's half. You get the rest when the job's done. **Failed**: Yell all you want. It's not going to change my mind. | | | | **Passed**: Get 500 gold **Failed**: Nothing |
| Just pay me when the job's done. | My only demand is that these vermin are permanently eliminated before my reputation is completely destroyed. | | | | Nothing |

Sabjorn will also, if asked, talk about how he gets free labor from Maccius by trapping him into a debt he can't afford to repay. In the basement, you'll easily find the tunnel Maccius pointed as the infestation's source. Fight your way past the tough Venomfang [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") as well as a few [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), taking care to avoid bear traps and tripwire-activated swinging maces along the way.

You'll emerge in a large chamber where a mad [bandit wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Wizard "Skyrim:Bandit Wizard") named Hamelyn is guarded by several vermin. Try to use sneak to avoid fighting them all the same time, as Hamelyn can cast powerful destruction spells and is especially lethal if he catches you in a weakened condition. Poison the skeever nest next to Hamelyn's alchemy lab and don't miss the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Three Thieves](/wiki/Skyrim:Three_Thieves "Skyrim:Three Thieves")* lying atop a chest nearby. Press on, avoiding two bear traps, and you'll arrive at the door leading to [the boilery](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Boilery "Skyrim:Honningbrew Boilery").

### Mellow Mead

Head up the stairs to a balcony overlooking the room and head towards the lone brewing vat on the far side. Poison it and exit using the [Honningbrew Brewhouse key](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Brewhouse_Key "Skyrim:Honningbrew Brewhouse Key") hanging on a hook on the right side of the door. Head back inside the meadery and you'll meet either [Commander Caius](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Caius "Skyrim:Commander Caius") or [Sinmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinmir "Skyrim:Sinmir") (if the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") have taken Whiterun) tasting the mead - Sabjorn will not pay you what he owes you yet (citing the need to go through with the mead tasting first), so if you got your 500 gold earlier, that's as good as it gets. The taster will sense something wrong with the drink and blame it on poor sanitary conditions. For this perceived offense, he will place Mallus Maccius in charge of the meadery and haul Sabjorn to jail at swordpoint - so you never DO get the rest of the pay (or any of it, if you didn't talk him into giving half in advance).

Once Sabjorn has departed, speak to Mallus about gathering business intelligence for Maven and he'll hand over the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabjorn%27s_Dresser_Key "Skyrim:Sabjorn's Dresser Key") to Sabjorn's dresser. Head upstairs and steal the [promissory note](/wiki/Skyrim:Promissory_Note "Skyrim:Promissory Note") from the dresser. An expert-locked door nearby will open to reveal a room with some silver ingots, a silver necklace, some coin purses, and the [Honningbrew Decanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Decanter "Skyrim:Honningbrew Decanter"), a miscellaneous unique item that can be sold to [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") for a fair price. Be sure to read the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") skill book *[A Game at Dinner](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Game_at_Dinner "Skyrim:A Game at Dinner")*, which is found on the table closest to the door.

### Mysterious Missive

Head back to the Bee and Barb in Riften and report your success to Maven, who is frustrated by her inability to identify the note's author. When you point out the author's symbol is the same as that on the [bill of sale](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Bill_of_Sale_(safe) "Skyrim:Goldenglow Bill of Sale (safe)") previously found in the Goldenglow Estate safe she suggests taking it to [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf"). Provided you didn't kill anyone but Hamelyn, she will then pay you with a leveled enchanted sword or dagger. Once you're back in the Cistern, Brynjolf will muse that the identical symbol points to someone attempting to drive a wedge between Maven and the guild, and will send you off to Mercer to continue your search. Mallus will now also be available as a [fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence_(merchant) "Skyrim:Fence (merchant)").

## Notes

- If you report back to Sabjorn while having a [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime") of at least 1000 gold in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), the captain of the guard will try to arrest you on sight. Remaining out of sight and talking to Sabjorn is virtually impossible, so it's advised to bring the captain to his knees and quickly talk to Sabjorn, then remain undetected until the winetasting scene starts. It is then recommended to stay hidden until the captain leaves with Sabjorn. Alternatively, just pay off your bounty before you head back to the Meadery.
- If you sneak past Hamelyn and don't kill him, Mallus will still talk as if you have killed him. Even if you return to Honningbrew Meadery Basement, after the quest is over, Hamelyn will be there.
- Despite Mallus suggesting it as an alternate point of entry, you can't enter the brewhouse until after you make your way through the tunnels for the first time. The front door is unpickable and can only be unlocked using the key that you find inside the boilery.
- Right after the persuasion check, you can exit out of the conversation, allowing you to restart the conversation and it offers a chance to repeat the check indefinitely and train [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech").

## Bugs

- If you break into [Honningbrew Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Meadery "Skyrim:Honningbrew Meadery") before receiving this quest, it will not become available at the end of [Loud and Clear](/wiki/Skyrim:Loud_and_Clear "Skyrim:Loud and Clear").
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, addresses this issue. However, if this bug has already been triggered on a prior version to 1.4, then the quest will remain unavailable on that save file even with the patch installed.
  -  If you cannot obtain the quest, you can force it to start using the console with `startquest TG03`, followed by `setstage TG03 10`.
- If you approach the nest in the first person view, the "activate nest" button needed to poison the nest may fail to appear.
  - Changing to the third person view can sometimes resolve this.
  -  You can also advance this manually using the console command `setstage TG03 45`.
- After completing the quest [Loud and Clear](/wiki/Skyrim:Loud_and_Clear "Skyrim:Loud and Clear"), if you do not ask Brynjolf why Maven Black-Briar is requesting a meeting, the quest will not become available. Also Brynjolf will not speak to you, saying only that he has "important tasks to be doing".
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
  -  If you cannot obtain the quest, you can force it to start using the console with `startquest TG03`, followed by `setstage TG03 10`.
- If speaking to Maven outside of the Bee and Barb, while she is headed to the inn, she will simply stand in the same spot day and night until the quest is over.
- Eimar has some lines at the Bannered Mare that don't make sense for him to use while he's there. One wasn't conditioned to the location he's in, and the other was using an incorrect function to check if this quest is finished or not.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.7, fixes this bug.
- If Whiterun Hold has a Stormcloak government at the time you do this quest, then [Sinmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinmir "Skyrim:Sinmir") is supposed to be present for the tasting rather than [Commander Caius](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Caius "Skyrim:Commander Caius"). However, there are multiple bugs that can interfere with this.
  - Activating this quest but not finishing it before activating [Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim") may cause Caius to be present for the tasting instead of Sinmir, where he will fail to drink the mead, causing the quest to stall.
    -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.
    -  You can also transport Sinmir to the Meadery using the console commands `prid 813ba` and `moveto player`.
    -  You can also skip this scene using the console command `setstage TG03 80`. This will progress the quest to where you have to talk to Mallus Maccius again.
  - Another variation of this bug can sometimes place Caius at the tasting even if the Stormcloaks have already gained Whiterun before you activate this quest. Fortunately, this variation does not prevent the quest from progressing as intended.
- If you successfully destroy three beehives and complete the Loud and Clear quest, but go back to Goldenglow Estate and destroy more beehives before you speak to Maven Black-Briar, Maven will speak to you as if you failed the earlier quest.
- After you finish the quest, the Honningbrew Mead barrels outside of the meadery may not be changed to Black-Briar Mead barrels.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, addresses this issue. Proper enable parents have been added to the existing barrels as well as the created replacement barrels. The barrels were also missing their ownership settings.

| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |

| 20 |  | Maven Black-Briar has sent me to Whiterun where I am to meet with someone named Mallus Maccius. Together, our goal is to bring down one of Maven's competitors, Honningbrew Meadery and discover where he obtained the financing to take her on. *Objective 20:* Speak to Mallus Maccius |
| 30 |  | I've become a key component in a cunning plan to frame Honningbrew Meadery's owner, Sabjorn, and have him imprisoned. The first part of the scheme is to approach Sabjorn under the guise of assistance with a pest problem he's having thanks to Mallus's tinkering. *Objective 30:* Speak to Sabjorn |
| 40 |  | Sabjorn has provided me with poison I'm to apply to the nests deep within the tunnels under Honningbrew Meadery. As Mallus predicted, I should be able to use the very same poison to taint Sabjorn's mead as well. *Objective 45:* Poison the Nest  *Objective 50:* Poison the Honningbrew Vat |

| 70 |  | *Objective 70:* Attend the tasting ceremony |

| 90 |  | Now that Mallus's position as the owner of Honningbrew Meadery has been secured, I need to find any information explaining how Sabjorn was able to fund this costly operation. *Objective 90:* Identify Sabjorn's silent partner |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Return to Maven Black-Briar |
| 110 |  | *Objective 110:* Return to Brynjolf |
| 200 | ☑ | The information I obtained from Honningbrew Meadery points to the same anonymous buyer of Goldenglow Estate. If successful, this individual would have completely estranged Maven Black-Briar from the Guild and destroyed it economically. It's becoming painfully obvious that it's time to shed some light on our mysterious adversary before they have a chance to strike again. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 45, 55.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TG03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TG03`.

Damphall Mine

**Damphall Mine** is a small [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") and [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") north of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") containing [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver"). It contains only one zone, *[Damphall Mine](#Damphall_Mine)*.

The mine also serves as a sanctuary for forest vegetation and alchemical ingredients that have long since disappeared from the surface of [Solstheim](/wiki/Lore:Solstheim "Lore:Solstheim") due to ashfall from [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain"), and there are hints that it was once a [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins").

## Related Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader")**: Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Ancient Technology](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Technology "Skyrim:Ancient Technology")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Retrieve Dwemer schematics to improve technology for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

A reaver stands guard outside the entrance to the mine, near a partially buried and burnt caravan wagon. There is a lit brazier on a stand to the left of the entrance.

### Damphall Mine

Upon entering, you are at the top of an earthen ramp leading down to the southeast. The tunnel is wide and lit by a lantern hanging from a support beam in front of you. As you follow the tunnel forwards, you will overhear two reavers talking. As the tunnel narrows, you will be able to see one of the reavers through a broken part of a wooden wall. You can snipe them through the gap with a [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"), which will cause the other to investigate and emerge into the tunnel where you are. As the tunnel bears to the south, there is a long wooden table on your right against the wall, with a basket underneath. The basket contains two pieces of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore"). On the table is a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), two large pieces of [charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal"), another piece of iron ore, and three bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"). There are two unusable barrels to the left of the table.

Farther along the same wall is an open crate containing a [deer pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Pelt "Skyrim:Deer Pelt") and two [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"). There is an opening into a large partially flooded room to the southeast with a lit brazier on a stand in front of you; to the left of the opening, on the east wall, is an iron ore vein. To your left, behind the wooden wall where the two reavers were talking, are three unusable barrels. On top of one of them is a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a random potion.

Glug!

Through the opening, the flooded cave has a floating dead reaver. Under the water, very deep down (an enchanted item of [waterbreathing](/wiki/Skyrim:Waterbreathing_(effect) "Skyrim:Waterbreathing (effect)") or an [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") character are highly recommended), are three more dead reavers. Scattered under the water are five lootable [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), an unlocked chest, two [clams](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam "Skyrim:Clam"), three [pearl oysters](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearl_Oyster "Skyrim:Pearl Oyster"), and a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"). To the southeast are two statues, one on either side of the wooden ramp leading out of the water to the next room; on the ramp is another Nordic barnacle and a pearl oyster. A waterfall cascades into a pit directly ahead, with a path around to the left and a low wooden railing between the path and the drop. You can see wooden ramps descending to the lower level on the other side of the room, as well as an opening to the southeast at eye level. Following the path around, you will pass an open crate containing two pieces of iron ore and a pickaxe, with a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") next to it.

What's for dinner?

There is a reaver sitting next to a fire through the opening. A second reaver to the right is quite difficult to see until you're close. Just to the left of the opening is a sack and a barrel. The opening leads to a kitchen area with a large firepit at the far end of the room. There are three sacks and an unusable mead barrel on your left, followed by a low set of shelves containing two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat"), a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a random common book, and a wooden bowl containing a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). Above this is a rack with a garlic braid and a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") hanging from it. On your right as you enter is a large set of shelves containing two sacks, a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a leveled [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"), a leveled [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing") potion, a random [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") potion, an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), a [slice of goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), and a bulb of garlic. To the left of this is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") with two [pearls](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearl "Skyrim:Pearl") on top.

Wooden ramps

Following the wooden ramp down, you'll pass a crate with a clam and a portion of [clam meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam_Meat "Skyrim:Clam Meat") on top, with a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") beside it. At the bottom of the second ramp is a tunnel heading southeast and a ramp down into the water to the northwest. With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") can be found here, and fish from [Underground](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity)#Biomes "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)") waters can be caught here. At the bottom of the latter ramp is a [Nordic barnacle](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle") cluster; there are two more under the water along with three more pearl oysters.

Following the path to the southeast, you'll enter a tunnel with shallow water and three [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiky_Grass "Skyrim:Spiky Grass") plants before the tunnel turns to the southwest. In the corner in front of you is a small ledge within jumping distance; there is an [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") growing up there. The tunnel is quite dark, and has vegetation along both sides. Just before you reach a patch of natural light coming from above, there is a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") that activates a [falling boulder](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") trap. You can avoid this by jumping onto a second ledge on the left. Among the vegetation on this ledge is a cast iron pot containing a bottle of ale and a wooden bowl on a wooden block containing a sample of [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota") and a [knife](/wiki/Skyrim:Knife_(weapon) "Skyrim:Knife (weapon)"). Just past these items is an unlit fire against the south wall.

Window dressing

Farther along, the tunnel opens into another area with a caged window in front of you, through which you can see an [oil lantern](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") and various treasures. To the right of the window is a large opening to the west. Through this opening, you may see a reaver wandering over a rock bridge and another [mining](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") at the back of the room, with some deep water to the left. Entering the opening and following the left wall around, you'll pass under some rocks and climb a ramp into the small room behind the window. The room features a long wooden table holding a [Dibella statue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dibella_Statue "Skyrim:Dibella Statue"), a [goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), a [candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlestick "Skyrim:Candlestick"), three [gold ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ingot "Skyrim:Gold Ingot"), a copy of *[Ahzidal's Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Descent "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Descent")*, a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), an unusable mead barrel, and a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") containing two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"). To the left of the table is a stack of five unusable barrels. On the wooden flooring are two Nordic barnacle clusters and a spiky grass plant. Hanging from a stone strut are two [hanging mosses](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss"). Behind a pillar to the east is an unlocked chest.

Under the water back in the main room, there are three clams surrounding a partially buried skeleton with its arm around an unlocked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"). Also under the water, there's another skeleton that can be looted, a sapphire, and two more clams. Under the bridge are three hanging mosses. On your right as you enter the main room is a lit lantern on the floor against the north wall; the path up to the rock bridge starts here. At the top of the earthen ramp, there is a silver ore vein on the north wall. Crossing the bridge, there is a lit lantern on the floor, with a flawless ruby nearby and an oil lantern overhead. On the other side of the bridge on your left is an open crate containing three iron daggers.

Front door

The tunnel narrows, with half of it at a slightly lower level. You can jump down and find a skeleton that can be looted for a few [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). At the top of a short rise, natural light beams down to the left. Also to the left is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"). In front of you is an old firepit, with two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") beside it. The path continues to the northwest, and is full of vegetation. As you go along, a total of nine [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") and two [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") are on the way, as well as a statue on your left with three [hanging mosses](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing on it, with another hanging moss growing from the ceiling opposite. You'll reach a tunnel blocked by a gate after this. It isn't locked, but there is a reaver standing directly behind it.

You call this home?

Through the gate is the main living area for the reavers. Two large tents are in front of you, with two reavers in front. One of the reavers is hammering at an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), while the other wanders in and out of the tent on the right. To the east at the back of the room is a large wooden scaffold structure with ramps leading up. There is a reaver patrolling up and down near the top. Sniping will cause two more reavers to investigate: a magic user will descend the ramps, while an archer looks down from a higher ledge. In the center of the room is an oil lantern hanging from the ceiling. On the left just past the gate is a hanging moss plant and a torch lighting part of the room.

To the left of the first large tent is a crate, a sack, and an unusable mead barrel. Inside the first tent is a bedroll on the left and a novice-locked chest directly ahead; to the right, a long wooden table holds a pickaxe, three random poisons, a large coin purse, a random healing potion, and a wooden plate with a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge") on it, while underneath the table is a deer pelt. In front of the tent is the anvil one of the reavers was using. Behind the first tent is a [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter"), with an open crate to the left containing two pieces of iron ore. In front of the second tent is an unlit firepit, with an open crate beside it containing two bulbs of garlic and a wooden bowl holding a sample of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), and a block of wood and a leg of goat beside that. Inside the second tent are three more bedrolls. To the right of the second tent are two food barrels, two sacks, and a crate, which is mostly under the ramp to the south.

Against the south wall is a lit brazier on a stand with a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") beside it. To the left of the tanning rack is a deer pelt on a crate, and to the left of this is a loose [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"). Farther to the left, a ramp leads up to the east to a small empty ledge. The next ramp heads up to the north. At the top is a large ledge with a lit brazier on a stand in front of you, two tents at the rear (one large and the other small), and a long wooden table by the front edge. Beside the brazier is a basket containing two sheaves of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), with a third sheaf behind the basket. On the table is a quiver of [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"), a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow"), and two small coin purses. To the left, between the table and the large tent, is a food barrel. Inside the large tent is a bedroll and a common book on the ground. In front of the tent is an open crate containing a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a metal bowl holding three eidar cheese wedges. The smaller tent contains a pile of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood"), including two loose pieces, and a crate. The ramp up is to its left.

Two more ramps take you up to the next level, with another ramp leading up to the east, and a second ramp leading down to the west. Following the path west, at the bottom of the ramp is a bucket on your left containing a piece of [corundum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore"). Continuing onward, you are on a natural bridge over the cavern far below. After a few paces it splits; staying to the right leads to the end of the cavern, and a grisly sight of a wooden block and the remains of a human. There is a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") and an open crate containing a flute and a copy of *[Song of The Askelde Men](/wiki/Skyrim:Song_of_the_Askelde_Men "Skyrim:Song of the Askelde Men")* next to the block. Behind and above these items is an unlocked chest. You can jump down to the other fork from here to save backtracking. The path continues against the southern wall toward the east. You will come to another junction, with another stone bridge climbing to your left, and a wooden ramp continuing to the east against the wall. Just past the ramp, there is an oil lantern hanging from the wall.

Climbing the bridge to the left as it recrosses the cavern below, at the top is a skeleton sitting in front of an archery target, with an iron arrow in its lap and a large coin purse and a satchel on the ground to the right. Numerous hanging moss plants grow from the ceiling around this cavern, but use caution when jumping for them, as the long drop will kill you should you fall to the bottom of the cavern. Return to the base of the bridge and take the ramp leading up to the east. At the top of the ramp, wooden planking joins with the ledge reached by going to the east up the ramp at the first junction.

On this ledge an archer reaver waits, unless you dealt with them from below. A large statue is flanked by a [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungus to the left and a [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") fungus to the right, with a sack and a barrel farther to the right beside a tunnel heading southeast. A few paces along the tunnel is a lit brazier on a stand, with a lootable skeleton behind it. The path turns here to the south and climbs sharply. At the top, you can turn either northwest to reach the skeleton, or east to climb further. At the top of this earthen ramp, there is yet another lit brazier on a stand in front of you, and a ledge to your right. The path continues up to the northwest.

Jumping on the ledge and following it up and around leads you to another ledge with an unlocked chest, where you can see a reaver below you; this reaver is around the corner and out of sight from below. Climbing the ramp heading northwest, halfway up a fly amanita is on your right. The ramp switches back to the east and continues up, with another lantern on the floor at the top. In front of you is the reaver you may have sniped from above, by a chain which opens a hidden door.

Know who your friends are

Opening the door reveals another room with several small waterfalls pouring down the opposite wall. A dead reaver is bent backwards on a [trap door](/wiki/Skyrim:Trap_Door "Skyrim:Trap Door") in the floor, with a lever to its right. You can hear two reavers talking, and if you move forward, you will see them off to the left slightly. The boss is partway up an earthen ramp, and the other reaver is leaning against a master-locked gate to the boss's left. To your right is a tunnel heading east; there is a third reaver in this tunnel.

Treasure room

The tunnel to the east is blocked after a few paces by a cave-in on some stairs leading up. Apart from the reaver, there is nothing of interest. To the right of the trap door is an open crate containing a bowl, two loaves of bread, a small coin purse, and two [garnets](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet"). Behind this is a crate with a goblet, a salt pile, an eidar cheese wedge, an empty [lesser soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem"), and two loose coins on top.

The reaver boss carries [a key](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Room_Key "Skyrim:Treasure Room Key"), which opens the master-locked gate leading to the treasure room. Between the ramp that the boss stood on and the trap door is an open crate containing a flute, an iron dagger, two [cups](/wiki/Skyrim:Cup "Skyrim:Cup"), and a leather strip. Beside this are two crates holding a red apple, an iron dagger, a sample of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), and three loose coins. Behind these is another open crate on a rock above the others, which contains a small coin purse, a leather strip, and a gold ingot.

Climbing to the top of the ramp the boss stood on and jumping to the south onto a small ledge, you can make your way along to find a hidden chest behind the second waterfall (there's a bottom row of four waterfalls, then two on the next level up; it's behind the second of these).

Inside the treasure room, there is a wooden table holding a leveled enchanted [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), two goblets, a garnet, an [emerald](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald "Skyrim:Emerald"), a [diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:Diamond "Skyrim:Diamond"), ten loose coins, and two pieces of [gold ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore "Skyrim:Gold Ore") in a metal bowl. There is also a random enchanted [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield") leaning against the table. The boss chest is to the right. The shortcut out is found by dropping through the trap door; you'll land in the deep water near the entrance.

## Notes

- North of the mine and southeast of the [Water Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Water_Stone "Skyrim:Water Stone") is an [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox") containing an [East Empire Pendant](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant").

## Bugs

- Follower NPCs will not jump down from the shortcut exit here due to the lack of navmesh jump markers.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.
  - Alternatively, either wait after jumping down from the shortcut exit, or make your way out manually. Your follower should rejoin you by then.

Danica Pure-Spring

**Danica Pure-Spring** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [priestess](/wiki/Skyrim:TrainerRestorationMaster "Skyrim:TrainerRestorationMaster") of [Kynareth](/wiki/Lore:Kynareth "Lore:Kynareth") living in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") where she tends to the sick and wounded inside the [Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth"). She is the master [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"), but will only offer training after you've completed her quest [The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature").

Recently, the legendary [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") tree was struck by lightning and faded away, and with the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") raging, Danica has been forced to neglect her duties as priestess, including tending to the tree. Before the quest, Danica spends her mornings, from 7am to 1pm, sitting on one of the benches underneath the tree, trying to find someone to help her make the tree bloom again. She then spends the rest of her day healing the [wounded soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Wounded_Soldier "Skyrim:Wounded Soldier") and [sickly farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Sickly_Farmer "Skyrim:Sickly Farmer") inside the temple, and continues all through the night, at times [conversing](#Conversations) with her assistant [Ahlam](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahlam "Skyrim:Ahlam"). During the quest, she patiently stays inside the temple until you return. This behavior continues after the quest is completed, due to a [bug](#Bugs).

She wears [hooded monk robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Monk_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Monk Robes") with [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000bacd7 "Skyrim:Clothing") and carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and a selection of [lower-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature")**: Restore the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") for Danica Pure-Spring.
- **[Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery")**: Deliver an item to an associate. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Dialogue

Her greetings:

:   *"Welcome, child."*
:   *"Hello, child of Kynareth.*" **(The Blessings of Nature is completed)**
:   *"Lately it seems I am more nurse than priestess, tending to those who have suffered, both in mind and body, from this terrible war."*
:   *"These are trying times for us all, I know. Many come to the Temple of Kynareth to pray, and I assist them as best I'm able."*

Topics:

:   **You're a priestess of Kynareth?**
:   *"Indeed. The temple here in the city is my charge. The goddess's divine blessings have no doubt helped make Whiterun a thriving and prosperous city. After all, it is she who brings rain to our crops and fair weather on the harvest days."*

:   **Has the Stormcloak uprising affected your duties?**
:   *"Somewhat, yes. At first it seemed a distant thing, heard only in the idle speech of guards and traders. When the wounded soldiers began to return from battle, I did what I could to help them. As more of the sick and injured came to the temple, my work as a healer became more important than my duties as a priestess. I wish only an end to the fighting, so that I can tend to the temple once more."*

Her goodbyes:

:   *"Grace of Kynareth be with you."*
:   *"May Kynareth's winds blow you to fortune."*
:   *"Travel great Skyrim, and Kynareth travels with you."*

### The Blessings of Nature

*"This is the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen")."*

With the Civil War raging, Danica has been forced to neglect one of her most sacred obligations to her goddess—tending the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") tree just outside the temple—because of the strain that the war is exerting on her primary obligation: caring for and comforting the sick and injured. As a result, the tree seems to have faded away and Danica needs a helping hand. She spends most of her time sitting underneath the tree, saying:

:   *"It's a shame, isn't it?"*
:   **What's so special about this tree?**
:   *"This is the Gildergreen. It was planted as a seedling in the early years of Whiterun. Disciples of [Kynareth](/wiki/Lore:Kynareth "Lore:Kynareth") could sense something holy in it, and traveled far to hear the winds of the goddess in its branches. They built the temple. Of course, not as many pilgrims these days."*

If she is not near the tree:

:   **I heard something happened to the tree at the temple.**
:   *"The Gildergreen, yes. It's a bit of an eyesore at the moment. More of a problem for the pilgrims than for me, but not many of them around anymore."*

If she is in the temple:

:   **Tell me about this temple.**
:   *"This is the Temple of Kynareth. The Gildergreen, outside, was planted as a seedling in the early years of Whiterun. Disciples of Kynareth could sense something holy in it, and traveled far to hear the winds of the goddess in its branches. Of course, not as many pilgrims these days."*

Regardless you can continue with:

:   **Why haven't the pilgrims been coming?**
:   *"A big dead tree isn't very inspiring if you're coming to worship the divine of wind and rains. Kynareth gives life, and we need a living tree to be her symbol."*

:   **What's so special about this tree?**
:   *"To the east of here is a hidden grove where the Eldergleam resides. It's the oldest living thing in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). Maybe all of [Tamriel](/wiki/Lore:Tamriel "Lore:Tamriel"). Our tree here in the city was grown from a cutting of that tree. You can still feel the glory of the mother tree through it. Even its name is an echo."*

Alternatively, if you never heard the rumor about the tree from [Hulda](/wiki/Skyrim:Hulda "Skyrim:Hulda"), she will provide even more background information:

:   **Tell me more about Eldergleam.**
:   *"It's an old tree. Very old. They say it was a seedling when the first men were arriving from [Atmora](/wiki/Lore:Atmora "Lore:Atmora"), thousands of years ago. The sap is precious. It can restore barren fields or bring life to rocks. I can use it to repair the Gildergreen, so we can worship properly again."*

Either will lead to:

:   **Is there any way to revive the tree?**
:   *"I've thought about that... Trees like this never really die. They only slumber. I think if we had some of the sap from the parent tree, we could wake up its child. But even if you could get to the Eldergleam, you couldn't tap it. Not with any normal metal."*

:   :   **Where is the tree?**
    :   *"If you want to help, you'll need something to cut into it first. You'll have to deal with the Hagravens. I've heard about a weapon they've made for sacrificing Spriggans. It's called "Nettlebane." The hags terrify me, or I would have gone after it myself."*

:   :   **What kind of weapon would work?**
    :   *"Eldergleam is older than metal, from a time before men or elves. To even affect it, you have to tap into the old magic. You'll have to deal with the Hagravens. I've heard about a weapon they've made for sacrificing Spriggans. It's called "Nettlebane." The hags terrify me, or I would have gone after it myself."*

Either leads to:

:   **I'll get Nettlebane for you.**
:   *"Your spirit is strong. Kynareth's winds will guide your path. It's held in a Hagraven nest called Orphan Rock."*

When you return from [Orphan Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan_Rock "Skyrim:Orphan Rock"), Danica has received a visit from a traveling pilgrim, namely [Maurice Jondrelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Maurice_Jondrelle "Skyrim:Maurice Jondrelle") who is understandably upset about the current state of the Gildergreen and now spends his time bothering the busy priestess:

*"I really don't have time to deal with you right now."*

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Maurice**: | *"What is it... what has happened to the Gildergreen? I have traveled long here to worship beneath its branches."* |
| **Danica**: | *"It was taken by a lightning strike. Wish I had time to deal with it, but it's hard enough with all these wounded from the war."* |
| **Maurice**: | *"Please, don't just let it stay like this. It's disgraceful."* |
| **Danica**: | *"I really don't have time to deal with you right now. Please just let me get back to my work."* |
| **Maurice**: | *"But this is supposed to be your work."* |

When she sees you, she will ask:

:   *"So, have you gotten Nettlebane back from those filthy Hagravens yet?"*
:   **I've found Nettlebane for you.**
:   *"Oh. I... well, I honestly didn't expect you to come back. Of course, I'm glad you did! Now... I don't really want to touch that thing, though. Do you think you could handle the next steps?"*
:   **What needs to be done?**
:   *"Eldergleam's sanctuary grove is to the east of here. You can use Nettlebane to retrieve some of its sap."*
:   **Why do we need Nettlebane?**
:   *"The hags are hateful of anything which grows from the earth. They made the weapon strong against the natural world. It's the only thing I've even heard of that could cut Eldergleam. Stick it in, give it a twist, and the stuff will just flow out."*

At the [Eldergleam Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Eldergleam_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Eldergleam Sanctuary") you have two possibilities; either extract the sap using Nettlebane or let Maurice Jondrelle create a sapling for you. She will be grateful if you've extracted the sap:

:   **I've got the sap.**
:   *"Wonderful. I'll use it to repair the tree. Thank you so much for all your help."*

The sapling, however, will render her exasperated:

:   **I've got a sapling.**
:   *"But... I can't run the Temple without the support of people who are inspired by the Gildergreen. How can this little tree bring new worshippers?"*

:   :   **That's not really my problem.**
    :   *"You're right. It's mine. I may not live to see this little one grow into a new Gildergreen, but I can be remembered as the woman who planted it. I thank you. And may Kynareth's soft rains fall before you."*

:   :   **Maurice said that renewal is more important than maintenance.**
    :   *"I... you're right of course. It can be hard to hear the winds of Kynareth when all you hear are the rabble in the temple. Death feeds new life. I'm sure that, in time, this little sapling will grow into a new Gildergreen that will tower over Whiterun. Thank you."*

All three options will end the quest and Danica will now be available as the master [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"). If you give Danica the sap, she will also treat you as a friend.

### Delivery

Danica also has an associate in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") named [Idgrod the Younger](/wiki/Skyrim:Idgrod_the_Younger "Skyrim:Idgrod the Younger"), the sister of troubled child [Joric](/wiki/Skyrim:Joric "Skyrim:Joric"). During the [Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery") quest, Idgrod will ask you to deliver a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Idgrod%27s_Note "Skyrim:Idgrod's Note") to Danica who has been treating Joric. When you hand the note to Danica:

:   **I have a delivery from Idgrod the Younger.**
:   *"Joric's sister? Poor child. Magic runs deep in that family's bloodline. It's not always a blessing. Thank you for this. Something for your trouble."*

## Conversations

Inside the [Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth"), Danica and fellow healer [Ahlam](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahlam "Skyrim:Ahlam") will often discuss Ahlam's useless husband [Nazeem](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazeem "Skyrim:Nazeem"). Danica always starts the conversation and chooses between a number of random statements and Ahlam will do the same, as seen in the table below:

| Speaker | Conversation |
| --- | --- |
| Danica | *"Something wrong, Ahlam?"* |
| *"Are you alright, Ahlam? You haven't seemed yourself today."* |
| *"What's wrong, dear friend? You seem... distracted today."* |
| Ahlam | *"Oh, it's Nazeem. He's been spending more and more time fawning over the Jarl. I swear, we're hardly ever home at the same time anymore."* |
| *"It's nothing, I just... It's Nazeem. How did we get to this point, Danica? Is there no love left between us?"* |
| *"Hmm? Oh, well... To be honest, I was just thinking of Nazeem. The gap between us seems to be widening. He is just so... self-absorbed."* |
| Danica | *"Now, now, my friend. You must look on the bright side. If soldiers storm the city, there's a good chance your husband may get killed."* |
| *"If you don't mind me saying so, Ahlam, your husband is a damn fool. Any moment spent thinking about him is a moment wasted."* |
| *"Ahlam, let's be honest. Your husband is an arrogant, domineering buffoon. These are the words you used to describe him to me... remember?"* |
| *"Oh dearest, who cares? So your husband is a lout. The work you do here, with me, is invaluable. The people of Whiterun know your true worth."* |
| Ahlam | *"But it's more than that. Nazeem is obsessed with this civil war, as is all of Skyrim. I swear, it will consume us all."* |
| *"Maybe Nazeem's obsession has merit. This civil war seems so big, so unceasing... I'm afraid, Danica. Afraid for us all."* |
| *"Ha! Well, when you put it like that, it certainly puts things into perspective. But enough wallowing. And thank you, Danica."* |
| *"Oh, you are terrible. You do know that, right? Ha ha ha ha ha."* |

She can also be seen talking to the patients, starting conversation by asking:

:   *"How are you feeling?"*
:   *"How do you feel?"*
:   *"Feeling any better?"*

She might ask the [wounded soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Wounded_Soldier "Skyrim:Wounded Soldier") specifically:

:   *"How is the pain? Any better?"*

And the [sickly farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Sickly_Farmer "Skyrim:Sickly Farmer"):

:   *"Has your fever cooled?"*

Afterwards she may say:

:   *"Patience. The body needs time to mend."*
:   *"More rest will do you good."*
:   *"Try to relax. You'll be well soon enough."*

She shares these lines with her fellow healers, [Ahlam](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahlam "Skyrim:Ahlam") and [Acolyte Jenssen](/wiki/Skyrim:Acolyte_Jenssen "Skyrim:Acolyte Jenssen").

## Notes

- Danica doesn't use any spells in combat, since she lacks a spell list.

## Bugs

- Danica was supposed to sleep inside the temple every night between midnight and 7am (8am after the Gildergreen is restored), but her bed is slightly further away than her sleeping package allows her to go. As a result, she keeps tending to the patients all through the night.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Dark Ancestor

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

Vighar in Bloodlet Throne

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Dengeir of Stuhn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn").
2. Travel to [Bloodlet Throne](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodlet_Throne "Skyrim:Bloodlet Throne").
3. Battle through and kill [Vighar](/wiki/Skyrim:Vighar "Skyrim:Vighar").
4. Return to Dengeir.

### A Dark Ancestry

After stealing [Lod](/wiki/Skyrim:Lod "Skyrim:Lod")'s [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Private_Letter "Skyrim:Private Letter") for [Dengeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn"), he'll trust you enough to handle an important matter. It is of great concern and embarrassment to him that his ancestor [Vighar](/wiki/Skyrim:Vighar "Skyrim:Vighar") is actually a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). For years he was magically bound within his grave, but the magic energies weakened and allowed him to escape. When asked, he will tell his family secret: *"You may have seen the open grave in our graveyard. Most of the townsfolk think it's the work of a corpse thief. The truth is less pleasant. It is...was, the grave of Vighar, my own ancestor, dead for centuries now. He is also a vampire. My family is entrusted with keeping him buried, but recently someone stole the wardstone, and Vighar escaped."* However, he is not interested in the stone, he just wants Vighar destroyed. *"No. It's too late for the wardstone. Vighar must be destroyed. If this gets out, my family will suffer great shame."* Dengeir has tracked him down to the vampire lair [Bloodlet Throne](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodlet_Throne "Skyrim:Bloodlet Throne") and wants you to head there and destroy him before anyone discovers his family's secret shame.

### Bloodlet Throne

Bloodlet Throne is a military fort hidden in the mountains southwest of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"). Travel to Helgen and leave through the east gate, taking the path leading southeast. Keep an eye on your map marker and make sure to take the right turns; never stray off the path, as it will lead directly to the fort. The exterior of the fort is unguarded, so climb the steps and enter.

Once inside, the sound of howling [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf") will meet you, along with a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Traps") triggering a [flame trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Traps") right in front of you. Enter [sneak mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") and proceed forward. Before long, you will encounter two leveled vampires; pick the fight and proceed down the stairs into a large chamber. Take the eastern path and fight another vampire, feasting on severed hands in the dining room. Follow the snowy tunnel to yet another huge chamber with big wooden structures and more vampires, along with the expected wolf. Climb the woodworks and use the [Arcane Enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") and, in the next tunnel, the [Alchemy Lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), then investigate the sleeping area for a bit of loot and a door leading to a room with the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Incident at Necrom](/wiki/Skyrim:Incident_at_Necrom "Skyrim:Incident at Necrom")* and a random enchanted dagger on the table. Proceed to the snowy tunnel leading south and cross the bridge leading to Vighar in the final chamber.

### The Next Act of the Show

The final chamber is obviously some kind of arena built to satisfy Vighar. As you approach, you will observe him seated on the ledge above, having a brief conversation with one of the other inhabitants:

**Vampire**: *"And who is this?"*
**Vighar**: *"It is no matter, this fool will be the next act of the show."*

With these words, Vighar will pull the handle by his side and cause several wolves to be released from their cells. He will coldly observe while you fight them. As soon as you manage to kill them, Vighar himself will jump down and attack, backed up by his companions. When all is said and done, locate the pull chain in the western alcove and head upstairs. Follow the path to a chest with some loot, then remove the door bar and gain access to the first huge chamber. Exit Bloodlet Throne and return to Dengeir for your reward.

## Notes

- Vighar is a very tough vampire, on par with [Master Vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Vampire "Skyrim:Master Vampire") or [Volkihar Master Vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Master_Vampire "Skyrim:Volkihar Master Vampire"). He will replace the normal end boss of the dungeon.
- This quest is not available if Dengeir is Jarl of Falkreath.
- If the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") add-on has been installed, Bloodlet Throne will have three hostile [gargoyle](/wiki/Skyrim:Gargoyle "Skyrim:Gargoyle") statues added and the wolves will be replaced with [death hounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Hound "Skyrim:Death Hound").
- If you couldn't complete [Some Light Theft](/wiki/Skyrim:Some_Light_Theft "Skyrim:Some Light Theft") (see Bugs section on the page), the dialogue option to start the quest will not be available. One solution is to raise Dengeir's [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"). Open the console, click on Dengeir and enter `setrelationshiprank player 1`.

## Bugs

- Dawnguard may only add the gargoyles and not change the wolves to death hounds.
- At times, even if the quest has been started, Vighar may not appear. Instead, the final boss of the dungeon is the random high-level vampire who is supposed to be there if the mission has not been triggered. This does not seem to prevent the successful conclusion of the quest, since Dengeir will act just like you had killed his ancestor and not notice the difference.

## Quest Stages

| Dark Ancestor (FreeformFalkreathQuest03) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Tell Dengeir that Vighar is dead |
| 200 | ☑ |  |
| Dark Ancestor (FreeformFalkreathQuest03B) | | |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Destroy the vampire Vighar |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table:
  - FreeformFalkreathQuest03: 0, 10.
  - FreeformFalkreathQuest03B: 0, 20.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformFalkreathQuest03 / FreeformFalkreathQuest03B stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformFalkreathQuest03 / FreeformFalkreathQuest03B`.

# Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Assassin

## Overview

This article is about the corpse in Hag's End. For the randomly encountered one, see [Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Assassin "Skyrim:Assassin").

| Dark Brotherhood Assassin (RefID: 0009D760) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Hag's End](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End "Skyrim:Hag's End") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0009D760 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0009D761 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 0 (**Dead**) | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 25 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 70 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") | | |
| Perks | [Extra Damage 1.5](/wiki/Skyrim:Extra_Damage_1.5 "Skyrim:Extra Damage 1.5") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | Any Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Very Aggressive |
| Voice Type | [MaleNord](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleNord "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleNord") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [BanditFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:BanditFaction "Skyrim:BanditFaction") | | |

The dead assassin

The **Dark Brotherhood Assassin** is a long-dead [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") found behind a sliding wall in a hidden alcove revealed by pulling a handle behind the throne, in the throne room of [Hag's End](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End "Skyrim:Hag's End"). [Olava the Feeble](/wiki/Skyrim:Olava_the_Feeble "Skyrim:Olava the Feeble") will have a vision of his final resting place if you earn a bonus during the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") quest [Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security"). He is clad in a complete set of unique [Ancient Shrouded Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Shrouded_Armor "Skyrim:Ancient Shrouded Armor").

## Related Quests

- **[Locate the Assassin of Old](/wiki/Skyrim:Locate_the_Assassin_of_Old "Skyrim:Locate the Assassin of Old")**: Find the Dark Brotherhood Assassin.

## Notes

- Despite being supposedly long-dead, the Assassin's remains show no signs of decay.
- It is possible to obtain the Ancient Shrouded Armor without [Olava's Token](/wiki/Skyrim:Olava%27s_Token "Skyrim:Olava's Token"). Take [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") with you into Hag's End and during the fight with the first set of witches, she will resurrect the body of the Dark Brotherhood Assassin, who will join you once you exit the cell. When he turns to ash, loot the ash pile for the entire set of Ancient Shrouded Armor.
- It is also possible to obtain the Ancient Shrouded Armor by using [The Ritual Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ritual_Stone "Skyrim:The Ritual Stone") power. Activating the power near the body will raise it; exiting the cell within two minutes (for example, exiting to the Deepwood Redoubt balcony) will cause the body to follow you outside. Once the power wears off, you can loot the body for the armor.
- Version 2.0.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") makes the Assassin's corpse immune to reanimation.

## Bugs

- Clearing out Hag's End and then starting Locate the Assassin of Old may cause the Assassin's corpse to disappear.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Initiate

## Overview

Two **Dark Brotherhood Initiates** will become available as [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") after finishing all [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") quests. They are found in the [Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary") after you complete [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!") and begin improvements for the Dawnstar Sanctuary from [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

One is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") female found in the main room with [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir"), usually cooking. The other is a Nord male found in the living quarters, often reading. Both initiates wear [Shrouded Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Armor "Skyrim:Shrouded Armor"), [Shrouded Gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Gloves "Skyrim:Shrouded Gloves"), [Shrouded Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Boots "Skyrim:Shrouded Boots"), and a [Shrouded Cowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Cowl "Skyrim:Shrouded Cowl"), and are equipped with an [Ebony Dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Dagger "Skyrim:Ebony Dagger"). Despite being assassins, the Initiates can only dual wield if they have at least one Forsworn sword or axe. Because they do not have default arrows, their inventories must be kept stocked with arrows in order to make ranged combat viable. Also contrary to their profession, they will still not effectively kill enemies without alerting/attacking other enemies in the room when ordered to attack.

The Dark Brotherhood Initiate is one of the few followers that will level with you past level 50. In addition, the Initiates are marked Essential and will not die. This makes the Initiate a good choice of follower at high levels.

They cannot be [recruited](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades") into the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades") and cannot be used as a [sacrifice](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Calling#The_Sacrifice "Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling") in [Boethiah's Calling](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Calling "Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling"). They also cannot be ordered to kill other Dark Brotherhood members (including the other initiate and [Shadowmere](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmere "Skyrim:Shadowmere")), but will do almost anything else.

Nazir will praise the duo for their devotion to the Dark Brotherhood: *"The new initiates are working out well. Eager, dedicated, and not afraid to get their hands wet."*

The male Initiate

The male Initiate is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Assassin "Skyrim:Assassin") who wears [Shrouded Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Armor "Skyrim:Shrouded Armor"), [Shrouded Gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Gloves "Skyrim:Shrouded Gloves"), [Shrouded Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Boots "Skyrim:Shrouded Boots"), and a [Shrouded Cowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Cowl "Skyrim:Shrouded Cowl"). He is always equipped with an [Ebony Dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Dagger "Skyrim:Ebony Dagger"), regardless of your level.

He will greet you with *"Yes, Listener?"*, *"I am yours to command."*, *"How may I serve you, my Listener?"*, *"Just say the word, master/mistress."*, or *"Ready when you need me, Listener."* You may order him to follow you with **"I command you to accompany me."** He will then respond with *"I am honored to be chosen."* or *"Lead on, Listener."* However, if asked to follow when you already have a human follower, he will decline to join you: *"But you already have a traveling companion. I fear I would just get in the way."*

When asked to do something, the Initiate will respond with *"Anything you need, Listener."*, *"Do you have any orders?"* or *"Just name it."* When consenting to a command, he will state, *"All right."* , *"I'm on it."*, or *"It shall be done."* After responding to a command, he will ask, *"That everything?"* or *"Still something you'd like me to do?"* If ordered to do an impossible task, he will apologize: *"Sorry, Listener. It can't be done."* When commanded to commit an offense against the Dark Brotherhood, he will deny your request: *"I won't do it. You ask too much."* If you cancel your command, he will state, *"Very well, Listener."* or *"All right."*

When told to wait, he will consent with *"Yes, Listener. I'll be here if you need me."* or *"Yes, Listener. I won't move unless you give the word."* When told to rejoin you, he will assent, *"Lead on, Listener."* If dismissed while in the Sanctuary with **"You're dismissed. Stay in the Sanctuary."**, he will affirm, *"Yes, Listener. I'll be here if you need me."* If released outside of the Sanctuary with **"You're dismissed. Return home."**, he will state, *"I will return to the Dawnstar Sanctuary immediately, Listener."*

If told **"I need to rearrange your equipment."**, he will simply consent with *"Of course."*

If you have broken the tenets of the Dark Brotherhood, he will state, *"With all due respect, Listener, you broke what few rules we seem to have. Nazir insists you talk to him and work this issue out."*

The female Initiate

The female Initiate is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Assassin "Skyrim:Assassin") who wears [Shrouded Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Armor "Skyrim:Shrouded Armor"), [Shrouded Gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Gloves "Skyrim:Shrouded Gloves"), [Shrouded Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Boots "Skyrim:Shrouded Boots"), and a [Shrouded Cowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Cowl "Skyrim:Shrouded Cowl"). She is always equipped with an [Ebony Dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Dagger "Skyrim:Ebony Dagger"), regardless of your level.

She will greet you with, *"Listener. It is an honor to stand before you."*, *"Yes, Listener? How may I serve you?"*, *"How may I serve you, my Listener?"*, *"I am yours, master/mistress."*, or *"Walk always in shadow, my Listener."* You may order her to follow you with **"I command you to accompany me."**, to which she will respond, *"I am yours, Listener."* However, if you already have a human companion, she will dither: *"Oh, well... You seem to already have assistance. Surely you mean to remain inconspicuous..."*

When asked to do something, she will ask, *"Of course, Listener. What is it?"* While conveying your order, she will state,*"Command me, my Listener."* Before executing your command, she will say, *"Of course. Right away."* or *"Right away."* After responding to a command, she will ask, *"Still something you'd like me to do?"* or *"Is that all?"* If ordered to do an impossible task, she will apologize with *"If only I could, Listener."* Despite her obvious devotion to you, when commanded to commit an offense against the Dark Brotherhood, she will balk: *"But Listener... Are you sure? I just can't bring myself to do it..."* If you cancel your command, she will say, *"As you will."* or *"As you wish, Listener."*

When told to wait, she will confirm, *"I'll remain in this location until ordered otherwise."* When told to rejoin you, she will say, *"Yes listener."* If dismissed while still in the sanctuary, you will tell her, **"You're dismissed. Stay in the Sanctuary."** She will then say, *"Of course. But if you need me, just give the order."* If you dismiss her outside of the sanctuary with **"You're dismissed. Return home."**, she will affirm, *"Yes, Listener. I'll return to the Dawnstar Sanctuary without delay."*

If told **"I need to rearrange your equipment."**, she will simply consent with *"Yes, Listener."*

If you have broken the tenets of the Dark Brotherhood, she will refuse to speak to you: *"I do apologize, Listener, but Nazir made it clear the initiates are not to speak with you until you first deal with him, and atone for your actions."*

## Notes

- Strangely, both of the initiates are marked to respawn if killed. However, due to being marked as Essential, they can never die and will never utilize this function.

## Bugs

- The Dark Brotherhood Initiates may follow the player too closely.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- If asked to wait somewhere, these followers never time out and return to the Dawnstar Sanctuary. This can be problematic because you'll be unable to pick up a new follower and may have forgotten where the Initiate follower was left behind.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- The inventories of these followers may reset, causing items they are carrying to be permanently lost.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.10, fixes this bug.

Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary

The **Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary** is an active [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") sanctuary west of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). It contains only one zone, *[Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](#Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary)*.

Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Marked for Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Marked_for_Death "Skyrim:Marked for Death") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").
The door is hidden beneath the road just west of Falkreath. The entrance will only be added to your map once you have completed the quest [With Friends Like These](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These "Skyrim:With Friends Like These"). Prior to this, the door will be present, but the location will not appear on your map, and the correct answer to the question required to open the door will be unavailable until you are taught it by [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") during "[With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...")" or by [Commander Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro") during "[Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!")".

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Arcturus](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcturus "Skyrim:Arcturus")†  [Arnbjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnbjorn "Skyrim:Arnbjorn")  [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid")  [Babette](/wiki/Skyrim:Babette "Skyrim:Babette") [Alchemist](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Alchemist")[Trainer (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Master)")[Alchemy (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Alchemy (Master)")  [Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero")  [Festus Krex](/wiki/Skyrim:Festus_Krex "Skyrim:Festus Krex")  [Gabriella](/wiki/Skyrim:Gabriella "Skyrim:Gabriella")  [Gaston Bellefort](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaston_Bellefort "Skyrim:Gaston Bellefort")‡ (dead)  [Lis](/wiki/Skyrim:Lis "Skyrim:Lis") (passive [frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"))  [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") [Trainer (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Master)")[Light Armor (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Light Armor (Master)")  [The Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother")  [Veezara](/wiki/Skyrim:Veezara "Skyrim:Veezara") |
