### Dark Brotherhood

- See [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood#Quests "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood").

### Thieves Guild

- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.

### Exterior

There is a black pool to the right of the door from which [Shadowmere](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmere "Skyrim:Shadowmere") emerges during [The Cure for Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cure_for_Madness "Skyrim:The Cure for Madness"). There are also several [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") plants around the area. To the northwest are two [iron ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"). Once accepted into the Dark Brotherhood, travel to Falkreath and approach the door. It will ask you "What is the music of life?" Answer with the password Astrid or Commander Maro taught you, "Silence, my brother". You will be welcomed to your new "home" and the door will open. Any incorrect answers result in the door stating "You are not worthy". You are able to keep answering without further penalty.

### Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary

Astrid's office

Upon entering there are Dark Brotherhood banners on either side of the passage, which leads down a short flight of stairs, around a corner into the first room. The first time you arrive, you will find Astrid leaning against the wall at the top of another flight of stairs to the north, with a doorway to the west.

There is a long stone table with a tactical map of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") on top. Anytime you enter, the map will be marked with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") stabbed into it showing the location of the current main Dark Brotherhood quest. There is also a copy of *[The Night Mother's Truth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Night_Mother%27s_Truth "Skyrim:The Night Mother's Truth")* on the table. Behind the table is a throne and small cupboard holding clutter. On the right, against the wall are a couple of sets of shelves and a cupboard holding some [ruined books](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book"), a copy of *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")*, one empty and one filled [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a copy of the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Sithis](/wiki/Skyrim:Sithis "Skyrim:Sithis")*, a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), and a full set of shrouded clothing including [shrouded robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Robes "Skyrim:Shrouded Robes"), a [shrouded hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Hood "Skyrim:Shrouded Hood"), [shrouded hand wraps](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Hand_Wraps "Skyrim:Shrouded Hand Wraps"), a [shrouded cowl maskless](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Cowl_Maskless "Skyrim:Shrouded Cowl Maskless"), and [shrouded shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Shoes "Skyrim:Shrouded Shoes"). Only the cowl is counted as [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"), the rest are clothes. There are also some crates, a barrel, and a couple of sacks of food.

The room to the west is Astrid and [Arnbjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnbjorn "Skyrim:Arnbjorn")'s bedroom, although the double bed on the south wall is unowned. Behind the head of the bed is a set of shelves holding more ruined books, a leveled [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), and a bottle of alto wine. To the left of the bed is a dresser with an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") on top, required as part of the quest [No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned"). There is a large primitive fireplace against the west wall with a large pile of firewood to the left. There is an end table to the right of the bed and two chairs in front of the fire. A wardrobe is against the north wall concealing access to a hidden room (see [notes](#Notes)). To the right of the wardrobe is a small table and chairs, with another bottle of alto wine on top.

Main area

Descending the stairs to the north leads to a large chamber where you will meet the rest of the "family", who are gathered together talking when you enter. There is a word wall to the north, where you learn a word for the Marked for Death shout. To the right is a wide flight of stairs leading up to a passage and to the right of this is a pool of water fed by a waterfall with a large circular stained glass window above which depicts [Sithis](/wiki/Lore:Sithis "Lore:Sithis") as a skeleton. There are many different fungi around the room and throughout the sanctuary as listed below. There are many Dark Brotherhood banners hanging from the walls of the chamber. To the right of the pool is a second passage. To the west is a large fireplace with an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), and [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") in front along with a long wooden table holding an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe"), an [iron greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword"), an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), and an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"). This is where you will normally find Arnbjorn working. To the right of this are several archery targets and practice dummies and where you will normally find [Veezara](/wiki/Skyrim:Veezara "Skyrim:Veezara") either sitting on the ground or practicing with the dummies.

Crafting stations

Lis' pit

Behind this, to the left of the word wall is an earthen ramp leading up to another doorway. There are a couple of barrels of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") to the left of this doorway. In the next room, to the right is a wooden bench with a respawning [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") containing leveled items beside it. Against the southwest wall are a couple of sets of shelves holding a filled petty soul gem, an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") containing uncommon ingredients, a leveled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Soul Gem"), a [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot"), a [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") flower, a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), and a flower basket. In the middle of this room is a stone table with copies of *[The Apprentice's Assistant](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Apprentice%27s_Assistant "Skyrim:The Apprentice's Assistant")* and *[An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Explorer%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim")* on top. Against the south wall is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") with two [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flowers on top. In an alcove to the north is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"). To the west is a wooden flight of stairs leading down to a pit containing [Lis](/wiki/Skyrim:Lis "Skyrim:Lis"), [Babette](/wiki/Skyrim:Babette "Skyrim:Babette")'s pet [frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), and the skeletal remains of [Gaston Bellefort](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaston_Bellefort "Skyrim:Gaston Bellefort"). At the top of the stairs is a small table and chair where the 300-year-old child [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") (and the only trader within the sanctuary), Babette, is usually found sitting. [Festus Krex](/wiki/Skyrim:Festus_Krex "Skyrim:Festus Krex") and [Gabriella](/wiki/Skyrim:Gabriella "Skyrim:Gabriella") can also both normally be found in this area. To the northeast is another doorway with stairs leading down into a dining room.

Dining room

The dining room contains two long tables placed end-to-end in the middle of the room with chairs arranged around them. On the tables is a [pheasant roast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Roast "Skyrim:Pheasant Roast"), two portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), two [venison chops](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison_Chop "Skyrim:Venison Chop"), a [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a joint of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [tomato](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), and several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). Nazir is normally found sitting at this table. To the northwest is a large fireplace with two pots hanging over it. To the left is a counter with a copy of *[Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste")*, a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") on top, and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") hanging from a rack above. To the right is another counter with shelves above it holding two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a tomato, and a couple of loaves of bread. Against the south wall are two thrones with a small table in front, a tall wardrobe to the right, and a very faded copy of [The Five Tenets](/wiki/Lore:The_Five_Tenets "Lore:The Five Tenets") in a frame to the left. To the northeast is a flight of wooden stairs leading up into sleeping quarters. Under these are several crates, a barrel, and a sack of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). To the left is a cupboard with two sacks and a bottle of alto wine on the shelves. Hanging above is a bunch of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear") and two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"). There are Dark Brotherhood banners hanging high on the walls at either end of the room.

The sleeping quarters contain five single unowned beds, a cupboard and a counter each holding two food sacks, two end tables, one of which has a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale") on top, two dressers, one with a thistle branch on top and the other with an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe") on top, a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), a large [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") and a novice-locked respawning [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing gold all found around the room. There is a doorway to the southeast and to the right, on a ledge overlooking the dining room, is a stack of barrels and a sack of food. Through the doorway is a passage with a small table and chairs with a bottle of wine on the left, with another framed copy of The Five Tenets hanging on the wall behind, and a small set of shelves to the right holding clutter. The passage runs to the southwest, with a doorway on the left and a stone table on the right with a sprig of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), and a [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull") on top. Opposite is a small set of shelves holding a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"), an iron helmet, and some ruined books. Hanging above are two bunches of dried elves ear and a bunch of [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam"). The doorway at the end leads back into the main chamber, at the top of the wide flight of stairs.

Word wall

Going through the doorway to the left off the corridor from the direction of the sleeping quarters leads to a small area containing two deathbell plants, with three more doors off of it, to the northeast, east, and south. The doorway to the northeast leads to a small room with an owned child's stone bed, used by Babette. Also in the room is a set of shelves holding several [skulls](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull "Skyrim:Skull"), a troll skull, some ruined books, and an urn, a throne, and a counter holding a flower basket, a sample of [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), a sample of [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), a nightshade flower, and a copy of the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") skill book *[Sacred Witness](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacred_Witness "Skyrim:Sacred Witness")*.

The doorway to the east leads into a strangely shaped room with a table and chair on the right with a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") on top. There are four weapon racks holding an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), with an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe") leaning against the wall next to it. Opposite is a set of shelves holding a piece of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") and a [mammoth tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk"). To the right of these are several crates and a dresser with two food sacks on top. In the corner is a cave-in, with several pieces of damaged and overturned furniture among the rubble. In the center of the room is a long wooden table and benches with an iron mace and a bottle of wine on top. Against the east wall is an unowned single bed with an end table to the left. On the end table is a bottle of wine. To the right is a cupboard holding clutter and a sack, another end table, and a set of shelves holding an [iron warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer"), an iron dagger, and a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe").

The Night Mother's room

The doorway to the south leads into a fairly empty room that is behind the circular stained glass window seen in the main area. It has more Dark Brotherhood banners on either side of it. There is a broken sideboard, a bloody wooden table, and a set of shelves in the room. On the shelves is another respawning knapsack containing leveled items, a bottle of alto wine, and a troll skull. There are several crates, barrels, and chairs around the room, as well as a second door to the south. This leads to another passage running east-west, and leads down some stairs to the main area to the right of the pool.

#### Plants and Fungi

|  |
| --- |
| Ingredients:  - 8 Bleeding Crown - 2 Blisterwort \* - 2 Deathbell - 5 Fly Amanita - 1 Imp Stool - 7 Namira's Rot - 2 Nightshade - 9 White Cap |

\* One additional growth cannot be interacted with.

### Changes during related quests

Once you have completed at least one of your initial contracts to kill [Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi"), [Beitild](/wiki/Skyrim:Beitild "Skyrim:Beitild"), or [Ennodius Papius](/wiki/Skyrim:Ennodius_Papius "Skyrim:Ennodius Papius"), the next time you enter the sanctuary you will find a commotion in the main area, with all the family including Astrid gathered around a new person named [Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero"). You may have seen this person before on the road near Loreius Farm with a broken wagon wheel in need of help. There is a [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Delayed_Burial "Skyrim:Delayed Burial") to convince Loreius to assist Cicero with the broken wheel that can be undertaken prior to meeting him in the sanctuary. Cicero is an Imperial assassin and Keeper of the Dark Brotherhood. As Keeper, he is responsible for caring for the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother")'s body and casket. He's come to Skyrim with the Night Mother in a large crate, seeking protection for them, at the last functioning sanctuary in the empire, after the last sanctuary in Cyrodiil fell. Most of the family seem unhappy about his arrival, with the exception of Festus Krex who is overjoyed and believes this marks the beginning of the return to the old ways.

The next time you visit the sanctuary you will find the Night Mother's casket has been moved and is standing upright in the small room behind the stained glass window. Cicero takes the strange shaped room at the back of the sanctuary next to Babette's as his sleeping quarters.

Following the completion of the Dark Brotherhood quest [Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security"), a total of five journals written by Cicero can be found in his quarters. They detail his life from his origins in Bruma, all the way through to recent events, including mentioning another disused sanctuary in Dawnstar, where he originally went when arriving in Skyrim. In the final volume it talks of the existence of another sanctuary in Dawnstar and provides the password granting access.

Astrid and Arnbjorn's room

Upon returning to the sanctuary at the end of the quest [To Kill an Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Kill_an_Empire "Skyrim:To Kill an Empire"), you will find several Penitus Oculatus agents on the road leading to the sanctuary along with horses and carriages loaded with firewood and barrels of oil, with more agents and barrels stacked near the entrance. There are oil slicks on and around the barrels, which can be ignited with any flames. Festus Krex can be found dead to the right of the entrance, pinned to a tree by many iron arrows. Upon entering the sanctuary, all is in pandemonium with fires raging throughout and agents slaughtering any of your brethren they find. They are led by [Arcturus](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcturus "Skyrim:Arcturus"). As you move through the sanctuary the fires continue to grow, herding you ever deeper. There are bodies of many dead agents, showing how valiantly each of your family fought, but it is obvious by the sheer number of agents it's overwhelming. In the first room, where you would normally find Astrid, is the body of Veezara, along with two agents discussing who betrayed the family. In the main chamber is Arnbjorn in werewolf form, but still wearing his shrouded cuirass; his death is scripted and unavoidable. Next Gabriella's remains can be found in the room containing the arcane enchanter. She's wearing her shrouded robes, shoes, and hand wraps. In the pit are the remains of Lis; unusually you can harvest two vials of frostbite venom from her, as if she were a giant frostbite spider. In the sleeping quarters you will find [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") battling with Arcturus. Once Arcturus is defeated you and Nazir need to find an escape. The Night Mother tells you to embrace her.

The secret room where you find Astrid performing the Black Sacrament

After a cutscene, you will hear Babette cajoling Nazir to dig out the Night Mother's casket more quickly. Once opened, you will find it next to the pool in the main chamber. The Night Mother instructs you to speak to Astrid. You will find her in a secret chamber off her and Arnbjorn's bedroom. The wardrobe has been pulled aside to reveal the chamber and Astrid laid out barely alive on the floor, with the [Blade of Woe](/wiki/Skyrim:Blade_of_Woe "Skyrim:Blade of Woe"), an iron dagger, and a nightshade flower beside her. A cave-in has blocked the passage at the top of the stairs leading to the sleeping quarters and the doorway that leads to the crafting stations and Lis' pit. There are numerous burnt corpses found in the main chamber and first room that can be looted for a few septims or a sample of bone meal. There is nothing else of interest. It is obvious that the sanctuary is finished and that you will need to move the Dark Brotherhood to new premises.

## Notes

- When you first enter the sanctuary after speaking with the black door, the game will not autosave.
- [Followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") cannot enter the sanctuary, and will stand outside waiting while you are inside. However, spectral entities such as [Arniel's ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Arniel%27s_Shade "Skyrim:Summon Arniel's Shade"), will follow you in.
- Sleeping in any of the beds here will normally provide the [Rested](/wiki/Skyrim:Rested "Skyrim:Rested") bonus. However, if your spouse is currently following you (and waiting outside), you will instead receive the [Lover's Comfort](/wiki/Skyrim:Lover%27s_Comfort "Skyrim:Lover's Comfort") bonus.
- If you approach the door to the sanctuary before starting "[With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...")", no map marker will be seen.
- If you complete the quest "[Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!")" instead of the Dark Brotherhood questline, all areas of the sanctuary will remain accessible and undamaged.
- Cicero's journals appear in his room during the quest [Whispers in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:Whispers_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:Whispers in the Dark").
- All cupboards, dressers, and end tables in the sanctuary are non-respawning and safe to store items in.

## Bugs

- After the sanctuary is destroyed, entering it may cause the game to freeze.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9.26.0.8, fixes this bug.
- After you finish "[To Kill an Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Kill_an_Empire "Skyrim:To Kill an Empire")", the items stored in the containers may disappear, and [Penitus Oculatus](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus") agents may continue to spawn outside. **?**
- If you have *[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")* installed, the Word Wall here may also teach you a word for the [Drain Vitality](/wiki/Skyrim:Drain_Vitality "Skyrim:Drain Vitality") shout. **?**
- If you use [Dead Thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Thrall "Skyrim:Dead Thrall") when entering the sanctuary, the thralls will disappear, but will remain on your active effects list. **?**
- The books on the bookshelf may permanently disappear after activating it. **?**
  - Reload a previous save, and try again.
- If you return to this sanctuary after the Dark Brotherhood moves into the [Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary"), the loading screen will still say "The Sanctuary in Skyrim's Pine Forest is the Dark Brotherhood's last remaining refuge in all of Tamriel." **?**

## Maps

  Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary

# Skyrim:Dark Elf (dead)

## Overview

**Dark Elves** are unnamed and deceased [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") scattered around Skyrim.

| Dark Elf ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Dark_Elf "Lore:Dark Elf")) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Race | [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | N/A | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00045800 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 0 (**Dead**) | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| Respawns | Yes | | |

_02.jpg)

A dead male Dark Elf in Cronvangr Cave

These **Dark Elves** are all male [farmers](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") and wear randomly determined farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") (7 variations) or a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") (4 variations), with a 50% chance for a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat "Skyrim:Hat") (3 variations). Additionally there is a slim chance they may carry a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and a small amount of gold.

They can be found in the following locations:

- [Cronvangr Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Cronvangr_Cave "Skyrim:Cronvangr Cave")
- [Faldar's Tooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Faldar%27s_Tooth "Skyrim:Faldar's Tooth")
- [Hob's Fall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Hob%27s_Fall_Cave "Skyrim:Hob's Fall Cave")
- Northwest of [Half-Moon Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Half-Moon_Mill "Skyrim:Half-Moon Mill"), east of [Moss Mother Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern") [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-48572&y=-52172&zoom=17&legacy=true)
- East of [Vahlok's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Vahlok%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Vahlok's Tomb")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")

| Dark Elf | | | |

.jpg)

A dead female Dark Elf

These **Dark Elves** are all female [farmers](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") and wear randomly determined farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") (7 variations) or a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") (4 variations), with a 50% chance for a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat "Skyrim:Hat") (3 variations). Additionally there is a slim chance they may carry a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and a small amount of gold.

They can be found in the following locations:

- [Darkshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkshade "Skyrim:Darkshade")
- [Unmarked bandit camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places#Unmarked_Bandit_and_Forsworn_Camps "Skyrim:Unmarked Places") south of [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch"), east of [Peak's Shade Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Peak%27s_Shade_Tower "Skyrim:Peak's Shade Tower") [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-6428&y=-85559&zoom=17&legacy=true)
- East of [Vahlok's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Vahlok%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Vahlok's Tomb")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")

| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 0 (**Dead**) | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |

.jpg)

The dead Dark Elf peddler

A dead **Dark Elf** peddler[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch_Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Netch Leather Armor") is found at a camp southeast of [Haknir's Shoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir%27s_Shoal "Skyrim:Haknir's Shoal"). [His journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Peddler%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Peddler's Journal") is found on his body, detailing how he made a deal with rieklings for netch leather and presumably died fighting off the nearby [horkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker "Skyrim:Horker"). He wears a [Dunmer Outfit](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmer_Outfit "Skyrim:Dunmer Outfit") and [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmer_Shoes "Skyrim:Dunmer Shoes"). Additionally he carries a [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") and a piece of [charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal"), as referenced in his journal to be part of dyeing the leather. He may also carry a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and a small amount of gold.

# Skyrim:Darkest Depths

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Catch underground fish.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Swims-In-Deep-Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water "Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water") |
| Location(s): | [Riften Fishery](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery "Skyrim:Riften Fishery") |
| Reward: | 400 Gold |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE001\_Fish\_MQ4 |
| Added by: | [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") |

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Frozen Fish](/wiki/Skyrim:Frozen_Fish "Skyrim:Frozen Fish") | **Next →** [Fishing Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Legend "Skyrim:Fishing Legend") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Frozen Fish](/wiki/Skyrim:Frozen_Fish "Skyrim:Frozen Fish") | | → Next | [Fishing Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Legend "Skyrim:Fishing Legend") | | |

[File:SR-quest-Darkest Depths.jpg](/w/index.php?title=Special:Upload&wpDestFile=SR-quest-Darkest_Depths.jpg "File:SR-quest-Darkest Depths.jpg")

Darkest Depths

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Swims-In-Deep-Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water "Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water") and receive the list.
2. Obtain a [Vampire Fish](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Fish "Skyrim:Vampire Fish").
3. Obtain a [Tripod Spiderfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripod_Spiderfish "Skyrim:Tripod Spiderfish").
4. Obtain a [Glass Catfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Catfish "Skyrim:Glass Catfish").
5. Obtain a [Direfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Direfish "Skyrim:Direfish").
6. (Optional) Read [Fishing Mastery, v4](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Mastery,_v4 "Skyrim:Fishing Mastery, v4").

## Detailed Walkthrough

Speak to Swims:

:   **I'm ready for the next fishing challenge.**
:   *"Of course. Maybe you can help me."*

:   **I'll explore underground and bring you the fish you need.** / **Caves are dangerous. You're lucky I'm the one doing this for you.**

    :   *"My thanks to you."*

He will then hand you [list of underground fish](/wiki/Skyrim:List_of_Underground_Fish "Skyrim:List of Underground Fish") to catch:

- [Direfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Direfish "Skyrim:Direfish")
- [Glass Catfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Catfish "Skyrim:Glass Catfish")
- [Tripod Spiderfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripod_Spiderfish "Skyrim:Tripod Spiderfish")
- [Vampire Fish](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Fish "Skyrim:Vampire Fish")

These fish can all be caught in underground fishing spots such as [Embershard Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Embershard_Mine "Skyrim:Embershard Mine") and [Broken Oar Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Oar_Grotto "Skyrim:Broken Oar Grotto"), a full list of underground fishing spots can be found [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity)#Fishing_Locations "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)").
(note - if fourth volume of Fishing Mastery is read, the quest shows "Eldergleam Sanctuary in Eastmarch,..." but there is no fishing spot in there. However, several Spadefish can be caught by hand in the cave's pool. 1 is needed for 'Caught in the Rain' part of this questline)

Once you have caught the required fish return to Swims:

:   **Here are the fish you asked for.**
:   *"Thank you. Here, this is for you."*

He will then hand you 400 gold.

## Quest Stages

| Darkest Depths (ccBGSSSE001\_Fish\_MQ4) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Swims-In-Deep-Water has given me another fishing challenge. I should read the list he gave me to see what I will need to catch. |
| 20 |  | The fish that Swims-In-Deep-Water would like me to catch are only found in caves, flooded mines, and other underground places. Once I've caught one of each, I should return them to him. I can read more about each fish, and where to catch them, in the fourth volume of Fishing Mastery. |
| 21 |  | I've read the fourth volume of Fishing Mastery. The fish I need to complete the challenge can only be caught underground. Eldergleam Sanctuary in Eastmarch, Brood Cavern in the mountains south of Morthal, Embershard Mine near Riverwood, and Chillwind Depths south of the Dragon Bridge were places mentioned that I could try my hand at catching them. |
| 200 | ☑ | I've given Swims-In-Deep-Water all of the fish he requested as proof of completing his fishing challenge. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE001_Fish_MQ4 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE001_Fish_MQ4`.

# Skyrim:Darkfall Cave

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Darkfall Cave ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darkfall+Cave+%28DG%29)) | | |
| Added by | [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 10 |
| Occupants | |
| [Frostbite Spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), [Trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |

| Region | |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | |
| Location | |
| South of [Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur") North of [Druadach Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Redoubt "Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt") | |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |

Darkfall Cave

**Darkfall Cave** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") south of [Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur") containing [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") and [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll"). It contains only one zone, *[Darkfall Cave](#Darkfall_Cave)*.

The cave is extremely dark, so consider bringing a light source if you don't have [night vision](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Eye_(effect) "Skyrim:Night Eye (effect)").

## Related Quests

- **[Touching the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Touching_the_Sky "Skyrim:Touching the Sky")**: Find and retrieve [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow").

### Exterior

The entrance to the cave is at the end of a mountain meadow which rises to just above the snowline. A few paces northeast of the entrance is a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberry "Skyrim:Snowberry") bush. There are a number of random encounters nearby, including leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") and [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn").

### Darkfall Cave

During Touching the Sky, if the Dragonborn has a second follower as well as Serana (possible if the second follower was acquired while Serana was waiting, before entering the Soul Cairn for the first time), it is best to dismiss the second follower. Otherwise, it is possible to bring them through part of the cave system, but they will almost certainly become permanently stuck somewhere along the way.

The entrance leads into a natural cave with a sparsely lit passage descending to the south. There are a couple patches of [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") fungus growing in this passage. At the bottom the passage turns west and passes a pool that is fed by a waterfall. If the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") is installed, this pool is a source of four rare [scorpion fish](/wiki/Skyrim:Scorpion_Fish "Skyrim:Scorpion Fish"), as well as three [tripod spiderfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripod_Spiderfish "Skyrim:Tripod Spiderfish"). Following the path west from the pool, it takes a couple of turns before passing a small ledge overlooking the water, which features a white cap fungus on the left. The passage turns south at this point. Ahead is a frostbite spider in an alcove. There is a concealed door at the back of the alcove, but no way to open it on this side. On the ground is a [dessicated corpse](/wiki/Skyrim:Dessicated_Corpse "Skyrim:Dessicated Corpse") and an [egg sac](/wiki/Skyrim:Egg_Sac "Skyrim:Egg Sac"), which can be looted and harvested, respectively. The path turns west at the alcove and continues to descend. A patch of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") is on the right, followed by a narrow suspension bridge over a turbulent underground river. The bridge creaks and quivers as you cross and is obviously in poor condition, with one of the rope handrails missing. On the far side is a small ledge with two [moonstone ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein"); one is on the ground, and the other is on the wall. There is also a small round wooden table to the right, with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") on top.

Once you have crossed, attempting to cross back again will result in the bridge collapsing and dropping you into the river below. You will be swept rapidly downstream. The only way to return to the other side of the chasm without falling into the river and having to proceed through the entire cave system is to use the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). This will enable you to mine the ore veins and leave.

Allowing yourself to be swept away by the river, you will be forced underwater several times during the ride, but never long enough to put you in danger of drowning. Staying above water, you will see several [glowing mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") and a couple of frostbite spiders. Eventually, you will drop over one final short waterfall and be deposited onto a wide rocky stream bed. Here two frostbite spiders soon followed by three more will converge and attack. On a pillar ahead are several more glowing mushrooms. Heading downstream, you will see raised banks on either side. On the right side are two more egg sacs that you can harvest, and just past these is a large perfectly circular hole in the wall lined with cobwebs. A [giant frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Giant Frostbite Spider") is in this alcove. Once you have dealt with the spider, at the back of the alcove is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and a [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") you can loot. There are a few [web sacs](/wiki/Skyrim:Web_Sac "Skyrim:Web Sac") in the water and on the ceiling outside the alcove, and several more glowing mushrooms on the walls. The stream passes under the cave wall and the path turns west, before turning north again by a lit brazier; the route also narrows and begins to climb.

At the top, an extinguished campfire is ahead, and to the right is the body of a [dead Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton_(dead) "Skyrim:Breton (dead)") woman with a lit [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch") beside her. On the corpse is a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Cave_Note "Skyrim:Darkfall Cave Note") which explains a little about why she was here. The camp has been set up at a crossroads; your approach is from the south. An unlocked wooden chest containing three more torches and other loot, an unowned bedroll, and a small table are also beside the fire. On the table are two random [potions of resist fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"), a [cure poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Poison "Skyrim:Cure Poison") potion, a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"), a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), three [spider eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg"), and a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). To the left of the table on the east wall is a concealed door, which acts as a shortcut to a large chamber deeper within the cave system. There is a lean-to and another bedroll to the north. Behind the lean-to is a chain which operates the concealed door. Returning south of the campfire, there are passages to the east and west. The path to the west ascends, and after a couple of turns enters a small chamber with a spiraling path leading up. A total of three [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") and one white cap fungi as well as several [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") grow in this chamber. At the top the passage ends at a dead end, where a chain to the left opens the nearby concealed door connected to the alcove with the spider near the cave entrance.

Following the blood-soaked path to the east of the campfire as it descends, a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") triggers a [rockfall](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") from behind near the top of the passage. After several turns, you will pass three glowing mushrooms on the left followed by two more on the right. The path then opens into a large chamber with several pillars of rock, various ledges, and a large ankle-deep pool of water. Two trolls wander near the north wall, and in the northeast corner is an unlocked chest, with gory human remains and a lit torch on the ground beside it. There are a few glowing mushrooms around the chamber and many hanging moss growing from the ceiling, but little of interest. To the southwest is the passage connected to the shortcut from the camp, with a glowing mushroom near the concealed door on this side. Near the passage are several broken stone pillars and what appears to be the roof of a small six-sided structure with unfamiliar architecture. Prior to beginning the quest [Touching the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Touching_the_Sky "Skyrim:Touching the Sky"), two more trolls will occupy the west end of this chamber. After killing them, you can exit the cave by returning to the campfire crossroads through the nearby concealed door, then following the passage ascending to the west through the other concealed door.

Shrine to Auriel

However, if you have started the quest, the trolls to the west are replaced by the armored [snow elf](/wiki/Lore:Snow_Elf "Lore:Snow Elf") [Knight-Paladin Gelebor](/wiki/Skyrim:Knight-Paladin_Gelebor "Skyrim:Knight-Paladin Gelebor") and his crude camp. The camp consists of an unowned bedroll, a lean-to covering a rough sideboard holding clutter, a small table also holding minor items, and a [Shrine of Auriel](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines "Skyrim:Shrines") which grants a [fortify marksman](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Marksman "Skyrim:Fortify Marksman") blessing. As you approach, Gelebor will address you. After a short discussion, he will raise the six-sided structure to reveal an empty basin in the middle and give you the [initiate's ewer](/wiki/Skyrim:Initiate%27s_Ewer "Skyrim:Initiate's Ewer"). The wall behind the basin then becomes a dark shimmering portal that transports you directly to the beginning of [Darkfall Passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Passage "Skyrim:Darkfall Passage").

## Notes

- Unlike most other large streams, the current of one of the streams in Darkfall Cave is too strong for you to negotiate.

## Bugs

- The bridge may never break the second time you and Serana cross it. **?**
  - Solution: Push Serana off the side of the bridge without the rope, push her off the section without the wooden fence across from the bridge, or use the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout on her. Then follow her downstream.
  - Solution: Jump off the bridge or the section across, ride the stream until it ends, then wait at least 1 hour. Serana should now join you downstream.

## Maps

- 

  Darkfall Cave

# Skyrim:Darkfall Grotto

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Cave: Darkfall Grotto | | |
| Added by | [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") |

| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 18 |
| Occupants | |
| [Chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), [Chaurus Hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Hunter "Skyrim:Chaurus Hunter"), [Feral Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Feral_Falmer "Skyrim:Feral Falmer") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC1zFalmerValley01 | |
| Region | |
| [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | |
| Location | |
| [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale") | |

Darkfall Grotto

**Darkfall Grotto** is a small cave in the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale").

### Exterior

The exterior to this cave is the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale"). It can be accessed by using the [paragon platform](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale#Paragon_Platform "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale") with the [amethyst paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst_Paragon "Skyrim:Amethyst Paragon"), or by following the icy river south, past the Wayshrine of Learning, and jumping down the waterfall at the end. Jumping down the waterfall causes you to fall a very great height and land in the river below. You will need to surface quickly and swim to shore; otherwise, you'll be swept away by the powerful current. When you fall in, [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") will exclaim: *"Ugh, I told you! Next time I say to please not go over a waterfall, maybe you'll listen to me."*

### Darkfall Grotto

The paragon portal teleports you to the top of a rock pillar near the west wall of the dimly lit main chamber. The broken stone arch forming the portal allows you to return directly to the paragon platform. Ahead on the pillar is an unlocked stone [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") holding quality loot under a [glowing mushroom](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom"), with a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") beside it. You may reach the floor of the chamber either by dropping into the water and quickly swimming to shore, or by using the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") and dropping directly onto the ground below.

At the bottom of the chamber, a path runs along the west and south walls near the waterfall cascading from above. Proceeding northeast along the south wall, you'll find the corpse of a [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") on the ground. To the east is a small Falmer settlement consisting of a pair of Falmer tents. In front of each tent is a Falmer corpse, with a Falmer chest inside both tents. The area is occupied by [feral Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Feral_Falmer "Skyrim:Feral Falmer"), which don't wear [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Armor "Skyrim:Falmer Armor") and generally don't use [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Weapons "Skyrim:Falmer Weapons") other than their claws. To the left of the second tent, against the north wall by a glowing mushroom that may be difficult to interact with, is a ramp ascending to one of several ledges. The ledges ultimately lead to the southeast corner of the chamber, where another Falmer corpse lies next to a Falmer chest between two more glowing mushrooms. Returning to the lower level, beyond the first two tents to the north is a third tent, with yet another Falmer corpse in front and a Falmer chest beside it. Three feral Falmer and a [chaurus hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Hunter "Skyrim:Chaurus Hunter") roam the area to the north below the third tent. Returning to the second tent, a ramp descending to the north along the shore features another Falmer corpse. Proceeding to the north wall, two empty tents are against the wall, with three dead [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") between them. It is possible to reach several additional ledges in this area, but all are empty.

To exit the cave, you must jump into the river and let it sweep you away to the northwest. You will drop down several waterfalls before ultimately falling into the cloudy lake in the final chamber in [Darkfall Passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Passage "Skyrim:Darkfall Passage"). Return to the wayshrine, which will now include portals to all other wayshrines you've raised in addition to the initial portal to the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale").

## Notes

- Be careful when you jump down the waterfall, as it is possible to strike the rock wall behind the falls and die.
- Be careful near the river, as your [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") can fall in and be swept away into Darkfall Passage.

## Bugs

- It is possible to become stuck near the walls in the river when attempting to leave. **?**
  - Conjuring a frost atronach, attacking it, and having it knock you free may resolve this issue.
  - Using "bats" as a Vampire Lord may also resolve this issue.

## Maps

Darkfall Grotto

# Skyrim:Darkfall Passage

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Cave: Darkfall Passage | | |

| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 18 |
| Occupants | |
| [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [Chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), [Chaurus Hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Hunter "Skyrim:Chaurus Hunter"), [Vale Deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Vale_Deer "Skyrim:Vale Deer"), [Vale Sabre Cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Vale_Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Vale Sabre Cat") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC1DarkfallPassageStart, DLC1DarkfallPassageOrigin, DLC1DarkfallPassageEndStart, DLC1DarkfallPassageWayshrine01, DLC1DarkfallPassageWayshrine02 | |
| Location | |
| [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Alchemy Labs](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") | 1 |

Darkfall Passage

**Darkfall Passage** is a small cave only accessible through [Darkfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Cave "Skyrim:Darkfall Cave") serving as the only access to the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale"). It contains only one zone, *[Darkfall Passage](#Darkfall_Passage)*.

The cave system is split into two distinctly different areas; the first contains many [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and their tents in several smaller chambers, while the second consists of a single huge chamber full of Vale fauna, bioluminescent fungi, and glowing crystallized rock.

## Related Quests

- **[Touching the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Touching_the_Sky "Skyrim:Touching the Sky")**: Find and retrieve [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow").

### Darkfall Passage

Passing through the portal at the end of Darkfall Cave leads to a small chamber with the remains of a wayshrine surrounded by [glowing mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") and strange glowing pink tubular worms (*"Cave Worms"* per internal game data) which retract their glowing segments as you approach. The ruined wayshrine cannot take you back to Darkfall Cave; the only exit is through the next wayshrine at the end of the cave. The cave's primary light sources are the bioluminescent fungi and fauna; a [light](/wiki/Skyrim:Light "Skyrim:Light") spell, [torches](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch"), or [night vision](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Eye_(effect) "Skyrim:Night Eye (effect)") are therefore recommended. A passage heads north, with patches of standing water along the undulating path and a [chaurus coccoon](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Cocoon "Skyrim:Chaurus Cocoon")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") on the left containing a [chaurus hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Hunter "Skyrim:Chaurus Hunter")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"). Use of [detect life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(effect) "Skyrim:Detect Life (effect)") is highly recommended in this area. Farther ahead is a [Falmer hive](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Hive "Skyrim:Falmer Hive") containing a skulking Falmer. On the right is a second empty hive. The passage continues, and after a couple of twists and turns leads to another occupied Falmer hive, with a second Falmer standing a short distance beyond. They are likely to attack simultaneously.

Beyond the hives and initial Falmer, a short tunnel leads to a chamber with a low ceiling, where you will encounter two [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). Six chaurus egg sacs in two small groups are in the chamber. Against one of the rock pillars near the middle is a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") with a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel") containing two random [potions of waterbreathing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Waterbreathing "Skyrim:Potion of Waterbreathing") and other loot. Behind the same pillar is a flooded vertical shaft which you can swim down into, with a submerged tunnel heading east to a second flooded shaft leading to a small chamber above. This chamber features another lootable skeleton beside an [elven bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Bow "Skyrim:Elven Bow") and [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Elven Arrow"), a leveled [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), two random [potions of resist fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"), and a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). Two [gleamblossom](/wiki/Skyrim:Gleamblossom "Skyrim:Gleamblossom") plants are also next to the skeleton. These rare plants are only found in Darkfall Passage and the Forgotten Vale, and can be harvested for use in [alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy"). The skeleton also carries a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Passage_Note_I "Skyrim:Darkfall Passage Note I"), which explains this person chose to die in this isolated chamber rather than face the cave's hostile creatures again. Returning to the previous chamber, a narrow passage flanked by glowing pink worms heads west.

The passage turns and heads north, where you will encounter a Falmer, and just beyond, a narrow passage on the right wall. Ahead along the main passage is a pillar in the middle of the passage with a [claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Claw "Skyrim:Claw") trap on the back. A [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") beside the pillar triggers the claw trap. The narrow passage leads back out into the main passage just beyond the trap. On the right just after the pillar is an unlocked Falmer chest. At the far end of the main passage is an unoccupied Falmer hive and an empty cocoon. The passage turns to the west, passing a table made from chitin holding a random [potion of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"), two [chaurus eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), a piece of [chaurus chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Chitin "Skyrim:Chaurus Chitin"), and a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"). At the next corner are three more chaurus cocoons, all of which are empty.

The passage turns south and opens into a large chamber containing many more chaurus cocoons, most of which are empty. A ramp with railings leads up to an empty Falmer tent ahead. Off to the right, beside a rock pillar is a chaurus cocoon containing a chaurus hunter. To the west is a Falmer standing near the bottom of another ramp, which leads up to a raised area where another Falmer is patrolling. Farther west is a screen of waterfalls. On the lower level before the ramp, behind the pillar is a Falmer tent with a table holding a random [potion of invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Brief_Invisibility "Skyrim:Potion of Brief Invisibility") and three random potions of resist element. At the top of the ramp to the west, empty Falmer tents are at either end of the raised area, and a ramp leads back down on the right. At the bottom of this ramp is another occupied cocoon. A single Falmer magic-user stands inside a large tent nearby, with a smaller tent on the left. Both of these tents back onto a narrow crevice that the waterfalls are cascading into. A third tent is to the south, with an occupied Falmer hive on the right. Three gleamblossom plants grow in front of the first two tents, with the larger tent containing an unlocked chest and a table holding two pieces of chaurus chitin, and the smaller tent containing a table with a [Falmer war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_War_Axe "Skyrim:Falmer War Axe") on top. The tent to the south is empty, with a path passing in front of the tent and hive.

After passing the tent and hive, to the south is a dead end with a concealed door inaccessible from this side. However, if you jump down into the crevice, you will land in a flowing creek that will deposit you next to two lootable skeletons. Follow the path upwards to find another skeleton and an unlocked chest. At the end of the passage, a rope release to the left will open the concealed door in the dead end. To the north on the left side of the crevice is a path rising up past more glowing pink tubular worms and then back down into another chamber inhabited by more Falmer. This chamber includes several tents, with a Falmer to the west on a ledge. An empty tent is on the lower level, with an apprentice-[trapped](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") wooden chest surrounded by three gleamblossom plants and scattered skeletal remains. The tension cable is on the near side, and triggers a pair of claw traps hinged on the bridge above. The bridge links raised sections on either side of the chamber. To cross the bridge, pass under it and then proceed up the ramp to the right. An empty tent is on the near side, and a lootable skeleton is on the bridge. On the far side is a fenced gated compound and three occupied Falmer hives on the chamber walls. Inside the compound, in the center is a grisly statue formed with various human bones standing on some glowing blue crystallized rock and surrounded by fencing. The first tent on the right is empty, but the second tent contains a table holding a piece of chitin, a [Falmer sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Sword "Skyrim:Falmer Sword"), a random potion of healing, [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), or [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), a random potion of resist element, and a random poison. To the left of the gates is an open pen filled with human bones and skulls, and the tent to the left contains an unlocked chest.

Scorpion tent with chest

To the west is a separate chamber with a large pile of the crystallized rock; stretched across the path is a string of [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes"). Many Falmer hives are on the walls at differing heights, but none are occupied. The path first circles this chamber, passing three more gleamblossom plants among the crystal, before continuing to the south and then turning east as it starts to rise. At the top is yet another chamber with a large gated pen in the middle containing two chaurus and fifteen egg sacs. Behind the pen on a raised section to the east is a large ornate tent. In front of the tent is an area that appears to be some kind of stage, where a leveled Falmer is standing. Inside the scorpion tent is an unlocked chest, with two gleamblossom plants to the right. On either side of the tent are bridges crossing through the screen of waterfalls, over which two more Falmer will approach if alerted by any fighting.

Crossing either bridge leads back across the same crevice seen earlier, now at a higher level, to a ledge with two paths leading away to the north and east. A tripwire across the front of the east path triggers a claw trap hinged from above, beyond which is another chamber containing a large, ornate Falmer tent flanked by two occupied chaurus cocoons in front of two empty normal Falmer tents. Four more tripwires are strung around an unlocked Falmer chest near the middle of the chamber, each triggering a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") from the ground. To the right of the entryway is a rope release that can be used to activate the claw trap repeatedly. Inside the large tent is a table with a built-in [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), two random potions of healing, and a random lingering poison.

Following the path heading north will eventually lead to some bone chimes hanging from the ceiling. Under the chimes is a tripwire which triggers a [rockfall](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") from above. A lootable skeleton lies just past the tripwire. The path turns east, then north again. Ahead the path splits, with the right side rising above the left. At the start of the lower path on the left is a lootable skeleton next to a satchel containing two leveled potions of healing. Just past where the two paths rejoin, the passage turns west and rises sharply. Near the top, on the left by a large rock is a lootable skeleton carrying another [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Passage_Note_II "Skyrim:Darkfall Passage Note II"), which mentions the many traps nearby and refers to the Falmer as "the cursed". An [elven sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Sword "Skyrim:Elven Sword") and [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Shield "Skyrim:Elven Shield") and a random potion of resist fire are beside the skeleton. To the north is an obvious concealed door with a claw trap hinged above, and on the wall to the left are two rope releases. The rope on the left lowers the concealed door, while the rope on the right triggers the claw trap from above, spears from below, and a [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") from the sides.

Darkfall Passage interior

The scenery changes drastically beyond the concealed door, with unique [Vale deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Vale_Deer "Skyrim:Vale Deer") and [Vale sabre cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Vale_Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Vale Sabre Cat") instead of Falmer. As soon as you lower the door, a Vale sabre cat marked with green stripes and spots stands facing you on a flat rock in front of a pillar. The path starts on the left and curves around the pillar. In the middle of the path between two rock pillars is the first [poison bloom](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison_Bloom "Skyrim:Poison Bloom") plant, another rare plant found only here in Darkfall Passage. These plants expel a small cloud of poisonous gas when you or other creatures approach, unless you harvest them before they begin to open. The path continues descending, passing another gleamblossom plant near more glowing crystallized rock. From here the path heads northwest, passing two more gleamblossom plants beside more crystal, followed by a ledge to the right of the main path with a cluster of three poison bloom plants on top surrounding a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"). The main path below the ledge features another four gleamblossom plants before descending to a cloudy underground lake. Vale deer, which bear similar markings to Vale sabre cats, roam this area. At the bottom, the path crosses an earthen bridge to a rock pillar in the lake. To the left of the pillar, the main path continues south past a poison bloom plant (which may have already been opened by the nearby deer) and across another bridge over the lake. To the right of the pillar, a secondary route leads west over a short bridge and past a single gleamblossom plant by the shore, with a group of three poison bloom plants on a raised ledge to the right. To the west and throughout the cavern, the rocks form many ledges and platforms which can be navigated using simple mountain climbing techniques. There is nothing of interest in the water.

Following the path across the bridge, a poison bloom plant is found halfway across. On the far side, a Vale sabre cat den under a large overhanging rock contains a single cat guarding the bodies of two Vale deer, with a gleamblossom plant nearby. The path forms a wide bridge to the northwest to again cross the chamber below. Halfway across is a cluster of three poison bloom plants and three gleamblossom plants. To the southwest, a dim glow is visible among the darkened rocks; casting [detect life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(effect) "Skyrim:Detect Life (effect)") will outline a Vale sabre cat. Following the path to the top, the ghost of [Prelate Sidanyis](/wiki/Skyrim:Prelate_Sidanyis "Skyrim:Prelate Sidanyis") stands in front of the first wayshrine, known as the **Wayshrine of Illumination**. He will welcome you, assume you are an initiate, and ask if you are prepared to honor the mantras of Auri-El. Once you confirm you are, he will cause the wayshrine to rise from the ground. Seven gleamblossom plants grow among the crystal around the wayshrine. On your left as you reach the top of the bridge, a path descends toward the dimly lit area seen from the halfway point. At the bottom you will encounter a Vale sabre cat, some skeletal remains with two random filled [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and two gleamblossom plants. If you are here during the related quest, don't forget to draw water from the basin in the wayshrine. The portal transports you to the start of the Forgotten Vale.

## Notes

- A total of 34 gleamblossom plants can be found here, 13 of which are in the Falmer-infested chambers.
- A total of 12 poison bloom plants can be found here, all of which are in the final chamber.

## Bugs

- The poison bloom plants and Vale sabre cats won't respawn.
- The portal to Forgotten Vale may not be apparent; it may simply resemble another wall, unlike other wayshrine portals which visibly shimmer. It may still be used by walking through the back wall of the wayshrine on the far side of the water basin.
- Before reaching the area with the wayshrine, looking at the ground at certain angles may turn the walls invisible and show the areas outside the map, with the lighting changing from very dark to very bright.

# Skyrim:Darklight Tower

## Overview

Darklight Tower

**Darklight Tower** is a medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"), [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag"), and [witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch"). It contains two zones: *[Darklight Tower](#Darklight_Tower)* and *[Darklight Chambers](#Darklight_Chambers)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Repentance](/wiki/Skyrim:Repentance "Skyrim:Repentance")**: Help [Illia](/wiki/Skyrim:Illia "Skyrim:Illia") prevent her mother [Silvia](/wiki/Skyrim:Silvia "Skyrim:Silvia") from transforming into a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven").

### Exterior

The path leading south to the tower from the road between Riften and [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") is unmarked and difficult to spot and is occupied by leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). Various species of harvestable mushrooms and plants grow throughout the area, including [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota"), [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap"), and [mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"). The tower itself is a dilapidated fort, with a large buttressed outer wall and a walkway along the top. An arch leads into a courtyard with several flights of stairs leading up to the entrance. As you approach, impaled goat heads and polished mammoth tusks betray the nature of the occupants inside.

### Darklight Tower

The first floor is the ruined entrance to the tower. Upon entering, you will see a woman named [Illia](/wiki/Skyrim:Illia "Skyrim:Illia") battling a witch in the second room. Once the witch is defeated, Illia will speak to you and ask you to assist her in stopping her mother from becoming a hagraven. There is an adept-locked door to the northeast, with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and a couple food barrels behind it. Illia carries the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower_Closet_Key "Skyrim:Darklight Tower Closet Key") to open the door. Otherwise, there is nothing of note on this floor. Against the south wall a candlelit stairway climbing further up the tower.

At the top of the stairs is a balcony that overlooks the room below and circles to the west. There are two [creatures](/wiki/Skyrim:Creatures "Skyrim:Creatures") in this area, one of which is leveled. At the far end of the balcony is a wooden door leading into a room with a hag, who will attack as soon as you or Illia enter. To the right of the southern stairwell is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy"), with a round wooden table beside it holding a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and a random empty [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"). There is also an unlocked chest hidden under an overturned table in the northwestern corner.

The stairs lead up to the third floor, a two-tiered space containing several rooms that make up the living quarters of the witches in the tower. There is a leveled creature and a witch on this floor. There are two raised sections of flooring linked by a bridge, with stairs leading up to the larger platform opposite the door you entered through. At the top is an area with doorways to both north and south, both of which are blocked by raised spears. A lever is located behind the southern door. The furniture in this room includes four unowned single beds, a table holding a [charred skeever hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide") and a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), and a variety of overturned furniture. The smaller of the two platforms contains a visible [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") trap that is triggered by a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate"), and a cupboard holding a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") and a random potion of healing, with a filled random soul gem on the ground in front of it. To the right of the cupboard is a table with a metal basin in the middle containing a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") and two bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic").

Beneath this area is a corridor heading west, which Illia will follow. The corridor turns south after a few paces, then passes a thick patch of cobwebs that conceal an unlocked chest on the right. The corridor continues, then turns east. There is a locked wooden door on the right that requires the key carried by Illia. Behind the door is a cupboard holding a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Magicka"), two random potions of healing, one potion of [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), and one other random potion. There are also three food barrels in the corner, and two sets of shelves holding only clutter. The corridor continues east and up some stairs into another room containing a large fireplace. A cupboard near the fireplace holds two poisons and a copy of *[The Aetherium Wars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars")*. The room also contains a lever beside a set of spears blocking a doorway. This is the southern of the two sets of spears seen previously. The lever lowers both sets of spears. Illia will warn you that there is a hagraven ahead.

There is a flight of stairs behind the northern spears, with a closed wooden door at the top. The door leads to a room with a hagraven and two creatures. The hagraven will be opposite the door in her tent behind a table. She prefers to attack with [Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt"). On the table is a [hagraven claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Claw "Skyrim:Hagraven Claw"), a random filled soul gem, a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Sun's Dawn, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Sun%27s_Dawn,_v2 "Skyrim:2920, Sun's Dawn, v2")*, and a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"). The usual hagraven decor (impaled goat heads, etc.) surrounds the tent. To the left of the tent is another unlocked chest, while the ground in front of the table contains two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") that appear to have fallen from a rack above. To the right of the door you entered through is a flight of stairs that have caved in. There is a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") among the rubble, while to the north is a wooden door leading to the next zone, *Darklight Chambers*.

### Darklight Chambers

Beyond the door is a curved flight of stairs that leads up to a circular room with large wooden stakes in the middle and a hag and a witch standing next to them. Among the stakes is a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(dead)#Dunmer_Male "Skyrim:Bandit (dead)"). Once the enemies have been dealt with, Illia will approach a master-locked door to the south and exclaim that the door is locked. She will suggest taking the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower_Key "Skyrim:Darklight Tower Key") from one of the hags nearby, or just picking the lock. To the east is another corridor leading up to a door.

The hagraven with the key is located in the next room, a multi-tiered hagraven lair that also contains a hag. There is a short hallway lined with damaging spikes, with stairs leading up to a floor with a hag standing in a tent by an unlocked chest. The hagraven is across a bridge to the south. More stairs lead up against the north wall to another level with a master-locked chest and a cupboard holding three random potions of magicka and three random poisons. Crossing the bridge and climbing another flight of stairs leads to a table with a random empty soul gem, an iron dagger, and a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") on top.

Beyond the master-locked door is a corridor which leads to a flight of stairs. The stairs lead to another corridor containing two food barrels and ending at a small room with a leveled hag. This room contains a small table holding an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") next to a set of shelves against the west wall. On the shelves are two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a random [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), and two potions of magicka. Against the north wall is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters"), while against the east wall is another unlocked chest. The only other item of interest in the room is an unowned bedroll in the middle of the floor. A damp corridor climbs north from here, then turns west and opens onto a balcony above the room with the wooden stakes in the middle. There are two leveled creatures and a hag on the balcony. In the middle of the balcony is a cupboard holding a random [potion of resist magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Magic "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Magic") and a leveled potion of magicka, while the edge of the balcony features a table holding a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") skill book *[Mystery of Talara, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystery_of_Talara,_v3 "Skyrim:Mystery of Talara, v3")*, another random filled soul gem, and a bottle of wine. Past the table are stairs curving up around the tower. At the top of the stairs, there is a square table holding an iron dagger and a wooden door leading outside, where Illia's mother [Silvia](/wiki/Skyrim:Silvia "Skyrim:Silvia") waits to perform her dark ritual.

### Exterior: Top of the Tower

Exiting through the door leads onto a walkway that passes under an arch into a courtyard behind the tower. The area outside the tower is full of hagraven totems, including various animal heads on stakes, mammoth tusks, taproots in netting, and two sets of large ribs with animal skulls and large antlers attached atop Silvia's tent and a nearby rock. Silvia is a fairly adept caster, and carries the unique [Staff of Hag's Wrath](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Hag%27s_Wrath "Skyrim:Staff of Hag's Wrath"). Once she has been dealt with, make sure to loot her body. There is a campfire next to a table holding a copy of the Destruction skill book *[Horror of Castle Xyr](/wiki/Skyrim:Horror_of_Castle_Xyr "Skyrim:Horror of Castle Xyr")*, two random poisons, a leveled filled soul gem, two samples of [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), and a sprig of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). Inside the tent is an unlocked, leveled boss chest. At the rear of the courtyard is an arch blocked by spears that are lowered by activating a lever to the left, while to the north are stairs leading up to the top of the surrounding walls and two towers, one of which is ruined.

Passing through the arch previously blocked by spears and following the path to the east will bring you to the [Ruins of Rkund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Rkund "Skyrim:Ruins of Rkund"). If you take the path west from the gate, you will pass a fallen tree next to a copy of the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") skill book *[Proper Lock Design and Construction](/wiki/Skyrim:Proper_Lock_Design "Skyrim:Proper Lock Design")* on the way to the collapsed entrance of an unmarked Nordic barrow. A [troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll") has taken up residence here, and guards an unlocked chest and a couple [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn").

## Notes

- The largest concentration of scaly pholiota in the game can be found here.
- If you wish to explore the tower more thoroughly while progressing with Illia, she tends to wait for you if you are a certain distance away, reducing the worry of her charging into battle alone.
- There is an inaccessible room in the center of the top of the tower, right before exiting to face Silvia. The room contains a bookshelf holding magicka potions.
- If you climb the mountain to reach the courtyard behind the tower, Silvia will not appear unless you first go in to talk to Illia to start the quest [Repentance](/wiki/Skyrim:Repentance "Skyrim:Repentance"). Then you can climb around back to kill Silvia.

## Bugs

- Climbing the mountain and killing the enemies at the top of the tower instead of entering the tower's lower entrance may result in being unable to earn Illia as a follower. Instead, she will speak to thin air and permanently stand still, awaiting a response from the recently slain hag. If you sit in the chair at the top of the tower, she will tell her mother that she is going to kill her, then walk back inside.
- Everything at the top of the tower may respawn despite the dungeon itself being classed as a "no reset zone".

## Maps

- 

  Darklight Tower
- 

  Darklight Chambers
