# Skyrim:Darkness Returns

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Walk the [Pilgrim's Path](/wiki/Skyrim:Twilight_Sepulcher "Skyrim:Twilight Sepulcher") and return the [Skeleton Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton_Key "Skyrim:Skeleton Key") to its rightful place.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Karliah](/wiki/Skyrim:Karliah "Skyrim:Karliah") |
| Location(s): | [Twilight Sepulcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Twilight_Sepulcher "Skyrim:Twilight Sepulcher") |
| Reward: | Nightingale Blessings |
| ID: | TG09 |
| Suggested Level: | 8 |

The entrance to the [Twilight Sepulcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Twilight_Sepulcher "Skyrim:Twilight Sepulcher")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Enter the [Twilight Sepulcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Twilight_Sepulcher "Skyrim:Twilight Sepulcher").
2. Speak to the [Nightingale Sentinel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Sentinel "Skyrim:Nightingale Sentinel").
   - *(Optional)* Find [Nystrom's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Nystrom%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Nystrom's Journal").
3. Follow the Pilgrim's Path.
4. Unlock the Ebonmere with the [Skeleton Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton_Key "Skyrim:Skeleton Key").
5. Listen to [Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:Nocturnal "Skyrim:Nocturnal").
6. Speak to [Karliah](/wiki/Skyrim:Karliah "Skyrim:Karliah").
7. Choose a Nightingale blessing.

### The Twilight Sepulcher

Gallus's spirit guarding the entrance to the Twilight Sepulcher

Once you enter the [Twilight Sepulcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Twilight_Sepulcher "Skyrim:Twilight Sepulcher"), you will come to a large hall where the spirit of a [Nightingale Sentinel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Sentinel "Skyrim:Nightingale Sentinel") stands watch. When you approach him, he will initiate a conversation:

*"I don't recognize you, but I sense that you're one of us. Who are you?"*
***"I'd ask the same question of you."***:
*"The last of the Nightingale Sentinels, I'm afraid. I've defended the Sepulcher alone for what seems like an eternity."*
***"The last? What happened to the rest?"***:
*"We were betrayed by one of our own kind. In fact, I'm to blame for what's happened here."*
***"How are you to blame?"***:
*"I was blinded. Blinded by dark treachery masquerading as friendship. Perhaps if I had been more vigilant, then [Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey") wouldn't have lured me to my fate and stolen the Skeleton Key."*
***"Wait a moment... You're [Gallus](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallus "Skyrim:Gallus")!"***:
*"I haven't heard that name in a long time. How do you know of me?"*
***"I have the Key."***:
*"The Key! You have the Skeleton Key! I never thought I'd see it again. And Mercer Frey?"*
***"Dead."***:
*"Then... it's over and my death wasn't in vain. I owe you a great deal, Nightingale."*

From here, you will have the option of three replies:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ***"I did this for Nocturnal."*** | ***"I did this to honor the Guild."*** | ***"I did this to get rich."*** |
| *"That's quite a noble sentiment for someone in our... well, in your line of work."* | *"You've done the Guild a great deed. And although they may not show it, I'm certain they appreciate your sacrifices."* | *"Were I able to provide it, I'd shower you in wealth for what you've done."* |

No matter which option you choose to reply with, Gallus will have the same response:

*"My only regret is that you had to undertake this task alone."*
***"Karliah helped me."***
*"Karliah... she's still alive? I feared she'd befallen the same fate, ending up a victim of Mercer's betrayal."*
***"Then take the Key and right all the wrongs."***
*"Nothing would bring me more pride than to return the Key, but I'm afraid it's impossible. From the moment I arrived here, I've felt myself... well... dying."*
***"How can a spirit die?"***
*"The Sepulcher isn't merely a temple or a vault to house the Key. Within these walls is the Ebonmere... a conduit to Nocturnal's realm of [Evergloam](/wiki/Lore:Evergloam "Lore:Evergloam"). When Mercer stole the Key, that conduit closed, severely limiting our ties to her."*
***"Then I'll have to proceed alone."***
*"I'm afraid so. I'm weakening, and I can feel myself slipping away. The years without restoration of my power have taken their toll. Whatever damage has been caused can only be corrected by following the Pilgrim's Path to the Ebonmere and replacing the Key."*

If you inquire further about the Pilgrim's Path, Gallus will say *"I wish I could help you, but I've been a prisoner in this very chamber for the last quarter century. The only possible help I've come across are the remains of some poor fellow who was trying to follow in your footsteps. Perhaps his journal can help?"* This will present you with an optional goal to retrieve [Nystrom's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Nystrom%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Nystrom's Journal"), which contains clues about the five "tests" you will face along the way. The journal is found on [Nystrom's remains](/wiki/Skyrim:Nystrom "Skyrim:Nystrom") on the east side of the chamber, along with a leveled, enchanted weapon.

### The First Test

|  |
| --- |
| ***"Shadows of their former selves, sentinels of the dark. They wander ever more and deal swift death to defilers."*** |

Nightingale Sentinels in the room of the first test

Continue into the Sepulcher. In the first chamber, you will notice two Nightingale Sentinels reside here. One will be found in a room to the left, along with an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") and a secret chamber. The door to the secret chamber can be opened by pressing a button found behind the table. The other Sentinel can be found wandering near the steps in the main room. Starting a fight risks gaining the attention of both of them, so you can either choose to fight or try your luck in sneaking past them.

Proceed onward into the next hallway, being mindful of the [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") in the hallway. On top of the stairs ahead, there is another Sentinel keeping watch. Note that the stairs themselves are pitch-black, but do not have any traps. Be careful however: if you use any form of light, it will likely attract the Sentinel.

### The Second Test

|  |
| --- |
| ***"Above all they stand, vigilance everlasting. Beholden to the murk yet contentious of the glow."*** |

The darkened room of the second test

The next chamber (and the second test you will face) is a room with brightly lit areas and a shadowy path running through them. Stick to the shadows here, since stepping into the light will result in continuous health damage that can quickly kill you. Note that if you're trying to level [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"), this is a good place to do so; it is impossible to resist the damage (even with console commands or the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts")) as the damage caused by the light is scripted and will drain your health **very** rapidly (up to 100 points of damage per second) regardless of your level. The light damage is also affected by game difficulty, so be especially cautious if you are playing at higher difficulties. There are several [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire")-triggered [dart traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") along the shadowy path: the first one can be found as you make your way up the first flight of stairs, across the landing just ahead of you; the second tripwire is located just before you descend the second flight of stairs; the third tripwire is found just before you travel across a wooden bridge; the last one is located at the top of the last remaining stairs descending down.

Once you reach the end of the chamber, proceed onward through the hallway until you reach the next room.

### The Third Test

|  |
| --- |
| ***"Offer what She desires most, but reject the material. For her greatest want is that which cannot be seen, felt or carried."*** |

A statue of Nocturnal in the room of the third test

The third chamber is located at the end of the hallway, and contains a statue of [Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:Nocturnal "Skyrim:Nocturnal"), a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(dead)#Dunmer_Male "Skyrim:Bandit (dead)") found on the floor, and a wooden tray with an offering of gold and soul gems. The third test along the Pilgrim's Path requires you to give Nocturnal an offering she desires: *Darkness*. In order to do so, find the chains hidden behind the stone torches on either side. Pulling both chains will put out the flames, creating darkness. This will cause a hidden passage to open from behind the statue, leading to a corridor and your fourth test.

### The Fourth Test

|  |
| --- |
| ***"Direct and yet indirect. The path to salvation a route of cunning with fortune betraying the foolish."*** |

The two paths in the room of the fourth test

The corridor that lies ahead has a path leading directly through to a door. However, this path contains multiple traps, including two pressure plates (which both trigger darts to be released from the ceiling) and a [pendulum trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades"). If you choose to brave the pendulum trap, beware: at the end there is another pressure plate to the right which triggers a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") from multiple sides of the room. Opening the door ahead releases a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram") from behind the door.

You can also choose to avoid that path by going through a master-locked door (easily opened with use of the [Skeleton Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton_Key "Skyrim:Skeleton Key")), which is located to the left side just before the pendulum trap. This path leads to a small chamber which has two Nightingale Sentinels guarding the area. This area also contains a copy of the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") skill book *[Proper Lock Design](/wiki/Skyrim:Proper_Lock_Design "Skyrim:Proper Lock Design")* (on the table near the southeast corner of the room), some gold, several bottles of [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), and other minor loot. A copy of the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") skill book *[Sacred Witness](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacred_Witness "Skyrim:Sacred Witness")* may be on the table near the altar on the northwest side (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

You may now continue through the corridors until you reach the door leading into the [Twilight Sepulcher Inner Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Twilight_Sepulcher_Inner_Sanctum "Skyrim:Twilight Sepulcher Inner Sanctum").

### The Final Test

|  |
| --- |
| ***"The journey is complete, the Empress's embrace awaits the fallen. Hesitate not if you wish to gift her your eternal devotion."*** |

Returning the Skeleton Key to its rightful place

Proceed unopposed down a hallway and through a second set of doors, opening into a room with a well. It is advisable to save before jumping in due to a large number of potential [bugs](#Bugs). You may suffer a small amount of health damage from the fall. Examine the skeletal remains of [Anders](/wiki/Skyrim:Anders "Skyrim:Anders"), the thief who is mentioned in Nystrom's [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Nystrom%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Nystrom's Journal"). A cutscene is triggered shortly afterwards, and the floor of the well descends to reveal a room with three closed doors and a lock at your feet (which requires the Skeleton Key). Use the key to re-open the Ebonmere. Nocturnal will then emerge from the Ebonmere.

Nocturnal emerging from the Ebonmere

**Nocturnal:** *"My, my. What do we have here? It's been a number of years since I've set foot on your world. Or perhaps it's been moments. One tends to lose track. So... once again the Key has been stolen and a "champion" returns it to the Sepulcher. Now that Ebonmere has been restored, you stand before me awaiting your accolades; a pat on your head... a kiss on your cheek. What you fail to realize is your actions were expected and represent nothing more than the fulfillment of your agreement. Don't mistake my tone for displeasure, after all, you've obediently performed your duties to the letter. But we both know this has little to do with honor and oaths and loyalty. It's about the reward; the prize. Fear not. You'll have your trinkets, your desire for power, your hunger for wealth. I bid you to drink deeply from the Ebonmere, mortal. For this is where the Agent of Nocturnal is born. The Oath has been struck, the die has been cast and your fate awaits you in the Evergloam. Farewell, Nightingale. See to it the Key stays this time, won't you?"*

You are now directed to speak with [Karliah](/wiki/Skyrim:Karliah "Skyrim:Karliah"), who has appeared inside the Sepulcher.

*"I'm glad you were able to bring the Key back safely. Nocturnal seemed quite pleased with your efforts."*
***"Pleased? She sounded indifferent."***:
*"I wouldn't take that to heart. It's her way. Think of her as a scolding mother continually pushing you harder to be successful; outwardly sounding angry but silently content. I assure you, had she been displeased with you, we wouldn't be having this conversation."*
***"What's this about becoming an Agent of Nocturnal?"***:
*"The circles at the base of the Ebonmere imbue you with powers befitting a Nightingale Agent. The crescent moon represents the Agent of Shadow, the half moon for the Agent of Subterfuge and the full moon for the Agent of Strife."*

Now you are able to select either of the three Agents of Nocturnal:

- **[Agent of Shadow](/wiki/Skyrim:Agent_of_Stealth "Skyrim:Agent of Stealth")** (Crescent Moon) - Use this power to be invisible for 2 minutes while sneaking.

:   *"The Agent of Stealth is the master of remaining unseen. They are able to manipulate the darkness and use it to their advantage.*
:   *On moonlit nights or in darkened rooms, this agent literally becomes invisible."*

- **[Agent of Subterfuge](/wiki/Skyrim:Agent_of_Subterfuge "Skyrim:Agent of Subterfuge")** (Half Moon) - Use this power to cause all nearby enemies to fight each other for 30 seconds.

:   *"The Agent of Subterfuge utilizes shadow to cloud the judgement of those around him.*
:   *By weaving the darkness to their will, this agent can manipulate others into fighting for the Nightingale for a limited time."*

- **[Agent of Strife](/wiki/Skyrim:Agent_of_Strife "Skyrim:Agent of Strife")** (Full Moon) - Use this power to invoke a powerful life-drain effect.

:   *"This*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *Agent of Strife can send forth a tendril of pure darkness into the heart of another, causing great injury to them.*
:   *At the same time, this tether will bolster the agent's own life force, making him stronger.""*

If you ask Karliah why you cannot be all three Agents at once, she will respond with *"This is Nocturnal's way of maintaining balance. If you ever feel the need to change your abilities, you can return to the Sepulcher and step onto a different circle. Be warned that once you've chosen, you can't reselect for at least a day."*

***"So what now?"***
*"Now, your life as a Nightingale begins. Should the need arise, you'll be summoned to the Sepulcher in order to defend it."*
***"And you?"***
*"The Guild has welcomed me back with open arms. I feel like a void in my life has finally been filled. I only hope that this isn't an ending to things, but actually the beginning."*
***"The beginning of what?"***
*"Why, perhaps the greatest crime spree Skyrim's ever known. There are pockets brimming with coin and coffers overflowing with riches ripe for the picking. We may be Nightingales, but in our hearts we're still thieves and we're damn good at what we do."*

You can now return to the [Nightingale Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Hall "Skyrim:Nightingale Hall") and use it as a home if you wish. Karliah will also reside there. Before you leave the Twilight Sepulcher however, there is a short cutscene where Gallus appears and speaks to Karliah before entering the Evergloam.

Karliah's final farewell to Gallus

**Gallus:** *"Karliah?"*
**Karliah:** *"Gallus! I feared I would never see you again. I was afraid you'd become like the others."*
**Gallus:** *"If it were not for the actions of this Nightingale, your fears would have come true. He/She honors us all."*
**Karliah:** *"What will you do now, my love?"*
**Gallus:** *"Nocturnal calls me to the Evergloam. My contract has been fulfilled."*
**Karliah:** *"Will I ever see you again?"*
**Gallus:** *"When your debt to Nocturnal has been paid, we'll embrace once again."*
**Karliah:** *"Farewell, Gallus. Eyes open... walk with the shadows."*
**Gallus:** *"Goodbye, Karliah."*

Approaching Karliah again and asking where Gallus went, she will respond by saying:

*"Gallus's Oath has been paid. His actions have satisfied the terms. Now his spirit becomes one with the Evergloam... the realm of perpetual twilight and the cradle of shadow."*
***"So, he's gone?"***
*"No, not gone... he's become one with the shadows. This is the greatest honor a Nightingale can possibly achieve. In death, he's become a part of that which we use to live."*
***"They're a part of the darkness around us?"***
*"Absolutely. When we say "walk with the shadows," we are asking those Nightingales who have passed on to protect us. It's believed that they are literally what guides our uncanny luck... by placing their hands in ours. That's why the Ebonmere needed to be reopened. Without it, there's no way Nocturnal was able to allow them through."*
***"How will I know if I'm needed here?"***
*"If this place is in danger ever again, the shadows will call. Should the need arise, a portal connects the Sepulcher and Nightingale Hall. Use it whenever you wish."*

To exit the [Sepulcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Twilight_Sepulcher "Skyrim:Twilight Sepulcher"), you can enter any of the three portals surrounding the Ebonmere. The portals will take you directly to the entrance of the Sepulcher, and if you look back, you will notice that the path that once led to the Pilgrim's Path now has a portal which will take you directly to the [Inner Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Twilight_Sepulcher_Inner_Sanctum "Skyrim:Twilight Sepulcher Inner Sanctum").

### Returning Home

Once you've returned to the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(place) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (place)"), [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf") will greet you by remarking, *"It's good to see you in one piece lad/lass!"* He will then go on to say: *"I just wanted to give you a proper thank you for everything you've done. The Guild is back on its feet again and on its way to a prosperous future."* He will also ask about the Skeleton Key. When you say that you've returned it back to the Sepulcher, Brynjolf will reply: *"That's it then. After all of those years of helplessly watching the Guild decline. But enough of that... I'm confident that with you in charge, we'll soon have more gold than we could possibly spend."* Asking where he will be from now on will cause him to say: *"I'll be down here, trying to coordinate everything with Delvin and Vex; to make sure the coin keeps flowing... and no one skims! If you still feel like doing some jobs, I'm sure Delvin and Vex have more than their fair share to give out. Either way, it's been a pleasure, my friend. Here's to the future of the Guild. May it last another thousand years!"*

If you have already completed the reputation quests, then you can now complete [Under New Management](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_New_Management "Skyrim:Under New Management"), the last main quest available for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"). However, you are still able to complete [jobs](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Special_Job_quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") given by either [Delvin](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") or [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex").

## Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked when you complete this quest:

-  **Darkness Returns** (10 points/Bronze)

## Notes

- The completion of this quest will remove the [Skeleton Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton_Key "Skyrim:Skeleton Key") from your inventory permanently.
- You cannot bring [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") into the [Twilight Sepulcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Twilight_Sepulcher "Skyrim:Twilight Sepulcher") with you, though the standard reminder may fail to appear.
- If you already have Nystrom's journal when you get the objective to retrieve it, re-read the book to complete the objective.
- Because there is now a portal from the Sepulcher entrance to the Inner Sanctum, the Pilgrim's Path becomes permanently inaccessible after the quest is completed.

## Bugs

- [Gallus's Encoded Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallus%27s_Encoded_Journal "Skyrim:Gallus's Encoded Journal") cannot be removed from your inventory after the quest is completed.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9.26.0.8, fixes this bug.
  -  The following console command will fix this: `player.removeitem CEDA6 1`.
  -  Alternatively, if you wish to keep it, using `player.drop CEDA6 1` will drop the journal and not delete it.
- Entering the Twilight Sepulcher, hearing the first of Gallus's dialogue, and then leaving will cause the door to the Pilgrim's Path to stay closed and never open upon returning. This will be caused by "Nightingale Sentinel" being replaced with "Gallus" after exiting dialogue with him. Speaking with the "Gallus" version of the sentinel with all topics will *not* cause the door to open because he does not have the proper permissions. **?**
  - Solution: If you go to the right around the door of the Pilgrim's Path, you will see a glitched area that can appear blue. You will also see the inside of the Pilgrim's Path. Use the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") shout to jump the gap and gain entrance to the path. Falling will either return you to the entrance area or kill you, depending on how you fall. The objective will not reappear until you talk to Nocturnal near the end of the quest.
- After going through the well and dropping into the main chamber, Karliah may not show up at all, show up and leave promptly, or show up late. It may help to wait a few hours before dropping into the well in order to have Karliah show up. It may also be helpful to NOT loot Anders upon dropping into the well. Karliah needs to be present for the whole conversation with Nocturnal, so ensure you save the game prior to dropping into the well and load up each time until it works properly. As the conversation ends, she may try to leave, so ensure that you are next to her and ready to speak as soon as Nocturnal goes away and your quest updates to "Speak with Karliah". If the quest doesn't update after Nocturnal tells you to drink from the Ebonmere, simply wait a few hours and the quest should update. **?**
  -  If Karliah is not showing up, it may be possible to finish the quest with the console, though the first course of action should always be to reload an earlier save. While Nocturnal speaks, move Karliah to you with the moveto player command: `prid 1B07F` then `moveto player` Never use the placeatme command, as that just spawns a duplicate, not the actual unique NPC, and it will likely result in issues and actual game breakage further along. When Nocturnal is finished, you may need to update the quest with `setstage TG09 60`.
- This quest may halt after you are able to receive one of the three abilities and Karliah has spoken to Gallus. Her dialogue says she will return to Nightingale Hall, but she stays there for 24 hours, then ends up in Snow Veil Sanctum. She also states that a portal will exist in Nightingale Hall, but none is there; in fact, nothing changes at all. Brynjolf shows up in the Thieves Guild (with his old Thieves Guild gear on, not the Nightingale gear) but just says "I'm busy, talk to me later." **?**
-  At the end of the quest, after Nocturnal speaks to you, you're instructed to speak to Karliah. However, in some cases all she says is "Yes, fellow Nightingale?" and gives no dialogue options. **?**
  - This seems to be caused by completing [Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers") a second time.
  - It helps to wait for a few hours after inserting the key. The game will reload upon completion of the wait with Karliah where she needs to be.
- Although Karliah says at the end of the quest that henceforth a portal connects the Sepulcher and Nightingale Hall, this portal is hard to find or nonexistent. **?**
- When you pull the chain next to the Nocturnal Statue during the third test, the lights will go out but the door will remain shut. **?**
- The *[Sacred Witness](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacred_Witness "Skyrim:Sacred Witness")* skill book may not be present. If you read the book in either of the Dark Brotherhood Sanctuaries, the one here will disappear.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Darkness Returns (TG09) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | With the Skeleton Key of Nocturnal safely in my possession, I'm bound for the Twilight Sepulcher to return it to its resting place. *Objective 10:* Enter the Twilight Sepulcher |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Speak to the Nightingale Sentinel  *Objective 25:* (Optional) Retrieve Nystrom's Journal *(if you followed the [appropriate](#Objective25) dialogue choices)* |
| 30 |  | Within the Twilight Sepulcher, I happened upon the spirit of Gallus, the Nightingale murdered by Mercer Frey. He warned me that removing the key from its resting place has corrupted the other resident Nightingale Guardian Spirits, distorting their morality and making them incredibly hostile. *Objective 30:* Follow the Pilgrim's Path |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Return the Skeleton Key to the Ebonmere |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Listen to Nocturnal |
| 60 |  | *Objective 60:* Speak to Karliah |
| 70 |  | *Objective 70:* Choose Nightingale Role |
| 200 | ☑ | I've returned the Skeleton Key to its proper resting place within the Twilight Sepulcher and encountered Nocturnal herself. As a reward for my actions, she allowed me to become a true Nightingale Agent and imbued me with the appropriate ability befitting my station. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 45.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TG09 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TG09`.

# Skyrim:Darkshade

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

Darkshade

**Darkshade** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll"). It contains only one zone, *[Darkshade](#Darkshade)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(B) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (B)")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear out a beast den. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The entrance to Darkshade is easily spotted due to it being on the bank of the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River") near the base of the waterfall east of [Valtheim Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Valtheim_Towers "Skyrim:Valtheim Towers"). A collapsed wooden platform is just to the right of the entrance. The cave appears to have been either a bandit lair or a mine before being attacked by the trolls who now inhabit the cavern. The corpses of a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_(dead) "Skyrim:Nord (dead)") lie in front of the entrance. A [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") and a fallen tree with a second dead Nord leaning against it are to the right of the entrance. The tree stump slightly farther along the bank has a patch of [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") growing on it. There is also a patch each of [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") and [red mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") on a small island in the middle of the river opposite the entrance.

### Darkshade

Darkshade interior

The entrance leads into a short tunnel, which takes a couple of turns and has gory humanoid remains scattered along its length before opening out into a chamber which contains what was once a campsite with a troll lurking about. There is a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") and a [fur cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor") on the ground, on the left as you enter the chamber. Immediately on your left when entering this chamber is a collapsed table, with an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), an [iron greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword"), a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), three [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks, and a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") concealed by a fern, that all seem to have fallen from it. The chamber is overrun with flora, but little that can be harvested. There are four unowned bedrolls on the ground and on the right is an earthen ramp leading up and around to a ledge behind some broken wooden scaffolding. There is a gold ore vein on the rear wall (see [bugs](#Bugs)), another pickaxe on the ground, near a tree stump, which has a patch of mora tapinella growing on it. By the broken scaffold is a broken table with an empty [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"), a [thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle"), a sheaf of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") on top. A [dead Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_(NPC) "Skyrim:Argonian (NPC)") can be found lying under an evergreen tree, with a passage heading north to the left of it. To the southwest is another fur cuirass, a pair of [fur shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Shoes "Skyrim:Fur Shoes"), a [deer hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Hide "Skyrim:Deer Hide"), and six food sacks scattered among humanoid detritus. High on the wall is a small ledge, which you can use as a shortcut back to the exit.

After a few paces the passage turns to the east, there is an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace") by a lit lantern on the ground. There is another troll roaming the next chamber, which contains a gold ore vein on a raised section to the northeast. There is a [dead Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf_(dead) "Skyrim:Wood Elf (dead)") to the west under another ledge with an earthen ramp leading up to it. The cave system continues to the north and after another short passage opens out into another chamber. It contains two trolls, one wandering up and down a series of ramps on your right and the other backwards and forwards along the far side of a stream bank to the left. The stream is formed by a waterfall falling down the cavern wall to the west. Climbing the ramps on the east side of the cavern leads to another narrow passage and a small chamber containing a dead [goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat"), a dead bandit, and a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") covered in blood.

Returning to the larger chamber, the stream forms a pool at this end, which appears empty, with paths along both banks. The northern bank has several piles of firewood, one of which has a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on top. With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") can be found here; fish from [Underground](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity)#Biomes "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)") waters can be caught here. On the left of this path is a huge tree stump with a patch of mora tapinella growing on it. Just beyond this are some support beams and an old extinguished campfire. The second of the trolls will be found in this area. There is a round wooden table holding a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") and a [dead rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), with two baskets on the ground nearby; one holds two fillets of [horker meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat"). Beyond these is an unowned bedroll with an iron mace beside it, as well as a copy of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Orsinium and the Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orsinium_and_the_Orcs "Skyrim:Orsinium and the Orcs")* and a gold ore vein also on the ground nearby. There is an empty ledge along the north wall that can be reached via rocks to the right of the waterfall.

The southern bank of the stream has an overturned cart that contained a pickaxe and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), among several shovels. There is another ledge along part of the southern wall with only a broken tree trunk and an empty brazier stand on top. To the left of the waterfall is a dead bandit, beside which is a leveled health, magicka, or stamina [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") and a leveled [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer"). A [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") is also hidden in the vegetation. There is a passage heading south, which has a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on the ground along it. This leads to a final chamber containing one more troll. Opposite to the south is a ledge with a passage heading away. In front of this is a dead [elk](/wiki/Skyrim:Elk "Skyrim:Elk") and a [dead Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_(dead) "Skyrim:Redguard (dead)"). This chamber is full of many bones and skulls from humanoids, mammoths, and other animals. By the start of the ramp leading up to the ledge is a [dead Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf_(dead) "Skyrim:Dark Elf (dead)"). At the top, to the right of the passage, is an unlocked boss chest, with five loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on the ground around it.

## Notes

- The world map refers to this location as "Darkshade", but the local map and entries in your journal refer to it as "Darkshade Copse".

## Bugs

- Although Darkshade is geographically located within the borders of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"), in the game data it is identified as being within [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, fixes this bug.
- You may not be able to mine the exterior gold ore vein.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- You may not be able to mine the gold ore vein in the first chamber, even after leaving and re-entering the cave.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.

## Maps

  Darkshade

Darkwater Crossing

**Darkwater Crossing** is a small mining [settlement](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") south of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

[Annekke Crag-Jumper](/wiki/Skyrim:Annekke_Crag-Jumper "Skyrim:Annekke Crag-Jumper") and her husband [Verner Rock-Chucker](/wiki/Skyrim:Verner_Rock-Chucker "Skyrim:Verner Rock-Chucker") originally discovered [corundum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") here and established what would become [Goldenrock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenrock_Mine "Skyrim:Goldenrock Mine"). They built themselves a [small house](/wiki/Skyrim:Verner_and_Annekke%27s_House "Skyrim:Verner and Annekke's House"), planted wheat and vegetables, and raised chickens and a goat. Since then, the mine has attracted several new residents who have made camp outside its entrance. The miners constantly worry that the mine may be running out of ore. Two of the residents, Annekke and [Derkeethus](/wiki/Skyrim:Derkeethus "Skyrim:Derkeethus"), can become followers and be chosen as [candidates to join](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades") the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") can be found next to the water, along with drying salmon and some netting.

The residents of Darkwater Crossing have unwittingly put themselves in danger by settling so close to [Darkwater Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Pass "Skyrim:Darkwater Pass"), a hidden [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer")-infested [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves"). Although one of the residents has already [gone missing](/wiki/Skyrim:Extracting_an_Argonian "Skyrim:Extracting an Argonian"), they are still unaware of this danger.

#### Miscellaneous Quests

- **[Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery")**: Deliver an item to an associate. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Extracting an Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Extracting_an_Argonian "Skyrim:Extracting an Argonian")**: Rescue [Derkeethus](/wiki/Skyrim:Derkeethus "Skyrim:Derkeethus") from his [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") captors.
- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader")**: Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

#### Miscellaneous Quests

- **[Special Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Delivery_(Sylgja) "Skyrim:Special Delivery (Sylgja)")**: Make a delivery for [Sylgja](/wiki/Skyrim:Sylgja "Skyrim:Sylgja") to Darkwater Crossing.

## Notes

- Unused game data indicates the settlement was originally intended to be much different than it appears in the final game.
  - An NPC named **Meieran** is referred to in conversation by Hrefna, Sondas, and Tormir. It appears he was intended to play a significant role in Hrefna's upbringing, and may have been meant to tend the crops in the settlement, something no one does in the final game.
  - Tormir mentions another nonexistent NPC named **Dasturn** in a greeting. Nothing else is known about this person.
  - Sondas was intended to be an innkeeper, rather than a miner, as shown by the internal name of his scenes with Tormir: `DialogueDarkwaterCrossingInn`. His outfit and class in the final game appear to be remnants of this plan. It also explains why Hrefna follows him and states that he watches over her while her mother works, as she was meant to stay with him at the inn. The name of this inn is unknown, but circumstantial evidence hints towards it being the **Roughwater Inn**. Also, the internal numbering of his inn scenes starts with 4, highly suggesting at least three scenes with other residents were removed.
  - Hrefna's scenes are numbered 1, 2, and 4, suggesting at least one scene was removed.
  - A [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Keys#Crossinghouse_Key "Skyrim:Keys") and location data indicate a dwelling known as **Crossinghouse** was also meant to appear here. Based on the remaining faction information and locklist, Hrefna and Tormir were meant to live there.
  - The (normally unseen) quest stages of Extracting an Argonian refer to Derkeethus as "one of the fisherman *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*", implying there were meant to be more. Another quest stage also implies Derkeethus had his own house at the settlement, which is something that no remaining game data corroberates.
  - An unused collection of scenes containing no data is named `FishingHoleScenes`. It's possible that this "fishing hole" was another completely removed location, but it might also just be the name for the collection of scenes involving the fishermen. It at least implies that there were to be multiple, and that they would've had scenes with each other while working.
- As can be seen by their Form IDs, the miners at Darkwater Crossing were created before Annekke and Verner. Moreover, the miners never interact with Annekke or Verner or acknowledge them in dialogue, and the reverse is also the case.
- There is a [random encounter](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions") spawn-point southeast of Darkwater Crossing, just behind the mine. If the random encounter includes hostiles, they may wander into the town and start attacking the residents.
- According to the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") soldier [Ralof](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralof "Skyrim:Ralof"), Darkwater Crossing was the scene of the [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") ambush that led to the capture of himself, [Gunjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunjar "Skyrim:Gunjar"), and [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"). [Lokir](/wiki/Skyrim:Lokir "Skyrim:Lokir") was captured here as well.
  - None of the residents here mention the ambush, and you cannot ask them about it.
- Darkwater Crossing also [appears](/wiki/Online:Darkwater_Crossing "Online:Darkwater Crossing") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | |

| South-southwest of [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") Northeast of [Nilheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilheim "Skyrim:Nilheim") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Arcane Enchanters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") | 1 |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore") | 1 |
| # of [Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") | 1 |

Darkwater Pass

**Darkwater Pass** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") south-southwest of [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). It contains only one zone, *[Darkwater Pass](#Darkwater_Pass)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Extracting an Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Extracting_an_Argonian "Skyrim:Extracting an Argonian")**: Rescue [Derkeethus](/wiki/Skyrim:Derkeethus "Skyrim:Derkeethus") from his [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") captors.

### Exterior

To find the cave, leave Darkwater Crossing via the bridge heading southwest, on the far side take the road leading northwest toward [Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol"), and follow the path marked by a pile of rocks on your left shortly before reaching the next bridge. At the top the path forks, with the left (southeast) fork leading to the cave and the right (west) fork eventually leading to [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"). The cave entrance is marked by a statue with a lit brazier on top and a pair of iron doors flanked by Falmer totems. It is near a large waterfall along [Darkwater River](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_River "Skyrim:Darkwater River"), on the shore of a pool formed by the waterfall.

### Darkwater Pass

As soon as you enter, you are in a narrow partially flooded tunnel heading roughly north. There is a mist or fog in the air making visibility even worse. Use of [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)") or the [Aura Whisper](/wiki/Skyrim:Aura_Whisper "Skyrim:Aura Whisper") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") is very useful in this cave. After a short distance, the tunnel turns to the west, with an [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the turning. The tunnel opens into a cave, with the ground rising to the right toward a [Falmer hive](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Hive "Skyrim:Falmer Hive") that conceals a Falmer. Ahead are a stone bridge and platform, similar to those found in [Nordic ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins").

Crossing the bridge, you will see a large partially flooded chamber ahead, with a leveled Falmer wandering near a Falmer tent with another Falmer inside. In the distance, there is a waterfall falling down the far wall of the chamber, and several varieties of fish are swimming in the water below the falls. To the north is another tunnel. Next to the waterfall is an unlocked Falmer chest, and it is possible to climb the left side of the cave to reach a lit brazier with a random healing potion beside it (good mountain climbing skills required), opposite to this is a ledge with another healing potion which can be accessed by using whirlwind sprint. On the north wall of the cave, to the left of the tunnel is a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein"), and on the ground in front of it is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"). As you enter the tunnel to the north, the ceiling becomes vaulted with pillars supporting it every few paces; there are three leveled chaurus in hiding ready to ambush you behind the pillars. There are several [chaurus egg sacs](/wiki/Skyrim:Egg_Sacs "Skyrim:Egg Sacs") in this area and also throughout the rest of the cave. In front of the east wall of the vaulted chamber is a ledge holding two [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"), an urn, and an apprentice-locked wooden chest. The path continues to the north, up a flight of wide stairs.

At the top, the tunnel turns to the west again and climbs more stairs. At the top, you enter a room with a large trap door in the floor under which [Derkeethus](/wiki/Skyrim:Derkeethus "Skyrim:Derkeethus") will be trapped during the quest [Extracting an Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Extracting_an_Argonian "Skyrim:Extracting an Argonian") (see [bugs](#Bugs)). There are doorways to the west and south here. To the south you can hear and see a Falmer wandering about. Take care as there are two Falmer hives in the same room, both of which conceal leveled Falmer. The room is circular and the walls have indented shelves all around. Two of these shelves hold random [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"), and another has a leveled [potion of the warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_the_Warrior "Skyrim:Potion of the Warrior"). There is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") at the rear of the room with a copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Catalogue_of_Weapon_Enchantments "Skyrim:Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments")* and a random [aversion to shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Aversion_to_Shock "Skyrim:Weak Aversion to Shock") poison. Finally, behind the enchanter is an unlocked Falmer chest.

Back in the trap door room, there is a burial urn to the left of the west exit. There are also three alcoves in the northern wall. The left alcove houses an urn, a random healing potion and a [coin](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") are on the floor in front of the center alcove, and the right alcove has a lever that opens a hidden door.

To reach Derkeethus, pull the lever to open the hidden door, behind which you will find a wooden spiral staircase. Take the staircase down to the bottom where there is an unlocked wooden chest. A doorway in the west wall opens onto a short corridor with a loose [chaurus egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs") on the floor. This corridor heads south to a locked gate with a small circular room beyond. This circular room - the prison cell for Derkeethus - is called "Darkwater Pit". Shortly before the gate on the left side of the corridor is another burial urn. The pit is directly beneath the trap door and contains a few steps leading down to a shallow pool of water. Another chest and three more burial urns are in the cell. In one of the three burial urns is the [Darkwater Pit key](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Pit_Key "Skyrim:Darkwater Pit Key"), which will open the cage, but oddly, you have to open the cage to reach the urn with the key or, alternately, reach through the gaps in the gate to open the urn and take the key.

Final chamber

The path to the west climbs a wooden spiraling ramp with several [glowing mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") growing on the central pillar. The room at the top has stairs ahead, with a balcony along the rear of the room. There is a Falmer standing opposite where you enter to the right of a clearly trapped corridor. You can see a [claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Claw "Skyrim:Claw") trap hinged above the doorway. To the right of the stairs is a lever which triggers both the claw you can see and a second claw hinged on the ground. There is a burial urn near where the Falmer stands, and a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") is in the doorway, serving as another trigger for the claw traps. To the south, there is a doorway leading into a narrow corridor heading up stairs. On your right is an alcove containing two urns, one of which is broken. There are two random healing potions beside the urns. By a lit brazier the corridor turns to the west and continues to climb. Near the top it turns north then almost immediately back to the west. Ahead is another chamber.

There are several leveled Falmer in and near this chamber, including one concealed in a hive. There is a flight of stairs descending against the west wall, with another flight ascending from the bottom of these. At the top is a leveled Falmer who is patrolling the top of the stairs. From the top of those stairs, it is a short drop to access the lower of the two doorways at the rear of the room. Dropping down into the water and entering the doorway, take the first turn on the left and then immediately left again to find a stone table with an unlocked wooden chest and two burial urns. In front is a small waterfall dropping into a pool to the left of the stairs before dropping over the large waterfall to the east into the first large chamber. To the left of this waterfall is a Falmer hive on the wall with a concealed Falmer inside.

Opposite this is a bank sloping up from the water to the rear of the chamber. There is another leveled Falmer on this path. At the rear of the room you will see two doorways with wooden planking walls to the left of them; there is another Falmer standing behind these. Near the top of the ramp, you pass another claw on the right wall at head height, with the tripwire a few paces past it. Beyond this point, the architecture is decidedly Nordic. The tunnel climbs a few more stairs and then turns to the west again and then back on itself to the north. This is where the Falmer that was behind the wooden planking is standing, unless you have already dealt with him. The path passes the wooden wall seen from the other side; at the end is a large metal bowl with a chaurus egg sac growing in it. There is also a loose chaurus egg on the floor, and two more are inside the bowl. The path turns back to the south, and stairs lead up to iron doors that allow you to exit the cave.

## Notes

- In the water just outside the exit about 30 feet to the right, there is a skeleton with a random [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"), [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Helmets "Skyrim:Armor"), [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Shields "Skyrim:Armor"), [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor"), and [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") lying around; this person appears to have been murdered, as the skeleton is tied to a stone block.
- There is no map marker for the exit, which is west of the entrance marker and north of [Nilheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilheim "Skyrim:Nilheim") on the shore of a small pond.

## Bugs

- Derkeethus may decide to follow you to the door but refuse to exit. Reloading older saves does not seem to fix this issue.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.
  -  A workaround is to exit the cave and use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") commands `prid 0001B08D` and `moveto player` then talk to him, which should finish the quest.
  - Another solution is to push him as close to the exit as possible, then leave the cave; he should follow you outside.
- The cave interior is flagged as an outdoor area; therefore, it cannot be used for shelter from sunlight if you are a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire").
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.7.7.6, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Darkwater River

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Body of Water: Darkwater River ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darkwater+River)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Darkwater_River "Lore:Darkwater River")) | | |
| Regions | |
| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"), [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | |
| Location | |
| Between [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") and [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") | |

Darkwater River

The **Darkwater River** is a river connecting [Lake Geir](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Geir "Skyrim:Lake Geir") to the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River").

The source of the river is Lake Geir at the western end of [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"). The river flows into [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") to join the White River south-southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

## Walkthrough

The Darkwater River, or simply the Darkwater, is a river in eastern Skyrim connecting Lake Geir to the White River. The lake feeds into the river near [Nilheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilheim "Skyrim:Nilheim") in the western Rift. The river flows northeast into Eastmarch, cascading down the cliff which divides the two holds. After a series of pools and waterfalls, the river bends northwest near [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") and merges with the White River a few miles downstream, south-southwest of Windhelm and west of the fetid bogs of Eastmarch. Forts, ruins, caves, and major roads line its banks, and the fishing is said to be good.

A large tributary flows separately from Lake Geir. It passes north through [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"), curves northeast to create its own series of waterfalls down the cliff, and connects with the Darkwater River in Eastmarch near [Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol") shortly before the main river merges with the White River.

# Skyrim:Dawnguard (NPC)

## Overview

A generic member of the Dawnguard

**Dawnguard** are radiant members of the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). They are randomly encountered in the wilderness and, if you are a member of [Harkon's](/wiki/Skyrim:Harkon "Skyrim:Harkon") [court](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan"), are hostile toward you.

They attack in groups of three and can appear upon fast traveling to a location. If you are a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"), they will attack on sight. These assassins will continue to appear even if the Dawnguard [questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Quests#Main_Quests "Skyrim:Dawnguard Quests") has been completed.

Two Dawnguard appear along with Durak to start the quest "Dawnguard".

Typically, they wear either a set of [Dawnguard armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Armor "Skyrim:Dawnguard Armor") or heavy Dawnguard armor and are armed with a [crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Crossbow "Skyrim:Crossbow") and a [Dawnguard warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Warhammer "Skyrim:Dawnguard Warhammer") or a [Dawnguard war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_War_Axe "Skyrim:Dawnguard War Axe"). They may also carry small amounts of gold and minor random loot.

The vampire threat increases

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Reach level 10 and be approached by [Durak](/wiki/Skyrim:Durak "Skyrim:Durak").
2. Hear about the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)") vampire hunters.
3. Locate [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard").
4. Speak to [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran") and [Vigilant Tolan](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilant_Tolan "Skyrim:Vigilant Tolan").

### Find out about the Dawnguard

.jpg)

The destroyed Hall of the Vigilant

If your level is 10 or above an [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") named [Durak](/wiki/Skyrim:Durak "Skyrim:Durak") will find and approach you with a proposal to join the Dawnguard: *"You there. The Dawnguard is looking for anyone willing to fight against the growing vampire menace. What do you say?"*. The miscellaneous journal objective "Find out about the Dawnguard" will appear, and if you ask him to explain, he'll tell you that they are a group of [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") hunters. He'll mention that the [Hall of the Vigilants](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Vigilant "Skyrim:Hall of the Vigilant") was destroyed by vampires because the [Vigilants](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilants_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilants of Stendarr") didn't take the vampire threat seriously. If you ask him what he's talking about, he'll tell you they got torn to pieces when they went up against the vampires, and that's why his leader [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran") is reestablishing the Dawnguard. When you ask how to sign up, Durak will tell you to talk to Isran at Fort Dawnguard, southeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). If you didn't hear the rumor (see below) from a guard already, your map will now be updated, and the quest [Dawnguard](#Dawnguard) will officially appear in your journal, completing this short miscellaneous quest.

If you happen to tell Durak you're not interested in being recruited, he'll say *"That's what everybody says, right up until they find their throat being ripped out by a pack of hungry vampires."* and the conversation will end. If you approach him a second time, he'll respond *"Yeah, you change your mind? The Dawnguard could use somebody like you."* and the other dialogue options are the same as the first time around. If you tell him you're not interested this time, he'll tell you to talk to Isran and give you the location of Fort Dawnguard anyway, in case you change your mind.

Alternatively, you may start this quest in another manner, detailed below.

#### Find Fort Dawnguard

Fort Dawnguard

Upon installing the [Dawnguard add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), you may hear a new rumor from city [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Guards "Skyrim:Guards") regarding [the Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"): *"Heard they're reforming the Dawnguard. Vampire hunters or something, in the old fort near Riften. Might consider joining up myself."* If this is the first you've heard of the Dawnguard, your map will be updated with the location of [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard"), and the quest will officially appear in your journal.

Take the road that leads east from Riften. Right after the road turns southeast and you cross a small bridge, start watching the cliffs to your left. You'll find a small crack in the side of a cliff—the entrance to [Dayspring Canyon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dayspring_Canyon "Skyrim:Dayspring Canyon"). It's found between a hollow green log and a broken birch tree. A narrow, winding path leads you towards Fort Dawnguard. It is the only way to reach the fort until you discover the map marker.

Along the way, you may catch up to [Agmaer](/wiki/Skyrim:Agmaer "Skyrim:Agmaer"), another new recruit to the Dawnguard. If you haven't yet heard about the Dawnguard, his greeting will trigger the quest to appear in your journal: *"Oh, hey there! You here to join the Dawnguard, too?"* He expresses his anxiety concerning entering the fort on his own, and accompanies you the remainder of the way. He asks you not to mention his nervousness to Isran, but will make several comments expressing his low self-confidence as you make the walk. Despite his expressed fear of going in on his own, he will run inside the fort without waiting for you if you don't enter immediately after reaching the front steps to the entrance.

You may pass Durak just outside the fort, practicing his skill with a [crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Crossbow "Skyrim:Crossbow"). If you ask him what he's using, he'll answer *"Never seen a crossbow before? Not surprised. Kind of a Dawnguard specialty. Nothing better for putting down vampires."* He will then give you your own crossbow, along with 45 [steel bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Bolt "Skyrim:Steel Bolt") (see [notes](#Notes) below for how to get a second one).

When you reach the steps to the fort, you'll find [Celann](/wiki/Skyrim:Celann "Skyrim:Celann") guarding the entrance. If you choose to speak with him, he'll say he was surprised to hear from Isran at all, and comment that things must be pretty bad for Isran to request his help. If you ask Celann about working with Isran in the past, he'll tell you they were both members of the Vigilants of Stendarr, whose "hearts were in the right place" but left them both dissatisfied. The pair left together, but Celann didn't agree with Isran's "methods", so the partnership didn't last. On that note, he'll tell you *"Go on inside, Isran will want to talk to you."*

#### Join the Dawnguard

_02.jpg)

Isran and Tolan discussing the vampire attacks

_03.jpg)

*"You need to concentrate, boy. Try it again."*

Once inside, you'll find the Dawnguard leader, Isran, speaking to [Tolan](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilant_Tolan "Skyrim:Vigilant Tolan"), a priest of the Vigilant.

:   **Isran**: *"Why are you here, Tolan? The Vigilants and I were finished long ago."*
:   **Tolan**: *"You know why I'm here, the Vigilants are under attack everywhere. The vampires are much more dangerous than we believed."*
:   **Isran**: *"And now you want to come running to safety with the Dawnguard, is that it? I remember [Keeper Carcette](/wiki/Skyrim:Keeper_Carcette "Skyrim:Keeper Carcette") telling me repeatedly that Dawnguard is a crumbling ruin, not worth the expense and manpower to repair. And now that you've stirred up the vampires against you, you come begging for my protection?"*
:   **Tolan**: *"Isran, Carcette is dead. The Hall of Vigilants... everyone... they're all dead. You were right, we were wrong. Isn't that enough for you?"*
:   **Isran**: *"Yes, well... I never wanted any of this to happen. I tried to warn all of you... I am sorry, you know."*

At this point, Isran will turn to you, asking *"So who are you, what do you want?"* You can tell him you're just looking around and ask about the fort, to which he'll reply, *"Why do I even post guards? This is the headquarters of the Dawnguard. Well, it used to be, a long time ago."* If you tell him you've come to join the Dawnguard, or simply that you've heard about the vampire hunters, he'll be pleased that you're interested but comment that most of their work at the moment is going toward restoring the fort.

If you are already a fully transformed into a vampire when engaging for the first time in the conversation with Isran and you respond, "I heard you were looking for vampire hunters" Isran will reply "You heard right, I'm glad the word is finally starting to get around. But that means it won't be long until vampires start to take notice as well." If you reply, "What exactly are you planning to do to these vampires?" then Isran responds, "First thing is to get this Fort back into shape. Right now a vampire could practically walk right into the front door. But I have something for you to do since you're asking" and he goes on to talk about Dimhollow Crypt.

When you ask how you can help, he'll respond *"I need someone out in the field, taking the fight to the damn vampires, while we're getting the fort back into shape. Tolan was telling me about a cave some of the Vigilants were poking around in. Seemed to think it was..."* and ask Tolan to tell you about [Dimhollow Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Dimhollow_Crypt "Skyrim:Dimhollow Crypt"). Tolan will inform you that *"[Brother Adalvald](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilant_Adalvald "Skyrim:Vigilant Adalvald") was sure it held some long-lost vampire artifact of some kind. We didn't listen to him anymore than we did Isran. He was at the hall when it was attacked..."*

Isran will then assign your first task to you: *"Go see what the vampires were looking for in this Dimhollow Crypt. With any luck, they'll still be there."* Isran will then give you a crossbow and some steel bolts (if you haven't received them from Durak already), saying *"Here, you should take a crossbow. Good for taking out those fiends before they get close."* and then invite you to explore and take anything you need from Fort Dawnguard before sending you off on your mission. Before you leave, Tolan will offer to meet you at Dimhollow Crypt, saying *"It's the least I can do to avenge my fallen comrades."* Isran and Tolan will argue a bit, as Isran doesn't believe the Vigilants are trained for such a mission, and Tolan is offended at the implication that Isran thinks the Vigilants are soft, cowardly, and weak. He will stand by his decision, though, telling you *"I'm going to Dimhollow Crypt. Perhaps I can be of some small assistance to you."* The quest [Awakening](/wiki/Skyrim:Awakening "Skyrim:Awakening") begins immediately.

## Notes

- This quest cannot be started if you have a bounty in The Rift.
  - Pay your bounty, and the Dawnguard questline should begin like normal.
- After beginning this quest, the [Hall of the Vigilant](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Vigilant "Skyrim:Hall of the Vigilant") will be destroyed, regardless of your level. It also doesn't matter if you visited it beforehand or not.
  -  The Hall can be reverted to its original form by opening the console and entering the code `"xx003531".enable`.
- Several of the Dawnguard members are non-essential. If you wish to join the [Castle Volkihar Clan](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan"), you can use it to advantage by quietly eliminating Agmaer and Durak early on.
- You can bypass this quest completely and start [Awakening](/wiki/Skyrim:Awakening "Skyrim:Awakening") without this quest ever appearing in your quest journal. In order to do this, you must not have received information about the Dawnguard from a guard or Durak upon entering Dayspring Canyon. Then, be sure not to come within close range of Agmaer between entering Dayspring Canyon and approaching Fort Dawnguard, and don't talk to Durak. When you enter the fort, the quest-related events will still occur in the same manner, even without the quest being started. The Hall of the Vigilant will still be destroyed, though, and the conversation between Isran and Tolan will still take place.
- If you receive a crossbow from Durak, you can drop it, give it to a follower, or store it in a container before talking to Isran. He will then give you a second crossbow and 45 more steel bolts. You can also retrieve any steel bolts Durak fires.
- It is possible to join the Dawnguard even if you are already a vampire yourself.

## Bugs

- On some occasions, the quest marker both on your map and on your compass will not point in the right direction. This is due to the marker being associated with the wrong door for Dayspring Canyon.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.2.2, fixes this bug.
- Members of the Dawnguard may attack you if you have lycanthropy.
  - Reload a previous save, use beast form, and wait until it expires. Then proceed to Fort Dawnguard.
- If you have attacked, and/or possibly killed, any Vigilants of Stendarr prior to entering Dayspring Canyon, all Dawnguard members might be hostile, preventing you from ever joining, as the Dawnguard and Vigil of Stendarr are allied factions.
  - It may be possible to bypass this by avoiding any hostile interactions with Vigilants of Stendarr.
- The next quest, Awakening, may not trigger upon completion of this quest. **?**
  - Waiting 15 minutes of real time may fix this.
  - A commonly cited workaround is to skip the quest entirely. However, this causes quests later on to break.
- This quest may fail to work correctly (such as Agmaer not greeting you, Isran and Tolan not engaging in conversation upon entering Fort Dawnguard, or not initiating Awakening). This may also happen on all subsequent new games. **?**
  - A complete reinstall of Skyrim may fix it.
- Durak may approach and walk in circles, preventing dialogue. He may remain stuck in place indefinitely. **?**
  -  Use the console command `setstage DLC1VQ01MiscObjective 10`. After that, normal dialogue is possible. This option sometimes leaves the quest entry blank in your journal, however. An alternative option is to move Durak to you using the following: `prid xx015c16` then `moveto player`. He then seems to start the quest normally.
- If you have a bounty in Riften, the members of the Dawnguard may be hostile, upon meeting, preventing joining. To avoid this, take care of the bounty before entering Dayspring Canyon.
- Even after you finish the quest, [Vigilants of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilants_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilants of Stendarr") will still act as if the Hall of the Vigilant is still active and [Keeper Carcette](/wiki/Skyrim:Keeper_Carcette "Skyrim:Keeper Carcette") is alive, even though the Hall has been destroyed and Keeper Carcette is dead. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Introduction (DLC1VQ00) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Find out about the Dawnguard |
| Dawnguard (DLC1VQ01MiscObjective) | | |
| 10 |  | I've learned of a group of vampire hunters known as the Dawnguard. It seems they are looking for new recruits. *Objective 10:* Speak with the leader of the Dawnguard |
| 180 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table:
  - DLC1VQ00: 10, 15, 30, 100, 200
  - DLC1VQ01MiscObjective: 5, 20, 50, 80, 100, 110, 115, 120, 130, 140, 150, 190, 200, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1VQ00
  DLC1VQ01MiscObjective stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1VQ00
  DLC1VQ01MiscObjective`.

# Skyrim:Dawnguard (quest)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").
